{1 pratijñāsūtra PJS}

<3>

1.1

viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe |
śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||

1.2

abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn |
tatprasādāt kariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||

1.3

tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ |
santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hy anasūyavaḥ ||

1.4

na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ |
doṣo hy avidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||<4>

1.5

kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu |
neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||

1.6

nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate |
sāpavādā yataḥ ke cin mokṣasvargāv api prati ||

1.7

āgamapravaṇaś cāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣv apy apodyate |
na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣv apy apodyate ||

1.8

yathā kathañ cid ārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī |
vāgvṛttir alpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||<5>

1.9

mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhir viśeṣeṇoj jvalīkṛte |
vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||

1.10

prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā |
tāmāstikapathe kartum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||

1.11

athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtram ādyam idaṃ kṛtam |
dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||

1.12

sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit |
yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate ||

1.13

mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā |
na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||<6>

1.14

vidyāntareṣu nāpy etad yady abhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam |
anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvat tebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||

1.15

mīmāṃsāyāṃ tv ihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ |
nyāyamārge mahān doṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||

1.16

tasmāt prayojanaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam |
yat svenoktaṃ vadeyus tad bhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||

1.17

siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate |
śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||<7>

1.18

śāstraṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāv ubhau |
taduktyantargatas tasmād bhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||

1.19

siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanād yataḥ |
tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate ||

1.20

yāvat prayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate |
asambaddhapralāpitvād bhavet tāvad asaṃgatiḥ ||

1.21

iha tv ākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate |
dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmān nānyo 'bhidhīyate ||

1.22

na cāpy atrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate |
sambandhaṃ kriyayor hy eṣa brūte śāstrāc ca te pṛthak ||<8>

1.23

yo 'py ayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiś cid āditaḥ |
kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||

1.24

sadasadbhāvayos tasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate |
śrotuvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||

1.25

tasmād vyākhyāṅgam icchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ |
śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyas tu niṣphalaḥ ||<9>

1.26

loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate |
bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||

1.27

sarvavyākhyām upālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare |
parisaṃkhyās tutī kecithaśabdasya dūṣaṇam ||

1.28

sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā |
viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tv iyam ucyate ||

1.29

pravṛttis tu padeṣv eva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā |
vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||<10>

1.30

adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt |
tenaiṣām iti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye saty api grahaḥ ||

1.31

evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam |
prasiddhatvād avācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam ||<11>

1.32

vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate |
svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||

1.33

vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñ cil laukikārthavyatikramaḥ |
śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣam upālambho 'yam ucyate ||

1.34

athāta ity ayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate |
tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣādibhir bhavet ||

1.35

prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā |
na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||

1.36

sūtrārthe kliśyataś caivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ |
tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||

1.37

na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ |
yat tasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||<12>

1.38

prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣv anena kim |
phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||

1.39

codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt |
padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||

1.40

evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate |
padacchedadādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatis tv iyam ||<13>

1.41

brabīty eva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate |
nanv aśaktam idaṃ sūtraṃ samyak sūtritam ity api ||

1.42

sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate |
na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||

1.43

nānyato vedavidbhyaś ca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate |
pratyākhyānasya hetuś ca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||

1.44

yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvān nivārayet |
vākyārthe tatra sandehād vyākhyānaṃ cet pravartate ||

1.45

sūtreṣv api samānatvāt pratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate |
na vyākhyātavyam ityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||<14>

1.46

duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate |
asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvāt phalgutvāc cāpi parvayoḥ ||

1.47

madhyame cātidaurjanyāt parisaṃkhyaiva yujyate |
vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||

1.48

yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredam upadiśyate |
adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||

1.49

neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te |
yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||<15>

1.50

tadarthanirṇaye hetur jaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ |
vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāt tathā padatadarthayoḥ ||

1.51

adhyāhārādibhir muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate |
asambhavād avaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||

1.52

anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate |
prāthamyenāvaruddhatvād upāyavaśato 'tha vā ||

1.53

yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām |
tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ity ayam ||

1.54

vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptam anūdyate |
śeṣabhājāṃ bhavel lopa ity adhyāhārakalpanā ||<16>

1.55

viprakarṣāt paśoś ceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate |
padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamād iti ||

1.56

sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam |<17>
paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtram evānyathā kṛtam ||

1.57

agnayaś ca svakālatvād deyadharmāpayātanam |
vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpās tv amī kṛtāḥ ||

1.58

autpattikas tu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhor iti |
darśanāc ca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ity api ||<18>

1.59

sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate |
prasiddhair abhidhānād dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||

1.60

bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmād ekavākyatā |
vedādhyayanavākyād vā tenāthety asya dūṣaṇam ||

1.61

prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrair vedārthanirṇayaḥ |
na ca so 'sty athaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||

1.62

prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tac ca nāstīti dūṣaṇam |
prasiddho 'py athaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||<19>

1.63

pradarśanārtham ity eke, ke cin nānārthavācinaḥ |
samudāyād avacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||

1.64

śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat |
na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||

1.65

yad vākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvād asambhavāt |
yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||

1.66

sa nāsty atrāthaśabdasyety adhyāhārādikalpanam |
vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||

1.67

nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate |<20>
anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhir bādhyate dhruvam ||

1.68

tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kim api gamyate |
viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānād viśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||

1.69

sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitad ity abravīt paraḥ |
ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||

1.70

vedādhyayanam ākṣiptaṃ kim asūtritacodanā |
yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||

1.71

tadānantaryam uktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārtham avakalpate |
kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamād yasya kasya cit ||

1.72

kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam |<21>
saṅkalpādibhir apy eṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||

1.73

sādhāraṇyāt tu te 'py atra nopadeśyāḥ kathañ cana |
tasmād dharmabubhutsāyām asādhāraṇakāraṇam ||

1.74

nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tac ca nākhyayanād ṛte |
anyasyāpīty anenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||

1.75

prāg apīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpy anyasya sambhavāt |
pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tv ity anena kim ||

1.76

vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā |
na tāvat sādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||

1.77

iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ |
dharmamātrābhidhānād dhi buddhādivacanāny api ||

1.78

paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsety anyasyāpīti codanā |<22>
yad vā bhavatu nāmedṛk sūtraṃ vedam adhītya tu ||

1.79

jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryety atrāpi dvayam īpsitam |
nānadhītya na cāpy anyat kṛtvety etan na labhyate ||

1.80

vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyor vākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ |
adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāder apy anantarā ||

1.81

bhaved dharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhis tadā |
ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||

1.82

ity evam anuvādatvāt prāg apy eṣā prasajyate |
buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tv ity apākriyā ||<23>

1.83

prāg apīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyād vedalābhataḥ |
naivaitayor vacobhaṅgyor eko 'py artho vidhīyate ||

1.84

api cetyādikenoktam, kin tv ityetad vidhīyate |
ānantaryaṃ parastāc ca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||

1.85

ke cid adhyāharanti, <24>
asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ |
na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate ||

1.86

sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā |
ānantaryavacovyaktir āśritaivātra lakṣyate ||

1.87

śrutārthaṃ tv aparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate |
pratītā dharmajiñāsā vedādhyāyād anantarā ||

1.88

tatkālasyāvaruddhatvāt snānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet |<25>
virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||

1.89

snānasya tena bādhaḥ syād dharmajijñāsayā balāt |<26>
dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tv iti ||

1.90

punaruktyā gatārthatvāt tyaktaṃ kaiś cit, tad ucyate |
yady apy asya bhaved vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam ||

1.91

tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayed avirodhataḥ |
granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||

1.92

adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tv avirodhitā |
yas tv evamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||

1.93

adṛṣṭāyātha vāpy anyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram |
ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||

1.94

avidhitvam anāśritya so 'vasānam apekṣate |
tato 'pekṣāvaśāt snānam asnānādinivartanam ||

1.95

virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet |<27>
tasmād adhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||

1.96

dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānām evaṃ vyākhyeyam āśritā |
snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||

1.97

tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram |
yathaivādhyayanāt snānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||

1.98

tathā tataḥ paro 'py anyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ paras tataḥ |
tataś cāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||

1.99

yogyatvād āgate kāle prāthamyāt snānabādhanam |
so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthād bādha ity avagamyate ||<28>

1.100

guṇapradhānayor vāpi virodhād guṇabādhanam |
snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttir guruveśmanaḥ ||

1.101

virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam |
tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||

1.102

jijñāsetāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate |
gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvac ca na samāpyate ||

1.103

tāvat sakalavācitvān na snānaṃ paryavasyati |
gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||

1.104

tatparatvavidhānāc ca na tāvad dārasaṅgrahaḥ |
vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyād iti punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||<29>

1.105

smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛter yady apy anantaram |
viparītārtham ity asmāt tadvākyād apanīyate ||

1.106

athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastād upavarṇitaḥ |
tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvāt pradarśitaḥ ||

1.107

smṛtiprāptam idānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam |
pratiṣedhann adṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||

1.108

nivṛttya gurugehāc ca jijñāsārthaḥ punar bhavet |
praveśaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||

1.109

nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ |
smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syād akṛtārthasya nirgame ||

1.110

athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā |
ānantaryopadeśitvād ataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||<30>

1.111

yogyatvam athaśabdena yady api pratipāditam |
tad eva hetur atreti nātaḥśabdād vinā bhavet ||

1.112

lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā tad dhi prasajyate |
jijñāsāyāś ca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||

1.113

ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanam āśritam |
hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādy apy asau vadet ||<31>

1.114

snānabādhasya vā hetur ata ity ucyate punaḥ |
yogyasyādhītavedatvān nāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate ||

1.115

sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā |
jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||

1.116

iṣes tu karma bāhyaḥ syād dharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam |
samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||

1.117

evaṃ viṣayanānātvān na kā cit punaruktatā |
sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||

1.118

prakṛtyā vikṛtir yasmāc caturthyantā samasyate |
tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminn asamāsatā ||<32>

1.119

sa hi tasyety anenokto dharmasyety eṣa vigrahaḥ |
dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||

1.120

prāpnoty atra caturthy eva viśeṣaś ced vivakṣitaḥ |
sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||

1.121

sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu |
viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||

1.122

sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā |
anyasādhanam anyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||

1.123

kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca krator iti |<33>
śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaś ca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||

1.124

prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāt tu neṣyate |
aprasiddhas tv aśakyatvānnatarām ity ato 'bravīt ||

1.125

jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayād dharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca |
asandigdho hy ajijñāsyo yo vā syān niṣprayojanaḥ ||

1.126

svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate |
pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, <34>
pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||

1.127

sthite vedapramāṇatve punar vākyārthanirṇaye |
matir bahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayān nopajāyate ||

1.128

ke cid āhur asāv arthaḥ, ke cin nāsāv ayaṃ tv iti |
tannirṇayārtham apy etat paraṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

{2 codanāsūtra CDS}

2.1

dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate |
svarūpādes tataḥ siddhaḥ, <35>
svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||

2.2

dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate |
svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||

2.3

kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau |
tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||

2.4

codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam |
sākāṅkṣam iti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||<36>

2.5

sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣv api |
indriyāder asāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||

2.6

atyantāsaty api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi |
tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvāt pramāṇatā ||

2.7

codanety abravīc cātra śabdamātravivakṣayā |
na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaś cid asti vidhāyakaḥ ||

2.8

indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvan na sādhyate |
tāvac ca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||

2.9

nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam |<37>
pramāṇaṃ tv api śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate |

2.10

padārthas tanmatir vā syād vākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā |
pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||

2.11

jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate |
codanoktis tadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||

2.12

nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ |
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāc codanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||

2.13

dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate |
teṣām aindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||

2.14

śreyaḥsādhanatā hy eṣāṃ nityaṃ vedāt pratīyate |
tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmān nendriyagocaraḥ ||

2.15

pradarśanārtham atroktam indriyaṃ sūtrakāravat |<38>
nānyat kiñ ceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||

2.16

tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punar indriyakīrtanam |
kiñ ceti madhyam acchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||

2.17

yady api tv anumānasyāpy evamādau samarthatā |
vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit |

2.18

na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam |
liṅgasya kasya cit siddhaṃ yena syād anumānatā ||

2.19

nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate |
padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||

2.20

vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, <39>
padārthānāṃ ca hetutā |
sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||

2.21

nityatvāder asiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā |
sutarām apramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||

2.22

pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayet sadā |
smṛtivac ca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||

2.23

nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā |
buddhiḥ sākṣād adṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||<40>

2.24

nātmīyād anyadīyād vā pratyakṣāder vinā kva cit |
vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāc codanāsv api ||

2.25

tena saty api vijñāne pratijñāder yathaiva hi |
svātantryān na pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||

2.26

svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā |
pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||

2.27

yad vāptenāpraṇītatvād bālonmattādivākyavat |
vyomādivac ca nityatvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||

2.28

yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ |
svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syur vākyatvāt puruṣoktivat ||

2.29

prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām |
śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvād apramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi |<41>

2.30

na syād vaktṛguṇānāṃ ced vacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā |
taddoṣair apramāṇatvaṃ kim ity asya bhaviṣyati ||

2.31

evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare |
prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanv ity etadacūcudat |

2.32

tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate |
tato 'pi pratyayotpattes tasmāj jātyuttaraṃ tv idam ||

2.33

sarvavijñānaviṣayam idaṃ tāvat parīkṣyatām |
pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||

2.34

svato 'satām asādhyatvāt ke cid āhur dvayaṃ svataḥ |
apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||<42>

2.35

svatas tāvad dvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca |
niḥsvabhāvatvam evaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate |

2.36

kathaṃ hy anyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ |
kimātmakaṃ bhavet tac ca svabhāvadvayavarjitam |

2.37

vijñānavyaktibhedena bhavec ced aviruddhatā |
tathāpy anyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||<43>

2.38

tasmāt svābhāvikaṃ teṣām apramāṇatvam iṣyatām |
prāmāṇyañ ca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||

2.39

aprāmānyam avastutvān na syāt kāraṇadoṣataḥ |
vastutvāt tu guṇais teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam upajanyate ||

2.40

prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāt tadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ |
tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||

2.41

matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvāt prāmānyaṃ nopajāyate |
hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyaty avastunaḥ ||

2.42

indriyādiguṇāś cāsya kāraṇam, tadasad dvidhā |<44>
duṣṭatvād indriyādīnām abhāve 'nyatamasya vā |

2.43

ata eva ca vo bhrāntir doṣair mithyātvadhīr iti |
tadvyāptes tu guṇābhāvas tatkṛtā hy apramāṇatā ||

2.44

tasmāt kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam |
svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate |

2.45

anvayavyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ |
nājñāne dṛśyate hy etatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||

2.46

tataś ca puruṣābhāvāt sati vā śuddhyasambhavāt |
nirmūlatvāt pramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||<45>

2.47

svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām |
na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ||

2.48

ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet |
labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu |

2.49

jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvan nārtho 'vadhāryate |<46>
yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarād bhavet ||

2.50

tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt |
yāvad dhi na paricchinnā śuddhis tāvad asatsamā ||

2.51

tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syāt pramāṇatā |
tasyāpy evam itīcchaś ca na kva cid vyavatiṣṭhate ||

2.52

yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyan naiva gṛhyate |
nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānād ayatnataḥ ||

2.53

tasmād bodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā |
arthānyathātvahetūtthadoṣajñānād apodyate ||

2.54

aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ |
vastutvād dvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||<47>

2.55

avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate |
kāraṇābhāvatas tv eva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||

2.56

doṣataś cāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām |
guṇajñānānavasthāvan na doṣeṣu prasajyate ||

2.57

sākṣād viparyayajñānāl laghvyeva tv apramāṇatā |
pūrvābādhena notpattir uttarasya hi sidhyati ||

2.58

duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare |
arthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||<48>

2.59

tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīr vā parā na cet |
tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvād ādyamānatā ||

2.60

svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānāt pramāṇatā |
doṣajñāne tv anutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇatā ||<49>

2.61

evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ |
prārthyate tāvataivaikaṃ svataḥ prāmāṇyam aśnute ||

2.62

śabde doṣodbhavas tāvad vaktradhīna iti sthitiḥ |
tadabhāvaḥ kva cit tāvad guṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ |

2.63

tadguṇair apakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt |
yadā vaktur abhāvena na syur doṣā nirāśrayāḥ |

2.64

pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇās tathā |
prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syād ity udāhṛtam ||

2.65

tasmād guṇebhyo doṣāṇām abhāvas tadabhāvataḥ |
aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||<50>

2.66

pratyayotpattihetutvāt prāmāṇyaṃ nāpanīyate |
doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaś cen nanu saivāsthitir bhavet ||

2.67

tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ |
doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||

2.68

tatrāpavādanirmuktir vaktrabhāvāl laghīyasī |
vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkām api gacchati ||

2.69

ato vaktranadhīnatvāt prāmāṇye tadupāsanam |
na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||

2.70

tataś cāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate |
prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||

2.71

pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā |
tadabhāve hi tad duṣyeditaran na kadā cana |<51>

2.72

tenetaraiḥ pramāṇair yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ |
tayaiva syāt pramāṇatvam anuvādatvam anyathā ||

2.73

anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatir naiva kāraṇam |
tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvād ekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||

2.74

yatrāpi syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇair uttaraiḥ punaḥ |
nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtas tathā ||

2.75

saṅgatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā |
pramāṇāntaram icchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi |<52>

2.76

kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā |
prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||

2.77

śrotradhīś cāpramāṇaṃ syād itarābhir asaṅgateḥ |
syāc cet tajjanitenaiva jñānenānyena saṅgatiḥ ||

2.78

vede 'pi śatakṛtvaḥ syād buddhir uccāraṇānugā |
sādhanāntarajanyā tu buddhir nāsti dvayor api ||

2.79

yathā tv ekendriyādhīnajñānāntaranibandhanā |
saṅgatiḥ kāraṇaṃ prāptā tathā vede 'pi kalpyatām ||

2.80

tasmād dṛḍhaṃ yadutpannaṃ nāpi saṃvādamṛcchati |
jñānāntareṇa vijñānaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ pratīyatām ||

2.81

na cānumānataḥ sādhyā śabdādīnāṃ pramāṇatā |
sarvasyaiva hi mā prāpat pramāṇāntarasādhyatā ||<53>

2.82

nanu pramāṇam ityevaṃ pratyakṣādi na gṛhyate |
na cetthamagṛhītena vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||

2.83

prāmāṇyaṃ grahaṇāt pūrvaṃ svarūpeṇaiva saṃsthitam |
nirapekṣaṃ svakāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyayāntaraiḥ ||

2.84

tenāsya jñāyamānatvaṃ prāmāṇye nopayujyate |
viṣayānubhāvo hy atra pūrvasmād eva labhyate |

2.85

apramāṇaṃ punaḥ svārthagrāhakaṃ syāt svarūpataḥ |
nivṛttis tasya mithyātve nāgṛhīte parair bhavet ||

2.86

na hy arthasyātathābhāvaḥ pūrveṇārthas tathātvavat |<54>
tatrāpy arthānyathābhāve dhīr yad vā duṣṭakāraṇe ||

2.87

tāvataiva ca mithyātvaṃ gṛhyate nānyahetukam |
utpattyavasthaṃ caivedaṃ pramāṇam iti mīyate ||

2.88

ato yatrāpi mithyātvaṃ parebhyaḥ pratipādyate |
tatrāpy etad dvayaṃ vācyaṃ na tu sādharmyamātrakam ||

2.89

codanārthānyathābhāvaṃ kurvataś cānumānataḥ |
tajjñānenaiva yo bādhaḥ sa kathaṃ vinivāryate ||

2.90

tanmithyātvād abādhaś cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
nānumānād ato 'nyad dhi bādhakaṃ kiñ cid asti te ||

2.91

na cānyair agrahe 'rthasya syād abhāvo rasādivat |
teṣāṃ jihvādibhir yasmān niyamo grahaṇe 'sti hi ||<55>

2.92

taddhiyaivārthabodhaś cet, tādṛgdharme bhaviṣyati |
mamāsiddham idaṃ kin tu vedāj jāte 'vabodhane |

2.93

vaktuṃ na dveṣamātreṇa yujyate satyavādinā |
dveṣād asammatatvād vā na ca syād apramāṇatā ||

2.94

na cātmecchābhyanujñābhyāṃ prāmāṇyam avakalpate |
agnidāhādiduḥkhasya na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||

2.95

na cābhilāpikaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyenāvadhāryate |
tasmād ālokavad vede sarvasādhāraṇe sati ||

2.96

naivaṃ vipratipattavyam, bauddhāder vakṣyate 'ntaram |<56>
puruṣāśaktitas tatra sāpavādatvasambhavaḥ ||

2.97

vedasyāpauruṣeyatve siddhā tv evaṃ pramāṇatā |
kartṛmattve tu vedasya samyaṅmithyātvavādibhiḥ ||

2.98

kartā guṇāś ca doṣāś ca mahājanaparigrahaḥ |
evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam, mīmāṃsakaiḥ punaḥ ||

2.99

idānīm iva sarvatra dṛṣṭān nādhikam iṣyate |
evambhūtasya vedasya jñānotpattiṃ prakurvataḥ ||

2.100

svarūpaviparītatvasaṃśayau bhāṣyavāritau |
nivārayiṣyate cāpi duṣṭakāraṇakalpanā ||

2.101

puruṣābhāvatas tena taddvāreṇāpy aśaṅkitau |<57>
tathā satyatathābhāvo buddhyanutpattim āśritaḥ ||

2.102

tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ bravītītyevamādinā |
yathādṛṣṭārthavāditvaṃ tac cet pratyayitāditi ||

2.103

indriyeti tu mūlaṃ ced asyāstītyevam abravīt |
draṣṭṛtvasatyavāditve tac cet pratyayitāditi ||

2.104

dṛśyamānārthavāditve syād anāptoktisatyatā |
evaṃ tv ekāṅgavaikalyāt pratyudāharaṇasthitiḥ ||

2.105

ekaikābhāvamātre syād āptatvaindriyakatvayoḥ |<58>
apratyayitapakṣe syād aindriyasyāpy asatyatā ||

2.106

anindriyatvapakṣe vā satpratyayitabhāṣitam |
vyāhatagranthataivaṃ syāt, tasmāt pūrveṇa satyatā ||

2.107

pareṇa mūlasadbhāva indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ |
aprāmāṇyanivṛttyarthaṃ doṣābhāvopavarṇanam ||

2.108

guṇāt prāmāṇyam ityevaṃ tatpūrvaṃ sunirākṛtam |
pūrvatra pratiṣiddhatvān naitat prāmāṇyakāraṇam ||<59>

2.109

samuccayārtho vāśabdaḥ pūrvasmin, uttaratra ca |
vikalpenobhayor āha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak ||

2.110

śakye 'py asatye mithyātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satye 'py aśaktike |
nānena vacaneneha sarvajñatvanirākriyā ||

2.111

vacanād ṛta ityevam apavādo hi saṃśritaḥ |
yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syāt sarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ||

2.112

ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajño yena kalpyate |
nūnaṃ sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasādīn pratipadyate ||<60>

2.113

yajjātīyaiḥ pramāṇais tu yajjātīyārthadarśanam |
bhaved idānīṃ lokasya tathā kālāntare 'py abhūt |

2.114

yatrāpy atiśayo dṛṣṭaḥ sa svārthānatilaṅghanāt |
dūrasūkṣmādidṛṣṭau syān na rūpe śrotravṛttitā ||

2.115

bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭaṃ ca pratyakṣasya manāgapi |
sāmarthyam, nānumānāder liṅgādirahite kva cit ||

2.116

sarvajñakalpanānyais tu vede cāpauruṣeyatā |
tulyatā kalpitā yena tenedaṃ sampradhāryatām ||<61>

2.117

sarvajño dṛśyate tāvan nedānīm asmadādibhiḥ |
nirākaraṇavacchakyā na cāsīd iti kalpanā ||

2.118

na cāgamena sarvajñaḥ, tadīye 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt |
narāntarapraṇītasya prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||

2.119

na cāpy evamparo nityaḥ śakyo labdhum ihāgamaḥ |
nityaś ced arthavādatvaṃ tatpare syād anityatā ||

2.120

āgamasya ca nityatve siddhe tatkalpanā vṛthā |<62>
yatas taṃ pratipadyante dharmam eva tato narāḥ ||

2.121

yo 'pīndriyārthasambandhaviṣaye satyavāditām |
dṛṣṭvā tadvacanatvena śraddheye 'rthe 'pi kalpayet ||

2.122

tenāpi pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syāt pramāṇatā |
prāmāṇyaṃ cet svayaṃ tasya kāpekṣānyendriyādiṣu ||

2.123

yathaivātrendriyādibhyaḥ paricchedāt pramāṇatā |
śraddheye 'pi tathaiva syān na svātantryeṇa labhyate |

2.124

yathā ca teṣāṃ satyatvaṃ sidhyaty etena hetunā |
tathānyānavabuddhārthaprāmāṇyābhāvasādhanam |<63>

2.125

aśraddheyārthasatyatvaṃ śraddheye cāpy asatyatā |
pūrvajñānānuvāditvaṃ dṛṣṭāntavad iheṣyatām ||

2.126

api cālaukikārthatve sati puṃvākyahetukam |
mithyātvaṃ bauddhavākyānāṃ syād anyonyaṃ sapakṣataḥ ||

2.127

dharmādharmātiriktārthe prāmāṇyaṃ ca prasajyate |
sāṃkhyādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭānto durlabho 'sya ca |

2.128

alaukikārthavācitvaṃ nṛvākyatve satīti ca |
parasparam apekṣyaiva bauddhādeḥ syān mṛṣārthatā ||

2.129

vaded evaṃ ca yo nāma vādī prathamasaṅgataḥ |
tasyāpi hetuḥ syād eṣa bhavantaṃ pratyasaṃśayam ||

2.130

buddhādīnām asarvajñam iti satyaṃ vaco mama |
maduktatvād yathaivāgnir uṣṇo bhāsvara ity api ||

2.131

pratyakṣaṃ ca maduktatvaṃ tvayā sādhyā taduktatā |
tena hetur madīyaḥ syāt sandigdhāsiddhatā tava ||

2.132

pratyakṣādyavisaṃvādi prameyatvādi yasya ca |
sadbhāvavāraṇe śaktaṃ ko nu taṃ kalpayiṣyati ||<64>

2.133

na cāpi smṛtyavicchedāt sarvajñaḥ parikalpyate |
vigānāt, chinnamūlatvāt, kaiś cid eva parigrahāt ||

2.134

sarvajño 'sāv iti hy eva tatkāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ |
tajjñānajñeyavijñānarahitair gamyate katham ||

2.135

kalpanīyāś ca sarvajñā bhaveyur bahavas tava |
ya eva syād asarvajñaḥ sa sarvajñaṃ na budhyate ||

2.136

sarvajño 'navabuddhaś ca yenaiva syān na taṃ prati |
tadvākyānāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ mūlājñāne 'nyavākyavat ||

2.137

rāgādirahite cāsmin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite |
deśanānyapraṇītaiva syād ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt ||<65>

2.138

sānnidhyamātratas tasya puṃsaścintāmaṇer iva |
niḥsaranti yathākāmaṃ kuḍyādibhyo 'pi deśanāḥ ||

2.139

evamādyucyamānaṃ tu śraddadhānasya śobhate |
kuḍyādiniḥsṛtatvāc ca nāśvāso deśanāsu naḥ ||

2.140

kin nu buddhapraṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiś cid durātmabhiḥ |
adṛśyair vipralambhārthaṃ piśācādibhir īritāḥ ||

2.141

evaṃ yaiḥ kevalaṃ jñānam indriyādyanapekṣiṇaḥ |
sūkṣmātītādiviṣayaṃ jīvasya parikalpitam ||

2.142

narte tadāgamāt sidhyen na ca tenāgamo vinā |
dṛṣṭānto 'pi na tasyānyo nṛṣu kaś cit pravartate ||<66>

2.143

nityāgamāvabodho 'pi pratyākhyeyo 'nayā diśā |
na hi tatrāpi visrambho dṛṣṭo 'nena kṛto 'tha vā ||

2.144

sarvadā cāpi puruṣāḥ prāyeṇānṛtavādinaḥ |
yathādyatve na visrambhas tathātītārthakīrtane ||

2.145

svapnādijñānavac cāpi pratyayo 'syāgamārthayoḥ |
bhaved iti saśaṅkānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||

2.146

puruṣātiśayaś ceṣṭaḥ saiva cāgamanityatā |
kalpitaṃ smaraṇaṃ cāsya janmāntaranibandhanam ||

2.147

grāhyatve cāgamasyaivaṃ dveṣo 'rthagrahaṇe vṛthā |
yo hy anuccāritaṃ śabdaṃ gahṇātyarthe 'sya kā kathā |<67>

2.148

pumāṃs tāvat svatantraḥ syād arthagrahaṇavādinām |
āgamapratibhāne tu pāratantryaṃ dvayor api ||

2.149

anekapuruṣasthatvād ekatraiva ca janmani |
grahaṇasmaraṇād vede na svātantryaṃ vihanyate ||

2.150

anyathākaraṇe cāsya bahubhyaḥ syān nivāraṇam |
ekasya pratibhānaṃ tu kṛtakān na viśiṣyate ||

2.151

ataś ca sampradāye ca naikaḥ puruṣa iṣyate |
bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hy adyatvavannarāḥ ||

2.152

evaṃ ca kalpayantyanye yāvadāgamasiddhaye |
tāvan na kalpayaty etat samatvaṃ jaimineḥ paraiḥ ||<68>

2.153

na hi dṛṣṭādhikaṃ kiñ cit prāmāṇye tena kalpyate |
aprāmāṇyanimitteṣu parasyādṛṣṭakalpanā ||

2.154

dṛṣṭaprāmāṇyabādhaś ca nāstikasya prasajyate |
utpanne sati vijñāne balād bādhaprakalpanā ||

2.155

sādhite puruṣābhāve nirdoṣajñānajanmanaḥ |
pratyakṣān nāstikair vācyo viśeṣaś codanādhiyaḥ ||

2.156

upadeśo 'nyathā na syād atīndriyanidandhanaḥ |
tasya kartrā na ced dṛṣṭaḥ so 'rtha ity arthakalpanā ||

2.157

yad vānumānam evedam upadeśitvam ucyate |
dṛṣṭārthapūrvatāvyāptam, vyatireko 'sya nanv iti ||<69>

2.158

anyathāpy upapannatvaṃ vyāmohād iti kathyate |
liṅgasya vyabhicāro vā bālavākyanidarśanāt |

2.159

vedāj jñātvopadiṣṭaṃ ced ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam |
vedād apītyanenoktam, manvādeś caitad iṣyate ||

2.160

anyathā saṃvidāno 'pi vivakṣaty anyathā yataḥ |
tasmād ekāntato nāsti puṃvākyāt taddhiyāṃ gatiḥ ||<70>

2.161

bhrāntasyānyavivakṣāyām anyad vākyaṃ ca dṛśyate |
yathāvivakṣam apy etat tasmān naiva pravartate ||

2.162

vaktṛdhīr āptavākyeṣu gamyate, anyatra viplutiḥ |
tenotsargāpavādābhyāṃ vacasaḥ śaktir ucyate ||

2.163

padārtharacanāyatto vākyārthapratyayodbhavaḥ |
vivakṣāpūrvavijñānavaśāc ca racanākṛtiḥ ||

2.164

vivakṣāntarayuktā hi kurvāṇā racanāntaram |
āvāpodvāpabhedena dṛśyante 'rtheṣu mānavāḥ |

2.165

tenārthapratyayotpāde śroturjāte 'pi vākyataḥ |
jñāto nūnam aneneti vakturjñāne matir bhavet ||

2.166

āptoktikāraṇaṃ kañ cid anuyuṅkte naraṃ yadā |
tadā ca nirdiśatyāptaṃ sa jānātyetad ityasau ||<71>

2.167

tajjñānāntaritatvāc ca śabdās tāvad udāsate |
prāmāṇyasthāpanaṃ tu syād vaktṛdhīhetusambhavāt ||

2.168

arthe pūrvapratīte 'pi niścayo hi tadāśrayaḥ |
tenārthajñānagamyāpi prāmāṇye saiva pūrvabhāk |

2.169

ato 'tra puṃnimittatvād upapannā mṛṣārthatā |
na tu syāt tatsvabhāvatvaṃ vede vakturabhāvataḥ |

2.170

tadbuddhyantarayor nāstīty artho 'rthaiś ca pratīyate |<72>
ato na jñānapūrvatvam apekṣyaṃ nāyathārthatā ||

2.171

apramāṇatvasiddhau vā dṛṣṭānto ya udāhṛtaḥ |
buddhādivacanaṃ tasya sādhyenāsaṅgatocyate ||

2.172

teṣām api hi yat kāryaṃ pūrvatra pratipāditam |
tatra samyaktvam arthe tu vyāpāro naiva vidyate ||

2.173

svavyāpārātirikte 'rthe vedasyāpi mṛṣārthatā |
pūrvapakṣārthavattvena prasaktā siddhasādhyatā ||

2.174

ajñātvaivamabhiprāyaṃ kṛtakākṛtakatvayoḥ |
satyamithyātvahetūktimātrajñānāt paro 'bravīt ||

2.175

nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam, <73>
nānyatvād ityadūṣaṇam |
anyatvād eva dṛṣṭānto na hi pakṣe sapakṣatā ||

2.176

tasmād ayam abhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya varṇyate |
abhyupetyārthaviṣayaṃ vākyavyāpāram ucyate |

2.177

yadi syād vyavadhāne 'pi vākyārthāpekṣayānṛtam |
dṛṣṭānto nṛvaco 'trāpi hetuḥ sādhāraṇo bhavet ||

2.178

satyeṣv api hi dṛṣṭaiva paurṣeyeṣu vākyatā |
atīndriye 'pi kiñ cid dhi satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛcchayā ||<74>

2.179

nānyatvād iti cānena paroktād anyatocyate |
anyo hy eṣa tadābhāsaḥ, vipakṣaṃ vānyam abravīt |

2.180

yad vānyasmād visaṃvādān mithyātvaṃ tatra na tv iha |
viṣayasyāpi cānyatvāt sādhanāsaṅgataiva sā ||

2.181

na hy anyasyeti naikasmin mṛṣārthe 'nyamṛṣārthatā |
vivakṣāyā mṛṣārthatve na ca vākye mṛṣārthatā ||

2.182

śyāmatve puṃstvavac caitat sādhāraṇye nidarśanam |<75>
parokter vāpi duṣṭatvād vikalpasamam ucyate ||

2.183

yad vā pramāṇam evedaṃ samyaktve 'nyatvam ucyate |
dhiruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ |

2.184

codanājanitā buddhiḥ pramāṇaṃ doṣavarjitaiḥ |
kāraṇair janyamānatvāl liṅgāptoktyakṣabuddhivat |

2.185

tathānāptāpraṇītoktijanyatvād bādhavarjanāt |
deśakālādibhedādau cāptoktipratyayo yathā ||

2.186

akartṛkatvasiddhyā ca hetutvaṃ sādhayiṣyate |<76>
evamādyavabudhyāyaṃ nānyatvād ity avocata |

2.187

pratyakṣas tv iti dārḍhyaṃ vā prāthamyaṃ vāpi lakṣayet |
svarūpataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ mithyātvaṃ pararūpataḥ ||

2.188

jñānābhāvaś ca mithyātvaṃ dvayasyāsambhavād yadi |
pratyakṣaṃ tatpareṣāṃ ca siddham asyānumānataḥ ||

2.189

yathā ca tava mithyātvaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhayed idam |
tathā ca bādhakādhīnaṃ mithyātvam api sādhayet ||

2.190

dharma ity upasaṃhārye yacchreyaskarabhāṣaṇam |
taddharmapadavācyārthanirūpaṇavivakṣayā ||<77>

2.191

śreyo hi puruṣaprītiḥ sā dravyaguṇakarmabhiḥ |
codanālakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatā ||

2.192

anyat sādhyam adṛṣṭvaiva yāgādīnanuniṣṭhataḥ |
dhārmikatvasamākhyānaṃ tadyogād iti gamyate ||

2.193

paśvādīni ca dharmasya phalānīti vyavasthitam |
citrāgodohanādīnāṃ tāny uktāni phalāni ca ||

2.194

tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatvam, dhrmāṇīti ca darśanāt |
liṅgasaṃkhyāvinirmukto dharmaśabdo nidarśanam |<78>

2.195

antaḥkaraṇavṛttau vā vāsanāyāṃ ca cetasaḥ |
pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe 'pūrvajanmani ||

2.196

prayogo dharmaśabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca sādhanam |
puruṣārthasya te jñātuṃ śakyante codanādibhiḥ ||

2.197

na ca vastvantaraṃ śakyam apūrvaṃ svargayāgayoḥ |
jñātuṃ sādhanabhūtaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā nāpy ato 'nyathā |

2.198

śrutasādhanasādhyatvatyāgenāśrutakalpanā |
prasajyetāsya tādrūpye vyatireke tv arūpatā ||<79>

2.199

tasmāt phale pravṛttasya yāgādeḥ śaktimātrakam |
utpattau vāpi paśvāder apūrvaṃ na tataḥ pṛthak ||

2.200

śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaśabdair viśeṣataḥ |
nopākhyāyanta ityevaṃ nāpūrvaṃ dharmaśabdatā |

2.201

purastāc codanāśabdo vidhāv eva vyavasthitaḥ |
na ca tallakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇaṃ katham ||<80>

2.202

codanālakṣaṇo yaś ca śyenādir hi gamyate |
niṣedhābhāvatas tasya kathaṃ brūyād anarthatā ||

2.203

yady api syād vidhispṛṣṭe niṣedho naiva tādṛśaḥ |
vijñāyate hy anarthatvaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahaṇādivat ||

2.204

codanālakṣaṇaṃ coktvā niṣiddhatvād virudhyate |
śyenādāv upadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hīti na yujyate ||

2.205

hiṃsā hi phalam eteṣāṃ bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ |
sā hi prāṇaviyogātmā śyenas tatrāsivatpṛthak ||

2.206

upadeśābhidhānaṃ ca nāvidheye 'vakalpate |<81>
śyenāder avidhāne ca kasyānyasya vidheyatā ||

2.207

sarvatrāvasthito nyāyo bhāvanāṃśadvaye vidhiḥ |
sa bādhyeta, iha ye cāmī jyotiṣṭomādayo matāḥ ||

2.208

dharmatvena na te 'pi syur hiṃsāsādhanakā hi te |
na cāvidhīyamānasya phalatatsādhanāṅgatā ||

2.209

sādhanatvena vihitaṃ na cāvihitam ucyate |
sādhyatvena vidhānaṃ tu naiveṣṭaṃ lokavedayoḥ ||

2.210

tenaivamarthaśabdasya prayojanam ihocyate |<82>
pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabdaśravaṇena dhīḥ |

2.211

sā codaneti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdaye sthitam |
pravartakagṛhītis tu syād udāharaṇārthatā ||

2.212

tātparye hy arthaśabdasya neyaṃ vyākhyopapadyate |
arthagrahaṇalabhyaṃ vā tatpravartakabhāṣaṇam |

2.213

dharme pramāṇabhūtāyās tad vā lakṣaṇam uktavān |
evaṃ sati vidhibhyaḥ syād vidheyārthāvadhāraṇam ||

2.214

niṣedhebhyo niṣedhyānām anarthatvena nirṇayaḥ |
tenārthagrahaṇenoktā vidheyasyeha dharmatā ||

2.215

niṣedhyānām anarthatvam arthasiddhaṃ na sūtritam |
tasmād ubhayam ityatra vidheyapratiṣedhyayoḥ ||

2.216

yāgādibrahmahatyādivargayoḥ syān nidarśanam |<83>
śyenādīnāṃ vidheyatvādiṣṭasyāpi ca sādhanāt ||

2.217

upacārād anarthatvaṃ phaladvāreṇa varṇyate |
pratiṣiddhā hi setyatra sphuṭam etat kariṣyate ||

2.218

hiṃsā hīti ca yac cāpi brūte nābhicared iti |
śyenādīnāṃ svarūpe tu nottaragranthasaṅgatiḥ ||

2.219

vihitatvān niṣedhasya pravṛttis teṣu durlabhā |
yadā tu codanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ |

2.220

tadobhayādiko granthaḥ sadhyasādhanasaṃśritaḥ |
sādhyasādhanasambandhe vidhinā pratipādite ||

2.221

lakṣyamāṇatvam ubhayoḥ, dvividhaṃ ca phalaṃ kratoḥ |
svargādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedhānatikramāt ||

2.222

atikrameṇa hiṃsādi, <84>
śāstrāntaranirīkṣayā |
phalāṃśe bhāvanāyāś ca pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ ||

2.223

vakṣyate, jaiminiś cāha tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇā |
tena sāmānyataḥ prāpto vidhinā na nivāritaḥ ||

2.224

phalāṃśopanipātinyā hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ |
anarthaprāptihetutvaṃ bodhyate tatra yady api ||

2.225

śyenasvarūpaṃ nānarthas tatphalasya tv anarthatā |
parastūbhayam ityādeḥ phalasyāpi vidheyatām ||

2.226

bhāvanāntargatatvād vā matvānarthatvam ākṣipat |<85>
naivetyetāvatā cāsya vidheyatvanirākriyā ||

2.227

kiṃ vidheyam idānīṃ syād āha śyenādayas tv iti |
praśnāpākaraṇe cātra tavyo vidhivivakṣayā ||

2.228

prayukto na tu sādhye 'rthe, dvaye 'py anupayogataḥ |
anarthasyāpi sādhyatvam avidheyasya hīṣyate ||

2.229

sādhyatvarahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityam arthatā |
śatuś ca lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ teṣāṃ cāpy upadeśanam ||

2.230

bruvan sphuṭīkarotīṣṭam upadeśo hi nānyathā |<86>
vidhitvamādiśabdāt syād itikartavyatāsv api |

2.231

tasmāt phalāṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate |
aṃśadvaye tu yā nāma tanniṣedhābhidhāyinām ||

2.232

aviśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovad iti cottaram |
niṣedhenānavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hy anarthatā |

2.233

pratyakṣāder aśakyatvāt kalpyate niṣpramāṇikā |
na hi hiṃsādyanuṣṭhāne tadānīṃ doṣadarśanam ||

2.234

bāhye 'pi vicikitsā tu śāstrādevopajāyate |
hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhitvaṃ dṛśyate yan na tāvatā ||

2.235

karturduḥkhānumānaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ tadviparyayaḥ |
viṣaye 'syāḥ phalaṃ yādṛk pretya krtus tathāvidham ||

2.236

hiṃsā kriyāviśeṣatvāt sūte śāstroktadānavat |<87>
ya evamāha, tasyāpi gurustrīgamanādibhiḥ ||

2.237

surāpānādibhiś cāpi vipakṣair vyabhicāritā |
viruddhatā ca, yādṛgdhi dānais tādṛk phalaṃ bhavet ||

2.238

vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ, aduḥkhātmakatā tathā |
na ca yā sampradānasya prītis tādṛk phalaṃ śrutam ||

2.239

dātus tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate |
sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||

2.240

vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tv etadviruddhatā |
prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||

2.241

dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, <88>
tasya kīdṛk phalaṃ bhavet |
japahomādidṛṣṭāntāt parapīḍādivarjanāt ||

2.242

coditatvasya hetutvād viruddhāvyabhicāritā |
vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyan na ca kāraṇam ||

2.243

dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ |
anugrahāc ca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatām ||

2.244

vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet |
krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||

2.245

bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hy upakāritā |
anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||

2.246

hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmād dṛṣṭāṃ pīḍām apaśyataḥ |
poḍātaś cāpy adharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ ||

2.247

anyonyāśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan |
evamādāv aśāstrajñomleccho nodvijate kva cit ||

2.248

tasya nādharmayogaḥ syāt pūrvoktā yadi kalpanā |<89>
tasmād anugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvam apāsya ca |

2.249

dharmādharmārthibhir nityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau |
kva cid asyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||

2.250

pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati |
śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||

2.251

vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām |
tad eva cedaṃ karmeti śāstram evānudhāvatā ||

2.252

hiṃsādīnām adharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ |
evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhus tair apy etat parīkṣyatām ||

2.253

surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ |
vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syād viprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||

2.254

pañcamyām iṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ |
tasmād yady ādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||

2.255

śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tat phalam |
hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||

2.256

pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate |<90>
jñānam eva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||

2.257

jñāyante śāstratas tāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ |
vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣv api karmasu ||

2.258

abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātur eṣv api |
rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāder bhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||

2.259

tathāpy ekaphalatvaṃ cet kriyātvāt sarvasaṅkaraḥ |
yajitvādyaviśeṣāc ca citrādiphalatulyatā ||

2.260

bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced ihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati |
vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||

2.261

puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate |
na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhān na ca kalpyate ||

2.262

na ca prakaraṇasthatvāt puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet |
karmopakāraḥ kalpyas tu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||<91>

2.263

kalpanāvasaras tatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt |
kratvarthaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ paśor nārādupakriyā ||

2.264

dṛṣṭaiva tv avadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā |
abhicāre 'py upāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate |

2.265

tasmād anaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyām etad ucyate |
uddeśāc ca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||

2.266

bhāvanāvidhir apy eva phalāṃśād vinivartate |
ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenāder nāpy adharmatā ||

2.267

phalānarthānubandhitvāt taddvāreṇopacaryate |
nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||<92>

2.268

tasmāt kriyāntarād eva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate |
phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||

2.269

kevalaprītihetutvāt taddharmatvena hīṣyate |
nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāder dharmatā bhavet ||

2.270

phalaṃ tāvad adharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate |
yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syād anuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||

2.271

tasya dharmatvam ucyeta tataḥ śyenādivarjanam |
yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||

2.272

dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāt tadā śyene 'pi dharmatā |
yadi tv aprītihetur yaḥ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||

2.273

so 'dharmaś codanārthaḥ syāt tadā śyene 'py adharmatā |
yas tu hiṃsātvasādharmyād bāhyavaccodanāsv api ||

2.274

vaded anarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpy āgamabādhanam |
tam anādṛtya yo brūyād yāgāder apy asau vadet ||

2.275

svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvād bhojanādivat |<93>
gītāmantrārthavādair yā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||

2.276

pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvāt sānyārthatvena nīyate |
śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt sūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||

2.277

aśakteś cobhayoḥ sāmyān na sūtreṣv ity anuttaram |
prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate ||

2.278

sūtreṣu hy anayā yuktyā gatir eṣāpi yujyate |
tasmād āvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||<94>

2.279

ekadeśānumānād vā dve sūtre parikalpite |
itaretarasāmīpyād etāv eva parasparam ||

2.280

kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā |
viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvād atha vety api bhāṣite ||

2.281

vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvam uttaram |
arthaṃ vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ |

2.282

tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ |
dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||

2.283

vṛttam eva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate |<95>
codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||

2.284

labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hy anyathā bhavet |
tathā ca ye 'py anarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||

2.285

niṣedhais te 'pi dharmāḥ syuś codanālakṣaṇatvataḥ |
tasmād arthāparityāgād ekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||

2.286

labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syād arthānuvādataḥ |
viśeṣaṇād vinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||<96>

2.287

kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam ||

{3 nimittasūtra NMS}

3.1

pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yady api |
vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||

3.2

pratijñāmātram ityetajjaiminer matam ucyate |
vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāram abravīt ||

{4 pratyakṣasūtra PAS}

<97>

4.1

varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam |
tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||

4.2

lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate |
kimarthaṃ cānumānāder lakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||

4.3

na tāvad apramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpy akṣabuddhiṣu |
śakyate 'ntargatir vaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||

4.4

na cāpi siddhir eṣāṃ syād arthāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇāt |
na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇam iti niścitam ||

4.5

pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiś ca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt |
vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||<98>

4.6

tadetatpūrvakatve dhīr na ca tallakṣaṇād bhavet |
tadukter vānumānādi kiṃ na syāt tadapūrvakam ||

4.7

na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yat tayor api |
pratyakṣalakṣaṇād eṣāṃ kathañ cid avadhāraṇā ||

4.8

prasiddhatvād avācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate |
tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||

4.9

na tv ekaṃ lakṣayed eṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañ cana |
sambhavaty ekavākyatve vākyabhedaś ca neṣyate ||

4.10

na cāpy etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam |
tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||

4.11

taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet |
kena cit samprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syān niyogataḥ ||<99>

4.12

grāhyeṇānyena vety etat kṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam |
samprayogasya yena syād viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||

4.13

asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe |
tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||

4.14

tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāder yadutthitam |
viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||

4.15

satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaś ced, etad eva hi |
pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhir eva ca ||

4.16

svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttir vā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati |
tasmād vidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||

4.17

tena naiṣā vacovyaktir yatsatīndriyasaṅgame |<100>
vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||

4.18

pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ |
vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||

4.19

evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā |
evaṃliṅgakam ityetad bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||

4.20

yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam |
tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animittatā ||

4.21

pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye |<101>
asmād ādau prasiddhatvād yogyartham abhidhīyate ||

4.22

prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt |
tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiś ca sambandhāder anīkṣaṇāt ||

4.23

śakyam anyāpramāṇatvam iti sūtrair na paṭhyate |
na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||

4.24

na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati |<102>
sarvathā lokasiddhatvād dharmo 'yaṃ tāvad iṣyate ||

4.25

tataś ca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate |
animittaprasaṅgas tu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||

4.26

atītānāgate 'py arthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca |
pratyakṣaṃ yoginām iṣṭaṃ kaiś cin muktātmanām api ||

4.27

vidyamānopalambhatvam asiddhaṃ tatra tān prati |
bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyair vyabhicāritā ||

4.28

mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sad ity ayam |
na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yoginām api ||

4.29

pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |
satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpy asmatpratyakṣavad bhavet ||<103>

4.30

teṣām avartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ |
pratyakṣaṃ sā tatas tv eva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||

4.31

loke cāpy aprasiddhatvāt pratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ |
pratibhāvad dvayāsattvaṃ sad ity etena kathyate ||

4.32

laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī |
na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syād yoginām api ||

4.33

avidyamānasaṃyogāt syāc cet pratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit |
bhaviṣyaty api dharme syāc chaktety āha sad ity ayam ||<104>

4.34

pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānān na dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā |
phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāsty asau ||

4.35

asmatpratyakṣavac cāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |
pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvāc ca neṣyate ||

4.36

avidyamānasaṃyogāt pratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ |
yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||<105>

4.37

saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ |
pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||

4.38

samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ |
prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||

4.39

duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt |
evaṃ saty anuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||

4.40

tataś cāprāpyakāritvād yad bauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ |<106>
lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||

4.41

prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila |
adhiṣṭānādhikaś cārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||

4.42

vyāpāramātravācitvād aviruddhaṃ tad atra naḥ |
yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||

4.43

yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ |
sāṃkhyādīn vā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||

4.44

tayoś ca prāpyakāritvam indriyatvāt tvagādivat |
ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāc ca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||

4.45

cikitsādiprayogaś ca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate |
so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||

4.46

taddeśaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate |<107>
cakṣurādyupakāraś ca pādādāv api dṛśyate ||

4.47

tasmān naikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāt tatra vartanam |
bahirvṛttis tayoś ceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||

4.48

adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam |
pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||

4.49

dīpaprabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati |
tathā bahirgatāpy eṣā mūlacchedād vinaśyati ||

4.50

adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu saty apy ucchinnayatnayā |
tayārtho 'nupanītatvād ātmanā nānubhūyate ||

4.51

vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syād adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca |
śabde tv ādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāv asambhavāt ||<108>

4.52

puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau |
puruṣo laukiko vā syād yo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||<109>

4.53

vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate |
buddhijanmeti cāpy āha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||

4.54

vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ |
pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūd iti janma vivakṣyate ||

4.55

na hi tat kṣaṇam apy āste, jāyate vāpramātmakam |
yenārthagrahaṇe paścād vyāpriyetendriyādivat ||

4.56

tena janmaiva viṣaye buddher vyāpāra iṣyate |
tad eva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||

4.57

janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam |<110>
tac ca bhūtabhaviṣyattvāt kṛtaṃ buddher viśeṣaṇam ||

4.58

yadāpy aulūkyasiddhāntāt samavāyasya janmatā |
buddhis tatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||

4.59

pramāṇaphalabhāvaś ca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām |
sarvathāpy animittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||

4.60

yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt tasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ |
manaso vendriyair yoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||

4.61

tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārāc ca pramāṇatā |
vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||

4.62

na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate |<111>
yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāt tatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||

4.63

prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate |
mā bhūt kāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||

4.64

yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvād indriyārthayoḥ |
niyatā saṅgatir hetuḥ phale 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||

4.65

yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ |
vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpy akṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||<112>

4.66

saṃyoge tv ātmamanasoḥ syāc ced viṣayabhinnatā |
pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||

4.67

athāpy āśraya iṣṭas te na yogād viṣayāntaram |
ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||

4.68

prakṛṣṭasādhanatvāc ca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ |
karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā ||

4.69

pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate |
pramāṇaṃ tv indriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||

4.70

pramāṇaphalate buddhyor viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||<113>

4.71

viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam |
prasūte niścayaṃ paścāt tasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||

4.72

niścayas tu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāv ālocite tadā |
tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syād arthānavadhāraṇāt ||

4.73

hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ ced viśeṣyadhīḥ |
upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaś cet, iyaṃ phalam ||

4.74

viṣayaikatvam icchaṃs tu yaḥ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ vadet |
sādhyasādhanayor bhedo laukikas tena bādhitaḥ ||

4.75

chedane khadiraprāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā |
tathaiva paraśor loke cchidayā saha naikatā ||<114>

4.76

bhavate bhedahānena rucitā viṣayaikatā |
tattyāgena parebhyas tu bhedo rucim upāgataḥ ||

4.77

karaṇatvopacāras tu phale cet kalpyate tvayā |
kathañ cid viṣayaikatvaṃ parair vā kiṃ na kalpyate ||

4.78

paricchedaphalatvena vṛttasyānantarasya naḥ |
pramāṇatvaṃ bhavej jñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||

4.79

svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhān na yujyate |
pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvān na yujyate ||<115>

4.80

svākāraś ca svasaṃvittiṃ muktvā nānyaḥ pratīyate |
prāmāṇyaṃ yasya kalpyeta svasaṃvittiphalaṃ prati ||

4.81

svākārasya paricchedo na cākārāntarād vinā |
tasyāpy evaṃ tathā ca syān nākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||

4.82

na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate |
grāhye ca viṣayākāre grāhako 'nyo na labhyate ||

4.83

manasas tv indriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu |
manasā samprayukto hi tāny ātmā pratipadyate ||

4.84

sambaddhaṃ vartamānaṃ ca grahyate cakṣurādinā |
sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||<116>

4.85

lakṣaṇaṃ yac ca yair uktaṃ pratyakṣe laukike sati |
vidyamānopalambhitvāt sarvasyaivānimittatā ||

4.86

nirvikalpakapakṣe tu sutarām animittatā |
sādhyasādhanasambandho nāvikalpya hi gṛhyate ||

4.87

kathaṃ pratyakṣapūrvatvam anumānādi no bhavet |
yadā smṛtyasamarthatvān nirvikalpendriyasya dhīḥ ||

4.88

na cāvikalpya liṅgasya liṅgisambandhayos tathā |
gṛhītiḥ, <117>
upamāne 'pi sādṛśyagrahaṇāt smṛteḥ ||

4.89

arthāpattiḥ punaḥ prāyo nānyadṛṣṭe 'rtha iṣyate |
pravartate ca yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'py arthaḥ savikalpakaḥ ||

4.90

yatra cānumitaṃ liṅgaṃ sūryagatyādi liṅgi ca |
tatra pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate ||

4.91

pratyakṣāvagate cārthe kutas teṣāṃ pramāṇatā |
tair yadā sa pratīyeta tadā nākṣasya gocaraḥ ||

4.92

atha kasya cid arthasya jñānāt tatpūrvatā bhavet |
tadārthasya bhaviṣyattvaṃ na syād ajñānakāraṇam ||<118>

4.93

vartamāne hi kasmiṃś cid vijñāte 'rthe 'kṣabuddhibhiḥ |
liṅgād avidyamāno 'pi dharmo gamyeta tais tadā ||

4.94

pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇān vede 'pi gṛhyate |
prameyam iti so 'pi syāt tatpūrvatvād akāraṇam ||

4.95

ke cit tatpūrvakatvaṃ tu hetur naiveti manvate |
tatpūrvakatvād yat tāvat prāmāṇyaṃ tadasambhavaḥ ||

4.96

pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca, liṅgādyanyatamaṃ dhruvam |
pravṛttir anumānāder na ca dharme 'sti tādṛśam ||

4.97

anumānānumānāder na cāpy astīha sambhavaḥ |
sambandhaliṅgiliṅgānāṃ pūrvasiddher asambhavāt ||

4.98

sattā ca nānumānena kasya cit pratipadyate |
dharmeṇānyad viśeṣyaṃ cet, <119>
pakṣo 'siddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||

4.99

tasmād adṛṣṭapūrvatvāt kena cid vastunā saha |
dharmasya nānumeyatvam asādhāraṇavastuvat ||

4.100

adṛṣṭasadṛśatvāc ca svyaṃ cānupalambhanāt |
dharmasya nopameyatvam asādhāraṇavad bhavet ||

4.101

nanv arthāpattir evaṃ syāj jagadvaicitryadarśanāt |
sukhiduḥkhādibhedo hi nādṛṣṭāt kāraṇād ṛte ||

4.102

dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāritvāt tadabhāve 'pi sambhavāt |<120>
sevāvyayanatulyatve dṛṣṭā ca phalabhinnatā ||

4.103

syād evaṃ yadi śakyeta svābhāvikanivāraṇā |
karmaśakteś ca vaicitrye hetur anyo bhaved yadi ||

4.104

yathā ca phalavaicitrye karmaṇāṃ śaktatā svataḥ |
tathā ca citratā loke svabhāvād upapatsyate ||

4.105

adharme dharmarūpe vā hy avibhakte phalaṃ prati |
kim apy astīti vijñānaṃ narāṇāṃ kvopayujyate ||

4.106

kiṃ nu yāgād ito dukhaṃ hiṃsādeḥ kiṃ sukhodbhavaḥ |
svargaputrādibhedaś ca kīdṛśāt karmabhedataḥ ||

4.107

iti yāvad avijñānaṃ tāvan naiva pravartate |
pravṛttyaṅgaṃ ca yajjñānaṃ tasya mūlaṃ pratīkṣyate ||

4.108

tasmāt siddhe 'pi sāmānye viśeṣo nāgamād ṛte |<121>
viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritā ||

4.109

gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tadantarbhāvakāritaḥ |
sāmānyapratyayo 'pi syāc chāstrād evety akāraṇam ||

4.110

yathārthāpattir evaṃ ca nānumānopameṣyate |
śāstraṃ cet tadapekṣeta tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||

4.111

pratyakṣāgrahaṇaṃ yat tu liṅgāder avikalpanāt |
tan na, iṣṭatvād vikalpasyāpy artharūpopakāriṇaḥ ||

4.112

asti hy ālocanā jñānaṃ prathamaṃ nirvikapakam |
bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam ||<122>

4.113

na viśeṣo na sāmānyaṃ tadānīmanubhūyate |
tayor ādhārabhūtā tu, vyaktir evāvasīyate ||

4.114

mahāsāmānyam anyais tu dravyaṃ sad iti cocyate |
sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca pratyakṣasyaivam āśritam ||

4.115

viśeṣās tu pratīyante savikalpakabuddhibhiḥ |
te ca ke cit pratidravyaṃ ke cid bahuṣu saṃśritāḥ ||

4.116

tān akalpayad utpannaṃ vyāvṛttānugatātmanā |
gavyaśve copajātaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ na viśiṣyate ||<123>

4.117

tad ayuktam, pratidravyaṃ bhinnarūpopalambhanāt |
na hy ākhyātum aśakyatvād bhedo nāstīti gamyate ||

4.118

nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi dvyātmakasyāpi vastunaḥ |
grahaṇam, <124>
lakṣaṇākhyeyaṃ jñātrā śuddhaṃ tu gṛhyate ||

4.119

na cāsādhāraṇatvena paravyāvṛttyakalpanāt |
viśeṣānugamākḷpteḥ sāmānyam iti nāpi tat ||

4.120

tataḥ paraṃ punarvastudharmair jātyādibhir yayā |
buddhyāvasīyate sāpi pratyakṣatvena sammatā ||

4.121

karaṇaṃ cendriyaṃ buddher na tatra jñānam āhitam |
tataḥ smṛtyasamarthatvād vikalpo 'to na vāryate ||

4.122

ātmany eva sthitaṃ jñānam, sa hi boddhātra gamyate |
smaraṇe cāsya sāmarthyaṃ sandhānādau ca vidyate ||

4.123

tenendriyārthasambandhe vicyamāne smarann api |
vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavān naraḥ ||<125>

4.124

tac caitadindriyādhīnam iti tair vyapadiśyate |
tadasambandhajātaṃ tu naiva pratyakṣam iṣyate ||

4.125

punaḥ punarvikalpe 'pi satī jātiḥ pratīyate |
tatsambandhānusāreṇa sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iṣyate ||

4.126

na hi praviṣṭamātrāṇām uṣṇād garbhagṛhādiṣu |
arthā na pratibhāntīti gṛhyante nendriyaiḥ punaḥ ||

4.127

yathā tv ābhāsamātreṇa pūrvaṃ jñātvā svarūpataḥ |
paścāt tatrāvabudhyante tathā jātyādidharmataḥ ||

4.128

yadi tv ālocya saṃmīlya netre kaś cid vikalpayet |
na syāt pratyakṣatā tasya sambandhānanusārataḥ ||

4.129

asambaddhavikalpe 'pi tulyam ātmādi kāraṇam |
tenāsādhāraṇatvaṃ syād atrākṣasyaiva kalpane ||<126>

4.130

nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi nākṣaṃ kevalakāraṇam |
tatpāramparyajāte vā rūḍhiḥ syāt paṅkajādivat ||

4.131

animittaiva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarāṃ savikalpakam |
pratyakṣaṃ sammataṃ loke na tathā nirvikalpakam ||

4.132

vṛddhaprayogagamyāś ca śabdārthāḥ sarva eva naḥ |
tena yatra prayukto 'yaṃ na tasmād apanīyate ||

4.133

siddhānugamamātraṃ hi kartuṃ yuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |
na sarvalokasiddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam ||

4.134

kalpanāyāḥ svasaṃvittāv indriyādhīnatā katham |
manas tatrendriyaṃ cet syād gotvādāv api tatsamam ||

4.135

svasaṃvittau tad iṣṭaṃ cet, <127>
loko na hy evam icchati |
tasmād rūḍhatvam eṣṭavyaṃ pāribhāṣikatāpi vā ||

4.136

manasas tv indriyatvena sudhaduḥkhādibuddhiṣu |
yathā pratyakṣataivaṃ nas tadadhīnā bhaviṣyati ||

4.137

tadadhīnatvasāmye 'pi kalpanāpoḍhaśabdanāt |
pratyakṣaṃ kiñ cid eveṣṭaṃ yathā tatra tathaiva naḥ ||

4.138

liṅgādyabhāvataś cāpi nānumānādidhīr iyam |
bādhakapratyayāsattvān nāprāmāṇyaṃ ca yujyate ||

4.139

na ca parvamadṛṣṭatvāt smṛtitvam upapadyate |
tasmāt pratyakṣam evedam, vyavahāras tathaiva ca ||<128>

4.140

jātyādyarthāntaraṃ yasmād atadrūpe 'pi vastuni |
bhavaty adhyasya dhīs tasmān mṛgatṛṣṇādibhiḥ samā ||

4.141

naitadaśvādibuddhīnām adhyāropādyasambhavāt |
sthitaṃ naiva hi jātyādeḥ paratvaṃ vyaktito hi naḥ ||

4.142

yadi hy ekāntato bhinnaṃ viśeṣyāt syād viśeṣaṇam |
svānurūpāṃ sadā buddhiṃ viśeṣye janayet katham ||

4.143

sphaṭikādau tu lākṣādisvarūpā yā matir bhavet |
avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānāṃ hi bhedadhīḥ ||<129>

4.144

na tu jātyādinirmuktaṃ vastu dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana |
tadvimokena vā tāni lākṣādisphaṭikādivat ||

4.145

tatrāpi cen na dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiś cit kadā cana |
raktādibuddhisamyaktvaṃ vinivāryeta kena vā ||

4.146

na cāpy ayutasiddhānāṃ sambandhitvena kalpanā |
nāniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ, niṣpattau yutasiddhatā ||

4.147

tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaś cin na vidyate |
tasmāc cāpi na sambandhaḥ padārthānāṃ pratīyate ||<130>

4.148

samavāyaviyogāc ca viśleṣaḥ syāt parasparam |
tatkḷptāvavyavasthā syāt tasya tasyānyasaṅgateḥ ||

4.149

atha tasyātmarūpatvān nānyasambandhakalpanā |
abhedāt samavāyo 'stu svarūpaṃ dharmadharmiṇoḥ ||

4.150

na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandhaṃ pratipadyate |
tasmiṃs tābhyām abhinne tu na nānātvaṃ tayor bhavet ||

4.151

nanu dharmātirekeṇa dharmiṇo 'nupalambhanāt |
tatsaṅghamātra evāyaṃ gavādiḥ syād vanādivat ||<131>

4.152

āvirbhāvatirobhāvadharmakeṣv anuyāyi yat |
taddharmi yatra vā jñānaṃ prāgdharmagrahaṇād bhavet ||

4.153

ato jātyādirūpeṇa dharmi yad gṛhyate naiḥ |
pārarūpyaṃ na tasyāstīty aprāmāṇyaṃ na yujyate ||

4.154

yasyāpi vyatirekaḥ syād dharmebhyo dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
nityaṃ tasyāpi tādrūpyān na mithyātvaṃ prasajyate ||

4.155

yo hy asadrūpasaṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetān yathā punaḥ |
sa mithyā na tu tenaiva yo nityam avagamyate ||

4.156

na cānekendriyagrāhyaṃ bhinnatāṃ pratipadyate |<132>
mā bhūd bhinnaśarīrasthagrāhyatvād bhinnarūpatā ||

4.157

jātyabhedād abhedaś cet, indriyatvena tatsamam |
tulyabuddher ato bhinnā na sattendriyabhedataḥ ||

4.158

buddhibhedāc ca naikatvaṃ rūpādīnāṃ prasajyate |
ekānekatvam iṣṭaṃ vā sattārūpādirūpataḥ ||

4.159

kva cic ca saṅkarān nākṣam ekam ity avasīyate |
dārḍhyadaurbalyabhedena vyavasthāpi yataḥ kva cit ||

4.160

yathā hi manasaḥ sārdhaṃ rūpādau cakṣurādinā |
pravṛttiḥ sukhaduḥkhādau kevalasyaiva dṛśyate ||<133>

4.161

na kva cit saṅkarābhāvāt sarvatraiva nivartate |
kva cic ca saṅkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkaro 'nyatra kalpyate ||

4.162

śrotrāder upaghāte 'pi śabdādismṛtidarśanāt |
vartamānasya cājñānād vyavasthā sampratīyate ||

4.163

ekaṃ yadi bhaved akṣaṃ sarvair gṛhyeta vā na vā |
kalpyate śaktibhedaś cet, śaktir evendriyaṃ bhavet ||

4.164

śṛṇuyād badhiraḥ śabdaṃ saṅkare cakṣurādinā |
manaso vā svatantratve vartamānārthabuddhiṣu ||<134>

4.165

na smared badhiraḥ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ cet smṛtikāraṇam |
smṛtivad vā bhaved asya vartamānārthadhīr api ||

4.166

smṛtiś ca na bhavet paścād gṛhṇīyāt tan na cen manaḥ |
śrotragrahaṇavelāyām, na cāsarvā smṛtir bhavet ||

4.167

bodhātmakatayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
yugapadviṣaye 'py asya karaṇāpekṣitā na cet ||

4.168

tasmāj jñānānusāreṇa vyavasthāsaṅkarau kva cit |
grāhyagrāhakaśaktibhyaḥ kāryadvāreṇa kalpitau ||<135>

4.169

cakṣūrūpādibhedas tu pañcadhaiva vyavasthitaḥ |
tena nīlādibhede 'pi nendriyānantyakalpanā ||

4.170

tasmāt pañcabhir apy akṣair bodhaḥ sattāguṇatvayoḥ |
dravyamūrtau punardvābhyāṃ rūpādāv ekaśaḥ sthitaḥ ||

4.171

nanu jātyādirūpe 'pi śabdābhedopacārataḥ |
pravartamānā mithya syād buddhī rūpeṣu buddhivat ||

4.172

na śabdābhedarūpeṇa buddhir artheṣu jāyate |
prāk śabdād yādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdād api hi tādṛśī ||

4.173

nanu gotvādirūpeṇa gavākārādibuddhayaḥ |
na prāk śabdārthasambandhajñānāt santi kadā cana ||

4.174

jātyādes tatsvarūpaṃ ced aśabdajño 'pi lakṣayet |
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdarūpatvaniścayaḥ ||<136>

4.175

yathā rūpādayo bhinnāḥ prāk śabdāt svātmanaiva tu |
gamyante tadvad evaitat saṃjñitvaṃ kevalaṃ param ||

4.176

na cāvikalpitaḥ śabdād iti vācyo na gṛhyate |
tenāgṛhītaśabdo 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate ||

4.177

śrutisaṃsparśabodhe 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate |
vivekād arthaśabdānāṃ cakṣuḥ śrotradhiyā kṛtāt ||

4.178

anantadharmake dharmiṇy ekadharmāvadhāraṇe |
śabdo 'bhyupāyamātraṃ syān nātmādhyāropakāraṇam ||

4.179

na copeye 'bhyupāyasya rūpādhyāsaḥ prasajyate |
na hi dīpendriyādīnāṃ rūpādhyāropa iṣyate ||

4.180

nityaṃ yadi ca gotvādi śabdarūpeṇa gṛhyate |
rūpāntaraṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ ced bhedādhyāsau kuto nvimau ||<137>

4.181

yady abhedo na mithyātvam, bhedaś cet syāt svarūpataḥ |
nādhyāropaprasaṅgaḥ syād bhrāntyā tv adhyāsakalpanā ||

4.182

śabdenaiva ca nirdeśo gṛhīte 'rthe 'vakalpate |
gaur ity eva ca nirdeśo vācyatadbuddhivādinām ||

4.183

nirdeśatulyatāyāṃ ca śrotrā vaktṛsvarūpatā |
śabdajñānaprameyeṣu vijñānasyāvasīyate ||

4.184

bhrāntihetusamānatve 'py upāyatvānmatiśrutī |
manyate 'rthe samadhyaste nārthādhyāsaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ||

4.185

gotve sāsnādimadrūpāṅgādirūpābhidhāyake |
nirākārobhayajñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ ||

4.186

yadi cābhedarūpeṇa śabdenārthaḥ pratīyate |
ekarūpatvam akṣādau devanādeḥ prasajyate ||<138>

4.187

syād anakṣanivṛtyā cet, na prāk śabdāt pratīyate |
gavādiṣv api tulyaṃ cet, nekarūpasya darśanāt ||

4.188

traye bibhītakādīnāṃ naikadharmānvayo 'sti hi |
śabdaḥ sādhāraṇas teṣāṃ jātiśabdād vilakṣaṇaḥ ||

4.189

parasparavibhinnaṃ tu jñāyate 'trākṛtitrayam |
tadadhyāse na yujyeta tadrūpasyāvibhāgataḥ ||

4.190

bhinnāḥ syur akṣaśabdāś cet, nārthe saṃśayadarśanāt |
na sāmānyād ṛte sa syād, rūpābhedaś ca gamyate ||

4.191

bhavatyādau ca bhinne 'pi nāmākhyātatvasaṃjñayā |
rūpaikatvena cādhyāse tulyārthatvaṃ prasajyate ||<139>

4.192

śabdaniṣpattyabhedāc ca tiṅantārthasya sādhyatā |
katham, kathaṃ ca mūrtārtho vācake mūrtivarjite ||

4.193

gavāśvaśuklaśabdāder vācyarūpānapekṣaṇe |
vācakatvavyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ jātiguṇādiṣu ||

4.194

vṛkṣaplakṣādiśabdānāṃ tulye bhede ghaṭādibhiḥ |
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ katham arthānapekṣayā ||

4.195

sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na syad vācakabuddhivat |
ekatra copasaṃhāro na buddhyor nirvikalpake ||

4.196

vastumātre sa ced evaṃ sarveṣām ekavācyatā |
bhaved gavādiśabdānāṃ sarvair vastu hi gamyate ||<140>

4.197

na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam itīṣyate |
na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syād anyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||

4.198

na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate |
śabdārthayor yato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||

4.199

śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣv api dṛśyate |
ekādhikaraṇās tena syus te nīlotpalādivat ||

4.200

na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padam arthe prayujyate |
tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||

4.201

tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ |
na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||

4.202

tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā |
śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||

4.203

mama vācyānabhijñatvān na bhavet smaraṇaṃ tataḥ |
bhavatas tv artharūpasya vācakeṣv api darśanāt ||<141>

4.204

yathā tv ajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīr na jāyate |
tathaivājñātavācyānām upalabdhe 'pi vācake ||

4.205

tasmān nātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet |
smārakatvāc ca teṣv eva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||

4.206

tena sambandhavelāyām arthātmā yo 'vasīyate |
śabdād api sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||

4.207

pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim |
tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañ cit pratīyate ||

4.208

karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ |
bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||

4.209

ātmādhyāsas tu sādṛśyād uparāgāc ca dṛśyate |
na tāvad arthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||

4.210

na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate |
dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||

4.211

śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptir ucyate |
sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvair evānurañjanam ||

4.212

na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñ cid asty anurāgakṛt |<142>
na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīs tvagādibhiḥ ||

4.213

anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane |
nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||

4.214

tathās tv iti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati |
katham evaṃ vaded artho nānṛtād dhi pratīyate ||

4.215

śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ |
pravṛttir na tu tat tantram artharūpaṃ kadā cana ||

4.216

tasmāt prāg api ye śabdād bhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ |
gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||

4.217

śabdābhyupāyake 'py arthe tadabhāve ca yady api |
arthabuddhir na jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||

4.218

cakṣurāder abhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate |
svarūpanāśo rūpādes tāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||<143>

4.219

sambandhasya ca nityatvān nārethasya syād arūpatā |
yugapanna hi sarveṣām anyākārārthavedanam ||

4.220

tadākāre 'pi tadvac ced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām |
kiṃ nv arthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nv aśaktatā ||

4.221

sadasadbhāvayor arthe virodhitvād asambhavaḥ |
grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvam aśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||

4.222

yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyety abhidhāsyate |
tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||

4.223

devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt |
arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpy anityatā ||<144>

4.224

tatrāpy autpattikī śaktis tadrūpapratyayaṃ prati |
grāhyagrāhakayor iṣṭā niyogasya tv anityatā ||

4.225

tatra sarvair atādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogāt pratīyate |
teneṣṭam eva mithyātvaṃ kaiś cid adhyāsakalpane ||

4.226

yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdāt pratīyate |
tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdas tatra yathārthatā ||

4.227

niyogāt parato vāpi śabdena vyajyatām iyam |
tadgrāhyaśaktir arthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||<145>

4.228

sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā |
sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||

4.229

tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā |
buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānād upajāyate ||

4.230

cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣam asau bhavet |
viviktā eva te 'py arthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||

4.231

smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣatā tayoḥ |
tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tv arthasyāpi vāryate ||

4.232

gṛhītam api gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yady api |
tathāpi vyatirekeṇa pūrvabodhāt pratīyate ||

4.233

vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāsty avasaro miteḥ |<146>
yaḥ pūrvāvagato 'ṃśo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||

4.234

idānīn tanam astitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam |
na hi smaraṇato yatprāk tat pratyakṣam itīdṛśam ||

4.235

vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate |
na cāpi smaraṇāt paścād indriyasya pravartanam ||

4.236

vāryate kena cin nātastat tadānīṃ praduṣyati |
tenendriyārthasambandhāt prāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||

4.237

vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iti gamyatām |
vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api cendriyaiḥ ||

4.238

na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ |
tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣv api ||

4.239

sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirnaṃ tāvatā |
yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||

4.240

vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ |
gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtās tu ye ||

4.241

tadajñānān na mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām |<147>
te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpy eṣaṃ viviktatām ||

4.242

yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvad gotvādivas tv api |
saṅkīrṇam arthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsarvajitāḥ ||

4.243

vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ |
yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||

4.244

sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyan na gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ |
tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||

4.245

tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt |
tena yāvat pramātāṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||

4.246

na syāt tāvad bhavet teṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam |
tasmād yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||

4.247

pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane |
pratyakṣatvam ataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||

4.248

sambandhasyeti tat pūrvam anumānādi jāyate |
sarvaṃ cāpy anumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||

4.249

na pravartata ity etadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate |<148>
nanv evaṃ sati yāpy agner dūrād apy auṣṇyakalpanā ||

4.250

sāpi pratyakṣam eva syād yathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ |
pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||

4.251

vijñānaṃ nānyad astīti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ |
tatrāpy akṣair asambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||

4.252

yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate |
sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||

4.253

tasmād yadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam |
tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||

4.254

evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ |
pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

{5,1 vṛttikāragrantha VKG}

<149>

5,1.1

pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ |
dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||

5,1.2

dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau |
prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||

5,1.3

idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye |
ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||

5,1.4

nirmūlāsambhavād atra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate |
kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||<150>

5,1.5

na caitāni parityajya pṛthag loke pramāṇatā |
saṃsāramocakādeś ca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||

5,1.6

na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cid evaṃ vigānataḥ |
mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||

5,1.7

na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstram anāśritam |
tanmūlārthaprasiddhis tu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||

5,1.8

tasmād abhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śaknuyāt |
codanā cet samuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||

5,1.9

upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate |
jñāyate yena tajjñānam ekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||

5,1.10

autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate |
abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatas tena pramāṇatā ||<151>

5,1.11

sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtir anyathā |
codanā copadeśaś ca vidhiś caikārthavācinaḥ ||

5,1.12

vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhir āśritaḥ |
sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||

5,1.13

sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt |
pravṛttisiddhir icchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam ||

5,1.14

vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate |
śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||

5,1.15

vidhau tu tam atikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate |
tatsādhanasya dharmatvam evaṃ sati ca labhyate ||<152>

5,1.16

svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syād anāptanaroktiṣu |
āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||

{5.2}

5,2.17

ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ, luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ |
nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarāt paricodanā ||

5,2.18

pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānād vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam |
naitat pratyakṣam ityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||

5,2.19

tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā |<153>
yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tad iṣyate ||

5,2.20

sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hy etat, tatsator vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ |
śobhanārthas tu sacchabdaḥ, yad vākhyāhārakalpanā ||

5,2.21

arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam |
bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||

5,2.22

sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam |
na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||<154>

5,2.23

nimittadoṣabodhena paścād yatrāpy abādhanam |
bhavaty eva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||

5,2.24

sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam |
na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhis tatra balīyasī ||<155>

5,2.25

jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścād asambhavāt |
nāśyate yuktibhis tatra vyaktam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||

5,2.26

svataḥ prāmāṇyataś cātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt |
tadrūpapratyayotpattes tadasadvādinām api ||

{5,3 nirālambanavāda NAV}

5,3.1

pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam |
vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||

5,3.2

sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣv evaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ |
vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||

5,3.3

karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike |
sarvam ityādy ayuktaṃ syād arthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||<156>

5,3.4

tasmād dharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇair lokasammataiḥ |
arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||

5,3.5

yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvam etat prakalpyate |
jñānamātre 'pi kasmād vo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||

5,3.6

saṃvṛter na tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam |
satyā cet saṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cet satyatā katham ||

5,3.7

satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ |<157>
virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||

5,3.8

tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ |
vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||

5,3.9

nāstikyaparihārārthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, kalpaneti ca |
kalpanāpi tv abhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||

5,3.10

tasmād yan nāsti nāsty eva, yat tv asti paramārthataḥ |
tat satyam anyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||

5,3.11

svapnādibhogavac cāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā |
tannivṛttyartham eveha paramārthe kaś cit pravartate ||

5,3.12

na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaś cit pravartate |
yādṛcchikatvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||

5,3.13

paramārthaphalāvāptim icchadbhis tena yatnataḥ |
pratipattir vidhātavyā yuktibhir bāhyavastuṣu ||<158>

5,3.14

tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ |
tasyāpy abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||

5,3.15

tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvad dvayor api |
nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvat saṃvṛtikalpanā ||

5,3.16

tasmāt sādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpy ayam |
bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||

5,3.17

bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitam ekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt |
pramāṇam āśritaś caikas tatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||

5,3.18

pramāṇasthas tu mūlatvād ihedānīṃ parīkṣyate |
prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tv anumānataḥ ||

5,3.19

pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāt tacchaktyavekṣaṇāt |
tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanv iti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||

5,3.20

tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam |
tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||

5,3.21

kalpitaḥ samprayogas tu svapnādāv api vidyate |
tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgas tena durlabhaḥ ||<159>

5,3.22

mithyātvaṃ yad dvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathety atra cocyate |
sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||

5,3.23

stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāt tathā hi yaḥ |
pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||

5,3.24

siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca |
mā bhūtām evaśabdaś ca vyartho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||

5,3.25

sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ |
svāṃśābhyupagamāc cāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||

5,3.26

pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam |
hetuś copanyenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||<160>

5,3.27

vipakṣābhāvataś cātra vyatireko na kathyate |
sāmānyasya ca hetutvāt kasmāt pakṣaikadeśatā ||

5,3.28

jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ |
bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||

5,3.29

tasmād yad bhāṣyakāreṇa dattam uttam atra tu |
vikalpasamatā vā syād vaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||

5,3.30

dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣasya jātyukti kaiś cid āśritā |
pratijñādoṣam evāhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣabādhanam ||<161>

5,3.31

śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam |
tadā te śuddha eva syāt pakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||

5,3.32

pratyakṣādeś ca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate |
tanniṣedhakṛtas tasya tair bhavet pakṣabādhanam ||

5,3.33

suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayād ṛte |
pramāṇābhāsatā nāstīty etasmāt katyate balam ||

5,3.34

duṣṭajñānagṛhītāpratiṣedho hi yujyate |
gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||

5,3.35

agrāhyatvāc ca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyam anyatarasya vā ||

5,3.36

vaktṛśrotroś ca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇviśeṣyayoḥ |
tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvyor api ||

5,3.37

sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
tasmān nirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||<162>

5,3.38

nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cid vastu gamyate |
tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||

5,3.39

yady avastu kathaṃ tv asmāṃs tvaṃ bodhayitum icchasi |
budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tv atha sādhyate ||

5,3.40

asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, kḷptau vastu prasajyate |
katham iṣṭam abhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||

5,3.41

tathā pratyaya ity eṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet |
bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma cet siddhasādhanam ||

5,3.42

pratyāyyasya hi rūpāder nirālambanateṣyate |
avijñānātmakatvena kiñ cin nālambate hy asau ||

5,3.43

kartṛtve karaṇatve vā pakṣatvaṃ śabdayor api |
tannirālambanatvena pakṣābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||<163>

5,3.44

pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartrādyasambhavaḥ |
pratyaye tannimitte vā bādhaḥ svavacanena te ||

5,3.45

athāpi rūḍhirūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāt tathāpi tu |
grāhakaṃ vastu siddhaṃ naḥ pratyayo 'nyasya vastunaḥ ||

5,3.46

tam abhyupetya pakṣaś ced abhyupetaṃ virudhyate |
viśeṣyasyāprasiddhaś ca tava, asmākam atādṛśe ||

5,3.47

ātmadharmasvatantratvakalpane 'pi tathā bhavet |
na ca pratyayamātratvaṃ kiñ cid asty anirūpaṇāt ||

5,3.48

śabdārthamātrarūpeṇa yathānyeṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |
tathā ca bhavato na syād vācyabhedamanicchataḥ ||

5,3.49

nirālambanatā cāpi sarvathā yadi sādhyate |
viśeṣaṇāprasiddhiś ca dṛṣṭāntaś ca na vidyate ||<164>

5,3.50

kena cic cet prakāreṇa nirālambanatocyate |
rasajñānasya rūpādiśūnyatvāt siddhasādhanam ||

5,3.51

atha buddhir yadākārā tadālambanavāraṇam |
svākārasyābhyupetatvāt tadabhāvo virudhyate ||

5,3.52

bāhyānālambanatve 'pi bāhya ity agraho yadi |
stambhādau naiva tadbuddhir ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam ||

5,3.53

atha stambhādirūpeṇa nirālambanatocyate |
saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭatvāt tadvirodhaḥ prasajyate ||

5,3.54

dvicandrādiṣu tulyaś cet, nendriyāprāptito hi naḥ |
tatrānālambanoktiḥ syān nārthasaṃvittyabhāvataḥ ||

5,3.55

sarvatrārthendriyāṇāṃ naḥ saṃyogasadasattayā |
saṃvittau vidyamānāyāṃ sadasadgrāhikā sthitiḥ ||<165>

5,3.56

bhavatas tv indriyādīnām abhāvād grahaṇād ṛte |
nālambanasya hetuḥ syān niṣedho 'to na yujyate ||

5,3.57

bahirbhāvāprasiddhatvāt tenānālambanā matiḥ |
kathañ cit sādhyate naiṣa pakṣo hi jñāyate tadā ||

5,3.58

yathānyabodhanāśakter nāprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe |
pakṣasiddhis tathaiva syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇe ||

5,3.59

nāprasiddhe padārthe hi vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate |
