tatpūrvakatvāt pakṣaś ca vākyārthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate ||

5,3.60

paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ |
prameyatvādyabhedena jagataḥ siddhasādhanam ||<166>

5,3.61

yadi cātyantabhedena nirālambanatocyate |
kathañ cic ced virudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena ||

5,3.62

vastvādyākārataś cāpi dhīr nirālambaneṣyate |
grāhakāc ced abhinnatvaṃ śaktibhedo virudhyate ||

5,3.63

nirālambanabuddheś ca yady utpattiḥ prasādhyate |
dṛṣṭatvāt seṣyate 'smābhir bāhyagrāhyavivarjitā ||

5,3.64

samyaktvaṃ punar etasyās tvaṃ necchasi kathañ cana |
ātmāṃśe 'vasitā hy eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat ||

5,3.65

caitrādipratyayānāṃ ca nirālambanatā yadi |
dharmabhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhanotthitayā dhiyā ||

5,3.66

tato viṣayanānātvāt pratiyogyanirākṛtā |
rūpāt sālambanaprāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate ||<167>

5,3.67

yadi pratyayaśabdo 'pi pratyayatvena gṛhyate |
saṃvittyālambanatvaṃ ca vāryate, siddhasādhanam ||

5,3.68

buddhyutpādanaśaktiś ced vāryā, sādhayaṃ na sidhyati |
sādhanasya prayogo 'tra bodhakatvād vinā na te ||

5,3.69

na cābhidhāstyasambandhād ṛte bhedāc ca nāsty asau |
na cāsau tadgataṃ bhedaṃ bodhayantya dhiyā vinā ||

5,3.70

prāśnikair agṛhīte ca vākyasyāvayave pṛthak |
pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini ||

5,3.71

sādhanasyāprayogaḥ syād abhyupetyocyate yadi |
pūrvābhyupagamenaiva pratijñā bādhyate tataḥ ||

5,3.72

dharmādharmādibhede ca nāsiddhe paramārthataḥ |
śiṣyātmanoś ca dharmāder upadeśo 'vakalpate ||

5,3.73

tadanuṣṭhānato buddher iṣṭo bhedaḥ, <168>
sphuṭaṃ ca taiḥ |
sūtrāntare 'bhyupetatvād bhaved āgamabādhanam ||

5,3.74

sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca pakṣabādho 'tra te dhruvam |
kṛtsnasādhanabuddhiś ca yadi mithyeṣyate tataḥ ||

5,3.75

sarvābhāvo yatheṣṭaṃ vā nyūnatā vābhidhīyate |
teṣāṃ sālambanatve vā tair anaikāntiko bhavet ||

5,3.76

tadanyasya pratijñā cet, tadanyapratyayo mṛṣā |
tanmithyātvaprasaṅge ca sarvaṃ pūrva na sidhyati ||

5,3.77

stambhādisādhanajñānabhedo na hi tathā bhavet |
yāvad yāvat pratijñeyaṃ tadaṅgasya pratīyate ||

5,3.78

tāvat tāvat pareṣāṃ syān mithyātvād anyabādhanam |<169>
viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ ||

5,3.79

itthaṃ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyaṃ pratisādhanam |
bāhyārthālambanā buddhir iti samyak ca dhīr iyam ||

5,3.80

bādhakāpetabuddhitvād yathā svapnādibādhadhīḥ |
sāpi mithyeti ced brūyāt, svapnādīnām abādhanāt ||

5,3.81

tasmāt sādharmyadṛṣṭānto bhavataḥ sādhane na hi |
vijñānāstitvabhinnatvakṣaṇikatvādidhīs tathā ||

5,3.82

samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadānaikāntiko bhavet |
tanmithyābhyupapattau ca pakṣabādhaḥ prasajyate ||

5,3.83

tathā ca baddham uktādivyavasthā na prakalpate |
tataś ca mokṣayatnasya vaiphalyaṃ vaḥ prasajyate ||<170>

5,3.84

vikalpotpadyamānā ca jñānāstitvādidhīr yadi |
mṛṣeṣṭā, na ca dṛṣṭātra pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||

5,3.85

pramāṇābhāvatas tena jñānāstitvādi durlabham |
sarvaṃ cāpy asmadādīnāṃ mithyā jñānaṃ vikalpanāt ||

5,3.86

sānnidhyaviprakṛṣṭatve sattvāsattve ca durlabhe |
mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi sāṃkhyādiparivarjanāt ||

5,3.87

bauddhadarśana ekasmin pakṣapāto na yujyate |
mṛṣātvaṃ yadi buddheḥ syād bādhaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate ||

5,3.88

bādhād vināpi tac cet syād vyavasthā na prakalpate |
pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrajjñāne mṛṣā bhavet ||

5,3.89

svapnādibuddhir asmākaṃ tava bhedo 'pi kiṅkṛtaḥ |
na cānyat pratiyogyasti jāgrajjñānasya śobhanam ||

5,3.90

yaddarśanena mithyātvaṃ stambhādipratyayo vrajet |
svapnādipratiyogitvaṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||

5,3.91

tadīyadharmavaidharmyād bādhakapratyayo yathā |<171>
yogināṃ jāyate buddhir bādhikā pratiyoginī ||

5,3.92

jāgratstambhādibuddhīnāṃ tataḥ svapnāditulyatā |
prāptānāṃ tām avasthāṃ ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api ||

5,3.93

bādho 'yaṃ bhavitā tena siddhā sapratiyogitā |
iha janmani keṣāñ cin na tāvad upalabhyate ||

5,3.94

yogyavasthāgatānāṃ tu na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati |
yogināṃ cāsmādīyānāṃ tvaduktapratiyoginī ||

5,3.95

tvaduktiviparītā vā bādhabuddhir bhaviṣyati |
īdṛktve yogibuddhīnāṃ dṛṣṭānto na tavāsti ca ||

5,3.96

dṛṣṭāntas tv asmādīnāṃ yo gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate |
atha stambhādibuddhīnāṃ vadet sapratiyogitām ||

5,3.97

bādhyatvaṃ cāpi buddhitvān mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat |<172>
iṣṭaṃ sapratiyogitvaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhibhiḥ ||

5,3.98

tadātmanā ca bādhyatvaṃ grāhyāntaratayāpi ca |
bādhakaiś cāpy anekāntaḥ, tadanyatve ca pūrvavat ||

5,3.99

mithyādhīpratiyogitvaṃ svapnādāv iva te bhavet |
rāgādikṣayayogitvanimittādhigatis tathā ||

5,3.100

yāvān viśeṣa iṣṭaś cet sarvābhāvād viruddhatā |
mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmbādhabuddhivat ||

5,3.101

vācyo 'numānabādho vā yadi vā pratisādhanam |
pūrvasādhanadoṣāś ca sandheyāḥ, tasya cādhunā ||

5,3.102

sādhyābhedād avācyatvād hetor nobhayasiddhatā |
pratyayatvaṃ ca, <173>
sāmānyaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ na vidyate ||

5,3.103

bhavato 'tyantabhinnaṃ ca matpakṣe 'pi kathañ cana |
sārūpyānyanivṛttī ca netyetat sādhayiṣyate ||

5,3.104

tasmād dhetur na sāmānyam asti siddhaṃ dvayor api |
viśeṣayoś ca hetutvaṃ pakṣatattulyasaṃsthayoḥ ||

5,3.105

na syād anvayahīnatvād ataddharmatayāpi ca |
na cārthahīnā tadbuddhir hetutvena bhaviṣyati ||

5,3.106

āśrayāsiddhitā coktā viśeṣyasyāprasiddhitaḥ |
tathā hetor viruddhatvaṃ dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||

5,3.107

viśeṣaṇāprasiddhatvavikalpenaiva bodhite |
svapnādipratyaye bāhyaṃ sarvathā na hi neṣyate ||

5,3.108

sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam |<174>
janmany ekatra bhinne vā tathā kālāntare 'pi vā ||

5,3.109

taddeśo vānyadeśo vā svapnajñānasya gocaraḥ |
alātacakre 'lātaṃ syāc chīghrabhramaṇasaṃskṛtam ||

5,3.110

gandharvanagare 'bhrāṇi pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ gṛhādi ca |
pūrvānubhūtatoyaṃ ca raśmitaptoṣaraṃ tathā ||

5,3.111

mṛgatoyasya vijñāne kāraṇatvena kalpyate |
dravyāntare viṣāṇaṃ ca śaśasyātmā ca kāraṇam ||

5,3.112

śaśaśṛṅgadhiyaḥ, mauṇḍyaṃ niṣedhe śiraso 'sya ca |
vastvantarair asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatādhiyaḥ ||<175>

5,3.113

kāraṇatvaṃ padārthānām asadvākyārthakalpane |
atyantānanubhūto 'pi baddhyā yo 'rthaḥ prakalpyate ||

5,3.114

tasyotpattau kathañ cit syuḥ pṛthivyādīni kāraṇam |
eṣa pratyakṣadharmaś ca vartamānārthataiva yā ||

5,3.115

sannikṛṣṭārthavṛttiś ca na tu jñānāntareṣv iyam |
katham utpādayej jñānaṃ tatrāsaṃścet, kuto nviyam ||

5,3.116

arthasyāvidyamānasya vijñānotpattyaśaktatā |
bāhyālambanatāyāṃ nau vivādo 'rthasya saṃnidhiḥ ||

5,3.117

yadi nāsti, kim evaṃ syād asmatpakṣanivartanam |
tasmād yadanyathāsantam anyathā pratipadyate ||

5,3.118

tannirālambanaṃ jñānam, <176>
abhāvālambanaṃ ca tat |
bhāvāntaram abhāvo 'nyo na kaś cid anirūpaṇāt ||

5,3.119

bhavatā dvayamatyetad durnirūpaṃ sahetukam |
pratijñādoṣavac cāpi yojyā hetor viruddhatā ||

5,3.120

samastavyastadharmādisvarūpādiviparyayāt |<177>
dṛṣṭāntadoṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ, na hy ekavastuni ||

5,3.121

tava sādhyāṃśahetvaṃśavyāptadharmādisambhavaḥ |
ke cid vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto nāstīty apy anuyuñjate ||

5,3.122

tadabhāvād avṛtteś ca nāsty atrāvasaras tava |
vidhirūpapratijñāyām etad vaktuṃ hi śakyate ||

5,3.123

tatrāvastuvipakṣe 'pi prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ |
yasminn anityatā nāsti kāryatāpi na vidyate ||

5,3.124

tasmin, yathā khapuṣpādāv iti śakyaṃ hi bhāṣitum |
atra tv avastusādhyatvaṃ vastunaś ca vipakṣatā ||

5,3.125

tena syād vyatireko 'sya vācyaḥ, <178>
yaś cāpi darśayet |
pratiṣedhadvayāt tena vidhir eva pradarśitaḥ ||

5,3.126

na ca śakyo vidhir vaktuṃ vastuny asati kena cit |
evaṃ sthite ca sarvajñaniṣedhādāv iyaṃ gatiḥ ||

5,3.127

pratyakṣāder asāmarthyaṃ tadīyasyāsmadādivat |
vaidharmyāsambhave 'py etadanye tv āhur adūṣaṇam ||

5,3.128

vinaiva tatprayogeṇa hetur aikāntiko yataḥ |
sarvathā sadupāyānāṃ vādamārgaḥ pravartate ||

5,3.129

adhikāro 'nupāyatvān na vāde śūnyavādinaḥ |
nanu sarvaṃ bhavatsiddhaṃ mayedaṃ sādhanaṃ kṛtam ||

5,3.130

kimarthaṃ tadasiddhyā tvaṃ vikalpyātrātthadūṣaṇam |
vipralipsur ivāhaivaṃ kimarthaṃ nyāyavid bhavān ||<179>

5,3.131

nāśrauṣīḥ sādhanatvaṃ kiṃ prasiddhasya dvayor api |
yo 'pi tāvat parāsiddhaḥ svayaṃ siddho 'bhidhīyate ||

5,3.132

bhavet tatra pratīkāraḥ svato 'siddhe tu kā kriyā |
taṃ sādhayan virundhyād dhi pūrvābhyupagataṃ naraḥ ||

5,3.133

asādhite tu sādhyo 'rtho na tena pratipadyate |
parāsiddho na paryāptaḥ pareṣāṃ pratipattaye ||

5,3.134

tenāsādhanatā yuktā, svato 'siddhe tu kiṅkṛtā |
dvayoḥ siddhasya hetutvaṃ nādṛṣṭāyopadiśyate ||

5,3.135

pratyeṣyanti svasiddhena sādhanena svayaṃ yataḥ |
vadet katham asiddhaṃ cet, ityanenāpi kiṃ tava ||

5,3.136

gṛhītam agṛhītaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā sādhanāpi vā |
mayocyate cet tv asiddhaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na pratipadyase ||

5,3.137

yatra syāt puruṣādhīnā buddhis tatredam ucyate |
kuto 'sya pūrvavijñānam ityatretanna yujyate ||<180>

5,3.138

yadi caivaṃ bhaved atra pratijñāmātra eva hi |
maddoṣājñānamātreṇa pratipattir bhavet tava ||

5,3.139

yatas tu sādhanāpekṣā tenāsyaiva pramāṇatā |
tatsmṛtyutpattimātre tu vākyavyāpāra iṣyate ||

5,3.140

tasmād yathaiva sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanāt |
sādhyaṃ gṛhṇan na vaktāram apekṣeta tathā bhavān ||

5,3.141

yac cāpi bhavato jñānaṃ pratyakādiḥ kim atra te |
matprasiddhāsti yuktir vā sādhyaṃ vātra yathecchasi ||

5,3.142

tasmān na viduṣām etaduttaṃ yujyate yataḥ |
tava hetur asiddho 'yaṃ mama tena na sādhanam ||

5,3.143

satyaṃ yadi mamaivātra pratipattiḥ phalaṃ bhavet |
tadā tvadaprasiddhe 'pi hetau māṃ prati hetutā ||

5,3.144

yadā tu jñānamātratvapratipattau bhavān mayā |
pṛṣṭaḥ ko hetur atreti tadaivaṃ nopapadyate ||

5,3.145

svayaṃ na hy agṛhītena matprasiddhena vā bhavān |
hetunā sādhyam etat tu pratipannaḥ kathañ cana ||<181>

5,3.146

na ca vyāpriyate 'nyatra vacanaṃ prāśnikān prati |
svaniścayāya yo hetus tasyaiva pratipādanāt ||

5,3.147

matprasiddhatvam etasya kutaś cāvagataṃ tvayā |
kathaṃ cetthaṃ vivakṣā te svayam artham ajānataḥ ||

5,3.148

mayi jijñāsamāne 'pi buddhipūrvābhidhāyinaḥ |
iti jñātvā ca vo vṛddhair bhāṣitobhayasiddhatā ||

5,3.149

tena yadvanmamaitena tvamadhitsasi hetunā |
sādhyajñānam, tathaivāham ajñānaṃ tava dūṣaṇaiḥ ||

5,3.150

yathaiva ca bhavānīdṛk sādhyam uktvāsya sādhanam |
sādhyānurūpam ajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt ||

5,3.151

tathaiva pratipādyo 'pi tādṛksādhyabubhutsayā |
manvānaḥ sādhanaṃ duṣṭaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ na budhyate ||

5,3.152

saṃvittyā sādhanaṃ matvā tatsadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite |
sādhyasyāsambhavād eva tvaduktaṃ nāvabudhyate ||

5,3.153

tenāśeyaṃ na kartavyā mohād api mayerite |
sādhane sādhanaṃ jñātvā para evāvabhotsyate ||<182>

5,3.154

vispaṣṭaś cākṣapādokto virodho hetusādhyayoḥ |
yamadṛṣṭvā parair uktam adūṣaṇam idaṃ kila ||

5,3.155

nanu lokaprasiddhena pūrvam etena hetunā |
sādhyasiddhir mamāpy āsīt paramārtho 'sya nāstitā ||

5,3.156

yo 'dhunā paramārthena nāstītyevaṃ prakāśate |
kathaṃ pūrvam asāv āsīd asaṃścet sādhanaṃ katham ||

5,3.157

sādhanaṃ ced avaśyaṃ ca paramārthāstitā bhavet |
siddhir nāparamārthena paramārthasya yujyate ||

5,3.158

na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅgādeḥ samyagjñānādihetutā |<183>
bāṣpādināpy adhūmena mithyā vahnyādibodhanam ||

5,3.159

tasmād asatyahetor yā paramārthe matis tava |
sāpy asatyā na satyaṃ hi satyābhāsena gamyate ||

5,3.160

ye 'pi rekhādayo dṛṣṭā varṇānāṃ pratipādakāḥ |
na te svenāpi rūpeṇa paramārthatvavarjitāḥ ||

5,3.161

varṇātmanā na satyāś cet, sarvabhāveṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ |
padārthāntararūpeṇa na satyaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate ||

5,3.162

svarūpe vidyamāne tu yad apy evaṃ prakāśate |
svarūpābhāvakḷptau tu na satyaṃ nāpy asatyatā ||

5,3.163

hetvādīnāṃ tu bhavataḥ svarūpeṇāpy asatyatā |
tena bāṣpādivat teṣām upāyatvam, na lekhyavat ||<184>

5,3.164

upāyānāṃ svarūpaṃ hi saṃvṛttyātmakam eva naḥ |
tathā ca satyateṣṭaiva svarūpāsatyatā katham ||

5,3.165

saṃvṛtyā yat svarūpaṃ hi tadvāṅmātranibandhanam |
hetutvaṃ paramārthasya pratipattuṃ na śaknuyāt ||

5,3.166

paramāthāc ca lokasya na bhede hetur asti te |
laukikopāyagamyasya kena syāt paramārthatā ||

5,3.167

nanv asty api bāhye 'rthe buddhyārūḍhe na sidhyati |
vāsanāśabdabhedotthavikalpapravibhāgataḥ ||

5,3.168

nyāyavidbhir idaṃ coktaṃ dharmādau buddhim āśrite |
vyavahāro 'numānādeḥ kalpyate na bahiḥsthite ||<185>

5,3.169

astīdaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām idaṃ tatra parīkṣyatām |
bhedo 'sataḥ kathaṃ hi syād buddhiśabdayoḥ ||

5,3.170

nirvastuke kathañ cin nu prasavo buddhiśabdayoḥ |
śabdabhedo 'pi bhavatas tadabhāvān na sidhyati ||

5,3.171

yadi vā vidyamāno 'pi bhedo buddhiprakalpitaḥ |
sādhyasādhanadharmāder vyavahārāya kalpyate ||

5,3.172

tato bhavatprayukte 'smin sādhane yāvad ucyate |
sarvatrotpadyate buddhir iti dūṣaṇatā bhavet ||

5,3.173

yaś ca mantras tv ayokto 'yaṃ dharmyādau buddhim āśrite |
na bāhyāpekṣayā sa syād asiddhyādau mayerite ||

5,3.174

buddhiprakḷptisidhiś ca bhavatāṃ vyavahāriṇam |
maduktaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ siddhaṃ tvaduktaṃ tu na sādhanam ||

5,3.175

bāhyārthavyavahāritvāj jñānotpāde sthite 'pi naḥ |
kathañ cin na hi kalpyeta vyavahāro 'rthavarjitaḥ ||

5,3.176

nanu yadvanmayā hetur neṣyate dūṣaṇaṃ tathā |
tena me dūṣaṇābhāvād aduṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavet ||<186>

5,3.177

nedānīṃ dūṣaṇaiḥ kāryam, sādhanābhāvato yadi |
tvayaivāsmadabhipretā svapakṣāsiddhir āśritā ||

5,3.178

na cāsti vāsanābhedo nimittāsambhavāt tava |
jñānabhedo nimittaṃ cet, tasya bhedaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ ||

5,3.179

vāsanābhedataś cet syāt, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
svacchasya jñānarūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svato 'sti te ||

5,3.180

pramāṇaṃ vāsanāstitve bhede vāpi na vidyate |
kuryād grāhakabhedaṃ sā grāhyabhedas tu kiṅkutaḥ ||

5,3.181

saṃvittyā jāyamānā hi smṛtimātraṃ karoty asau |
kṣaṇikeṣu ca cit teṣu vināśe ca niranvaye ||

5,3.182

vāsyavāsakayoś caivam asāhityān na vāsanā |
pūrvakṣaṇair anutpanno vāsyate nottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||

5,3.183

uttareṇa vinaṣṭatvān na ca pūrvasya vāsanā |<187>
sāhitye 'pi tayor naiva sambandho 'stīty avāsanā ||

5,3.184

kṣaṇikatvād dvyasyāpi vyāpāro na parasparam |
vinaśyac ca kathaṃ vastu vāsyate 'nyena naśyatā ||

5,3.185

avasthitā hi vāsyante bhāvābhāvair avasthitaiḥ |
avasthito hi pūrvasmād bhidyate nottaro yadi ||

5,3.186

pūrvavad vāsanā tatra na syād evāviśeṣataḥ |
bhaṅgure pūrvasādṛśyād bhinnatvāc cāsti vāsanā ||<188>

5,3.187

naitad asty anurūpaṃ tu kṣaṇikatve dhiyāṃ tava |
pūrvajñānaṃ tv anutpannaṃ kāryaṃ nārabhate kvacit ||

5,3.188

na vinaṣṭaṃ, na tasyāsti niṣpannasya kṣaṇaṃ sthitiḥ |
tenotpannavinaṣṭatvān nāsty ārambhakṣaṇo 'pi hi ||

5,3.189

niranvayavinaṣṭatvād ānurūpyaṃ kutaḥ punaḥ |
na tadīyosti kaś cic ca dharma uttarabuddhiṣu ||

5,3.190

samānadharmatāṃ muktvā nānurūpyaṃ ca vidyate |
yadi syād ānurūpyāc ca vāsanā godhiyo yadā ||

5,3.191

hastibuddhir bhavet tatra vailakṣaṇyān na vāsanā |
tataḥ paraṃ ca gojñānaṃ nirmūlatvān na sambhavet ||

5,3.192

sarvaṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ na syād eva vilakṣaṇāt |<189>
bāhyārthānugrahābhāvāt pārārthyenāvaśīkṛtāḥ ||

5,3.193

niranvayavināśinyaḥ kuryuḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ kramāt |
vināśe kāraṇasyeṣṭaḥ kāryārambhaś ca nānyathā ||

5,3.194

tataiva jñānanāśena vinaṣṭāḥ sarvavāsanāḥ |
tena sarvābhya etābhyaḥ sarvākāraṃ yadutthitam ||

5,3.195

jñānam ekakṣaṇenaiva vināśaṃ gantum arhati |
yady āśrayavināśe 'pi śaktyanāśo 'bhyupeyate ||

5,3.196

kṣaṇikatvaṃ ca hīyeta na cārambho 'nyathā bhavet |
vāsanānāṃ pravāho 'pi yadi jñānapravāhavat ||<190>

5,3.197

vāsanātas tato jñānaṃ na syāt tasmāc ca vāsanā |
kuryātāṃ tulyam evaite nānyonyaṃ tu kadā cana ||

5,3.198

nānyo vilakṣaṇo hetur yenānyādṛk phalaṃ bhavet |
tasmāt saṃvṛtisatyaiṣā kalpitā nāsti tattvataḥ ||

5,3.199

na cedṛśena bhavena kāryam utpadyate kva cit |
yasya tv avasthito jñātā jñānābhyāsena yujyate ||

5,3.200

sa tasya vāsanādhāro vāsanāpi sa eva vā |
kusume bījapūrāder yallākṣādyupasicyate |<191>
tadrūpasyaiva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya, ity avāsanā ||

5,3.201

yuktyānupetām asatīṃ prakalpya yadvāsanām arthanirākriyeyam ||
āsthānivṛttyarthamavādi bauddhair grāhaṃ gatās tatra kathañ cid anye ||

{5,4 śunyavāda SNV}

5,4.1

evam ukte 'numānasya jñānam āśritya dūṣaṇe |
jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||

5,4.2

yat tāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate |
dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||

5,4.3

pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite |
atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||

5,4.4

tad yady etena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |
tvaduktaṃ sarvam ātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||<192>

5,4.5

tatra tāvad idaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api |
grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||

5,4.6

na cāpy ākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā |
na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||

5,4.7

gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam |
tasmād ākāravad vastu grāhyatvād vidyate dhruvam ||

5,4.8

ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānam ākāravad yadi |
tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāsty arthakalpanā ||

5,4.9

yadi vākāravattā syād bāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ |
tad asti gṛhyamāṇatvāt tatsiddhaivāsti dhīr api ||

5,4.10

kiṃ tāvad atra yuktaṃ syāj jñānam ākāravat, <193>
kutaḥ |
ekam ākāravad vastu grāhyam ity adhyagīṣmahi ||

5,4.11

tad yady ākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyate tasya ca |
grāhyatvam anyathā na syād iti grāhakakalpanā ||

5,4.12

tenākāravataḥ kḷptād grāhyād ākāravarjitam |
vastvantaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syād grāhakaṃ niṣpramāṇakam ||

5,4.13

tasyākalpanam icchaṃś ced arthe grāhakatāṃ vadeḥ |
saṃjñāmātre visaṃvadaḥ sidddhā tv ekārthakalpanā ||

5,4.14

grāhyagrāhakayor aikyaṃ sarvathā pratipādyate |
bāhyābhyantararūpaś ca parikalpyo mṛṣeṣyate ||<194>

5,4.15

matpakṣe yady api svaccho jñānātmā paramārthataḥ |
tathāpy anādau saṃsāre pūrvajñānaprasūtibhiḥ ||

5,4.16

citrābhiś citrahetutvād vāsanābhir upaplavāt |
svānurūpyeṇa nīlādi grāhyagrāhakarūṣitam ||

5,4.17

pravibhaktam ivotpannaṃ nānyam artham apekṣate |
anyonyahetutā caiva jñānaśaktyor anādikā ||

5,4.18

anekakalpanāyāś ca jyāyasī hy ekakalpanā |
śaktimātrasya bhedaś ca vastubhedād viśiṣyate ||<195>

5,4.19

tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāj jñānasyākārakalpanā |
jyāyasī, bhavatas tv arthaṃ kalpayitvā bhaved iyam ||

5,4.20

tadasiddhāvaśaktatvāt, tenaivaṃ viprakṛṣṭatā |
pratyāsannaṃ ca, <196>
sambaddhaṃ grāhyaṃ mama bhaviṣyati ||

5,4.21

itaś cākāravajjñānam, yasmāt tadvat prakāśakam |
svayamprakāśahīnasya bāhyasyopāsanaṃ matam ||<197>

5,4.22

na cāgrhīte jñānākhye prakāśyo 'rtho 'vadhāryate |
tadadhīnaprakāśatvād dīpābhāse yathā ghaṭaḥ ||

5,4.23

utpanneṣv api cārtheṣu prakāśābhāvataḥ kva cit |
pratibandhakayogād vā saṃvittir nopajāyate ||

5,4.24

jñānasyotpadyamānasya pratibandho na kaś cana |
na cāprakāśarūpatvaṃ yenāsyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ||

5,4.25

prāk cārthagrahaṇādiṣṭā tasyotpattis tadaiva ca |
saṃvedanaṃ bhaved asya, na cet kālāntare 'pi na ||

5,4.26

kiṃ hi tasya bhaved ūrdhvaṃ prāk ca nāsīn na yena tat |
pūrvaṃ gṛhītaṃ paścāt ca gṛhītam iti bhāṣyate ||

5,4.27

jñānāntarasya cotpattiṃ prakāśo na pratīkṣate |
tasya tasyāpi cānyena saṃvittāvasthitir bhavet ||<198>

5,4.28

jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvam arthābhāve 'pi |
parāmarśo 'rthorūpasya sa kathaṃ vopapadyate ||

5,4.29

tadrūpamārthamālikhya yadi dhīrnopajāyate |
bhūtakāle ca yadyarthas tatpūrvaṃ nopalakṣitaḥ ||

5,4.30

vaktāraś cāpi dṛśyante varttamānārthabuddhiṣu |
nīlo 'rtho 'yaṃ yato me 'tra tadrūpā jāyate matiḥ ||

5,4.31

tasmāt pūrvagṛhītāsu buddhiṣv arthopalmbhanam |
na copalabdhir astīhi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu ||

5,4.32

vivekabuddhyabhāvāc ca, sākārasya ca darśanāt |
ākāravattayā bodho jñānasyaiva prasajyate ||

5,4.33

na hy evaṃ kalpanā śakyā nirākārād ito matiḥ |
gṛhyate 'rthas tataḥ paścāt sākāraḥ sampratīyate ||<199>

5,4.34

ākāravattvabhedo hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum |
prāgbuddhigrahaṇād arthe saṃvittir neti sādhitam ||

5,4.35

na cārthākāra evāyaṃ jñānārūḍhaḥ pratīyate |
na hi so 'ntaḥpraveśāya paryāpto nārthahānaye ||

5,4.36

itthambhāve pramāṇaṃ ca tasya vaktuṃ na śakyate |
tadīyapratibimbatvam etasmād eva neṣyate ||

5,4.37

niścandre bimbarūpaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ yena divā jalam |
sa rātrau khe ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimbatām ||

5,4.38

vijñāne na kadā cit tu prāṅ nirākāradarśanam |
bāhye vākāravattādhīr yenaivaṃ kalpanā bhavet ||

5,4.39

śabdagandharasānāṃ ca kīdṛśī pratibimbatā |
jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya kathaṃ syād arthadharmatā ||

5,4.40

bāhyābhyantaradeśatvān na cārthajñānayor mithaḥ |
samparko 'sti yato mohādavivekamatir bhavet ||<200>

5,4.41

asammūḍhasya cādṛṣṭe na sammohaprakalpanā |
kalpyamāne 'tha vāpy evaṃ tad dvayor avatiṣṭhate ||

5,4.42

saṃsargadhama ākāras tasmād eva na yujyate |
deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, mūrāmūrtatayā tathā ||

5,4.43

tailokyena prasaṅgāc ca saṃsargo naikakālatā |
na cāpy ārjavataḥ sthānaṃ jñāne nārthasya vidyate ||

5,4.44

sarvathā kalpanāyāṃ ca cakṣuṣāpi rasādayaḥ |
gṛhyeran sarvabhāvānāmaṇvākārāś ca tadgatāḥ ||

5,4.45

na cāpi viṣayatvena sthāne saṃsargakalpanā |
viṣayatvaṃ hi kīdṛk syāt prāgākāropalambhanāt ||<201>

5,4.46

na hy asañcetito bhāvo viṣayatvena kalpyate |
viṣayatvāt tadākāra ākārād viṣayaś ca saḥ ||

5,4.47

dvayor ākāranirmuktaṃ sattvaṃ saṃsṛṣṭatā tathā |
svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktum ityādi yujyate ||

5,4.48

na cāpy asyeha sadbhāvaḥ prāg gṛhīto na copari |
na hy ākāravinirmuktaṃ grāhyam astīti bhāṣitam ||

5,4.49

tasmād arthena saṃsargo niṣpramāṇaka eva te |
jñānavaicitryasiddhyarthaṃ na cāstyarthasya kalpanā ||

5,4.50

tadadhīnaṃ hi vaicitryaṃ kva dṛṣṭaṃ yena kalpyate |
nirākāreṇa cotpattir vaicitryākārayoḥ katham ||<202>

5,4.51

nirākārāc ca viṣayād buddhyākāro 'tivismayaḥ |
smṛtisvapnādibodhe ca syād anākāratā tava ||

5,4.52

na hi tatrārthasaṃsargaḥ kevalā vāsanaiva tu |
hetutvenopapanneti saiva jāgraddhiyām api ||

5,4.53

anvayavyatirekābhyām evaṃ jñānasya gamyate |
na hi bāhyasya jñānāpeto nidarśyate ||

5,4.54

bāhyāpeto mayā yadvat, <203>
tasmāt saṃsargavāgiyam |
nirākāre 'pi vijñāne vāsanāsv eva yujyate ||

5,4.55

dvayor apy eka ākāra ityetasyāpramāṇatā |
deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, dvayoś cānavadhāraṇāt ||

5,4.56

evam evārthabuddhyoḥ syāt sādṛśyān nāvibhaktatā |
bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyaṃ nājñāte syāt khapuṣpavat ||

5,4.57

tathā dvicandramāyādāv anyathārthe vyavasthite |
yā syād ākārasaṃvittir nāsāv arthanibandhanā ||

5,4.58

nakṣatraṃ tārakā tiṣyo dārā ityevamādiṣu |
naikatrārthe viruddhatvāl liṅgānekatvasambhavaḥ ||<204>

5,4.59

parivrāṭkāmukaśunāṃ kuṇapādimatis tathā |
dīrghahrasvatvabuddhiś ca hy ekasminn apy apekṣayā ||

5,4.60

ghaṭatvāt pārthavadravyaprameyādimatis tathā |
yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca na syād aikātmyavattayā ||

5,4.61

nārthe hy ekatra yugapad viruddhākārasambhavaḥ |
pratyayānāṃ tu bhinnatvād bhavec chaktyanusārataḥ ||

5,4.62

nirapekṣaṃ svarūpeṇa tasmāj jñānaṃ yadākṛti |
tathārtho na yathārthaṃ tu jñānam utpadyate kva cit ||

5,4.63

itthaṃ vijñānatantratve ko nv arthaṃ kalpayiṣyati |
dhīranāropitākārā svātmany evopayokṣyate ||<205>

5,4.64

naitad asti, tvayaikaṃ hi grāhyaṃ grāhakam iṣyate |
na caikasyaivam ātmatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ kaścid asti te ||

5,4.65

agnyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ prasiddhā ye prakāśakāḥ |
na te prakāśyarūpā hi prakāśasya, anapekṣaṇāt ||

5,4.66

grāhyatvaṃ tu yadā teṣāṃ tadākṣaṃ grāhakaṃ matam |
akṣagrahaṇakāle tu grāhikā dhīr bhaviṣyati ||

5,4.67

tasyāṃ tu gṛhyamāṇāyām anyā dhīr grāhikeṣyate |<206>
nanv ātmā grāhako grāhyo bhavatābhyupagamyate ||

5,4.68

kathañcid dharmarūpeṇa bhinnatvāt pratyayasya tat |
grāhakatvaṃ bhavet tatra grāhyaṃ dravyādi cātmanaḥ ||

5,4.69

yas tu nātyantabhedo 'tra kva vāsāv iṣyate mayā |
pratyāsattinimittā tu pratyagātmapravarttitā ||

5,4.70

asmatprayogasambhinnā jñānasyaiva tu kartari |
bhavantī tatra saṃvittir yujyetāpy ātmakartṛkā ||

5,4.71

na cātra karaṇajñānagrāhakākāravedanam |
grāhyatvaṃ yena buddheḥ syād abhinnatve 'pi pūrvavat ||<207>

5,4.72

anyarūpāpi saṃvittir yady anyaviṣayeṣyate |
jñānākārāpi saṃvittiḥ kasmān nārthasya kalpyate ||

5,4.73

abhinnatvaṃ yadā ceṣṭaṃ grāhyagrāhakavastunoḥ |
tadānyatarasaṃvittau dvyākāraṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ||

5,4.74

yadā tu grāhyam ākāraṃ nīlādi pratipadyate |
na tadā grāhakākārā saṃvittir dṛśyate kva cit ||

5,4.75

tasmād abhinnatā cet syāt tasyāpy anubhavo bhavet |
grāhyo vā nānubhūyeta grāhakānanubhūtivat ||

5,4.76

grāhakagrahaṇe 'py evaṃ grāhyasaṃvedanaṃ bhavet |
śuddham eva nirākāraṃ grāhakaṃ saṃvidasti hi ||

5,4.77

grāhyād abhinnatāyā ca sā saṃvittir na yujyate |
grāhako vā na gṛhyeta tadgrāhyānanubhūtivat ||

5,4.78

yathāvad grāhyasaṃvittau grāhakagrahaṇe 'pi vā |
grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittir nāsty eva syād dvayor api ||<208>

5,4.79

sa bahirdeśasambaddhaḥ ity anena nirūpyate |
grāhyākārasya saṃvittir grāhakānubhavād ṛte ||

5,4.80

paraṃ prati hi sādhyatvad arthasyākārasiddhaye |
bahirdeśena sambandho na hetutvāya kalpate ||

5,4.81

tasmād bahir itīhedaṃ niṣkṛṣṭaṃ grāhakāṃśataḥ |
saṃvedyaṃ nīlapītādi pratyakṣāder udāhṛtam ||

5,4.82

na pūrvaṃ jñāyate buddhir ityatraitad vadiṣyate |
grāhakasyaiva saṃvittir lakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit ||

5,4.83

na smarāmi mayā ko 'pi gṛhīto 'rthas tadeti hi |
smaranti grāhakotpādagrāhyarūpavivarjitam ||

5,4.84

tasmād abhinnatāyāṃ ca grāhye 'pi smaraṇaṃ bhavet |
grāhakasmṛtinirbhāsāt tatrāpy eṣaiva gṛhyate ||

5,4.85

tadatyantāvinābhāvān naikākāraṃ hi jāyate |<209>
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ siddhaivaṃ bhinnatā tayoḥ ||

5,4.86

grāhyāṃśo grāhakāṃśena gṛhyate, grāhakaḥ punaḥ |
gṛhyeteti na vaktavyam, grāhakāntaravarjanāt ||

5,4.87

grāhyāṃśenāpy aśaktatvān na tasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
grāhakatvena caitasya hīyetaiva dvirūpatā ||

5,4.88

grāhake gṛhyamāṇe ca grāhyamātraprasañjanam |
na syād ākāra ekaś ced itarasyāpi nāstitā ||

5,4.89

udbhavābhibhavābhyāṃ ca grāhyāgrāhyatvadarśanam |
yathā dīpaprabhādīnāṃ rūpamātropalambhanam ||

5,4.90

divā cāgneḥ samīpasthaiḥ sparśa evopalabhyate |
gandhavad dravyavṛttau ca gandhasyaivopalambhanam ||

5,4.91

na guṇāntarasaṃvittir yathātrābhibhavāt, tathā |
nākārāntarasaṃvittir grāhyagrāhakabuddhiṣu ||<210>

5,4.92

grāhyād ananyabhūto 'pi kaś cin naivopalabhyate |
nityānityādayo dharmāḥ śabdādigrahaṇe yathā ||

5,4.93

abhedaṃ vābhyupetyāyaṃ prasaṅgo yadi gīyate |
ekasmin gṛhyamāṇe 'śe na gṛhyetāparaḥ katham ||

5,4.94

tasmād yat syād yadā yogyaṃ tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ tadā |
dvayaṃ ca tvadupanyastaṃ śaktyabhāvān na gṛhyate ||

5,4.95

kuto 'yam ekavastutve yogyāyogyatvasambhavaḥ |
udbhavābhibhavātmatvaṃ kathaṃ caikasya kalpitam ||

5,4.96

ekāṃśābhibhave ca syād itarābhibhavo 'pi te |
tathā tasyābhibhūtatvād grāhyatvaṃ na ca yujyate ||

5,4.97

ayogyatā vikalpyaivam, dṛṣṭāntā ye 'tra kīrtitāḥ |
rūpādibhedāt tatra syād udbhavābhibhavādyapi ||

5,4.98

yadāpy ekāntato bhedo rūpāder na parasparam |
tadāpi dravyarūpasya pariṇāmas tathā tathā ||<211>

5,4.99

abhinnatve 'pi na grāhyam iti yac cābravīd bhavān |
kṛtakatvādidharmāṇāṃ dhībhede 'nanyatā katham ||

5,4.100

na hy anyatpratyayād asti bhinnād grāhyasya bhedakam |
na ceyattaiva bhedasya deśato mūrtito 'pi vā ||

5,4.101

kāraṇānāṃ hi sambandhaḥ kāryaiḥ kṛtakocyate |
vibhāgo 'vayavānāṃ ca bhavet kva cid anityatā ||

5,4.102

buddhyāder ātmarūpādisthānaṃ nāśitvam ucyate |
nityatvaṃ sarvadā sattā, vastutvaṃ saiva kīrtyate ||

5,4.103

pramāṇajñānasambandhaḥ prameyajñeyatocyate |<212>
sarvatra cātra bhinnatvam asti kena cid ātmanā ||

5,4.104

tasmād yathaiva rūpāder deśabhedādibhir vinā |
buddhibhedena bhedo 'sti tathaivātra pratīyatām ||

5,4.105

atyantabhinnatāsmābhir naiva kasya cid iṣyate |
sarvaṃ hi vasturūpeṇa bhidyate na parasparam ||

5,4.106

sarvaṃ ca kṛtakatvādi kriyāhetvādyapekṣayā |
gṛhyate tadasaṃvittāvabhede 'pi na gṛhyate ||

5,4.107

jñāne naivaṃvidho bhedo nāpekṣānyatra vidyate |
paraspareṇa cāpekṣā syāc cet, sannihitaś ca saḥ ||

5,4.108

nanu grāhakam ityevaṃ grāhyam ity api vā matiḥ |
nīlādigrahaṇe nāstīty apekṣā katham ucyate ||<213>

5,4.109

mā bhūd evaṃ tathāpy atra dvyākāre grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
evaṃ cāgṛhyamāṇe vā jñāne dvyākāratā katham ||

5,4.110

uttarottaravijñānaviśeṣād yā prakalpyate |
grāhakākārasaṃvittiḥ smaraṇāc cānumānikī ||

5,4.111

ekākāraṃ kila jñānaṃ prathamaṃ yadi kalpyate |
tatas tadviṣayāpy anyā tadrūpaiva matir bhavet ||

5,4.112

ghaṭavijñānatajjñānaviśeṣo 'to na sidhyati |
grāhakākārasaṃvittau tv ākārapracayo bhavet ||

5,4.113

jāyate pūrvavijñānaṃ dvyākāraṃ yatra tat punaḥ |
tasyātmīyaś ca pūrvau ca viṣayasthāvupaplutau ||<214>

5,4.114

preṣv ākāravṛddhyaivaṃ pūrvebhyo bhinnatā, tathā |
grāhyavat smaraṇāt paścāt saṃvittau grāhakaḥ purā ||

5,4.115

na tāvad evamākārān paśyāmaḥ pracayānvitān |
viṣayavyapadeśāc ca narte jñānanirūpaṇam ||

5,4.116

tasmāj jñānātmanaikatve grāhyabhedanibandhaḥ |
saṃvittibhedaḥ siddho 'tra kimākārāntareṇa naḥ ||

5,4.117

nirākāratasāmye 'pi yathākāravatāṃ dhruvam |
bhedaḥ svābhāvikas tadvajjñānānāṃ kiṃ na sidhyati ||<215>

5,4.118

smṛter uttarakālaṃ cetyetanmithyaiva gīyate |
tadaiva hy asya saṃvittir arthāpattyopajāyate ||

5,4.119

gṛhītam eva yac coktaṃ tadabhedāt, na tad, yataḥ |
nāsmabhir vākyavṛttes tvaṃ nimittam anuyujyase ||

5,4.120

grāhyagrāhakataivāsya kena cin nopalabhyate |
pratyakṣajñānapakṣe ca naiṣā syād ānumānikī ||

5,4.121

ekākāre ca vijñāne yady anyo 'py atra kalpyate |
sahasrākārataikasya kasmān na parikalpyate ||

5,4.122

grāhyagrāhakayor bhedo nanv asty eva parasparam |
siddho naḥ pakṣa evaṃ syāt, <216>
na, jñānatvād abhedataḥ ||

5,4.123

bhinnābhinnatvam ekasya kuto 'tra parikalpitam |
tvayā sāṃkhyamatenaivam uktvā buddhasya śāsanam ||

5,4.124

ekaṃ ced grāhakaṃ grāhyaṃ kuto bhinnatvavāgiyam |
bhinnaṃ cet katham ucyeta tasyaikatvaṃ punas tvayā ||

5,4.125

ekajñānād ananyatvād grāhyagrāhakayor mithaḥ |
ekatvena bhavej jñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grākam eva vā ||

5,4.126

tatra cānyatarāpāye dvitīyāpāyataḥ punaḥ |
jñānasyāṃśadvayāsattvān naiḥsvābhāvyād abhāvatā ||

5,4.127

bhinnābhyāṃ vāpy abhinnatvād bhedo jñānātmano bhavet |
tatsvātmanaḥ, tataś caivaṃ siddhaṃ vastudvayaṃ hi naḥ ||

5,4.128

tayoś ca yadi saṃjñeyaṃ jñānam ity astv arthāpi vā |
jñānaṃ jñāyata ityartho dhīrbhāve karaṇe 'pi vā ||

5,4.129

sarvathā vastubhedo naḥ siddhaḥ śabdo yathāruci |
pravartatāṃ na nas tatra kācid vipratipannatā ||<217>

5,4.130

atha saty api bhinnatve grāhyaṃ jñānāntaraṃ bhavet |
jñānatve tasya kā yuktiḥ, pūrvoktā yadi seṣyate ||

5,4.131

jñānaṃ jñānam itīdaṃ tu na dvayor anuvartate |
vyatiriktaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ tvayā nābhyupagamyate ||

5,4.132

vyatireke tayor jñānān na jñānātmakatā bhavet |
tadrūparahitatve ca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||

5,4.133

tābhyāṃ ca tasya sambandhe pratyekaṃ vyatiṣajya ca |
bhedasāvayavatvādi doṣo vaiśeṣikādivat ||

5,4.134

yathā hi teṣāṃ jātyādau doṣā hy uktāḥ parair amī |
tathaivaiṣāṃ prasajyante bhinnābhinnārthasaṅgatau ||

5,4.135

tābhyām avyatireke vā bhedaḥ pūrvokta eva te |<218>
sādṛśyāpohasāmānyakalpanā vārayiṣyate ||

5,4.136

vastvantarasya cābhāvāt tvayāpoho 'pi duṣkaraḥ |
nājñānaṃ nāma kiñ cit syād apohyaṃ jñānavādinaḥ ||

5,4.137

apoho na hy abhāvasya kathañ cid upapadyate |
vastvantaram abhāvaḥ syād, apohyatvāc ca vastutā ||

5,4.138

tenājñānanivṛttau hi jñāne 'nyārtha prasajyate |
kalpitaṃ syād apohyaṃ cet, nātyantāsatyakalpanā ||

5,4.139

buddhir ajñānanirbhāsā tavājñānaṃ prakalitam |
tataś ca jñānam evaikam apohyatvena sammatam ||<219>

5,4.140

na cātmāpoha evāsti kva cit sāmānyakalpane |
vṛkṣasya na hy apohyatvaṃ vṛkṣeṇaiva kadā cana ||

5,4.141

apohye caiva vijñāne jñānatvaṃ na bhavet tava |
vṛkṣatvaṃ na hy apohyeṣu kalaśādiṣu yujyate ||

5,4.142

tataś cājñānam evārtha ity abhinnārthatā bhavet |
ajñānapratyayaś cāyaṃ kimālambana iṣyate ||

5,4.143

na tāvaj jñānanirmuktam ajñānaṃ grāhyam asti te |
na ca vastu niṣiddhaṃ tadabhāvaḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate ||

5,4.144

bhāvo na gṛhyate yena tasyābhāveṣu kā kathā |
svāṃśaparyavasānaṃ ca tulyam atrāpi kāraṇam ||

5,4.145

tena jñānāntaraṃ vā syād grāhyam ātmāṃśa eva vā |
svarūpaviparītaṃ ca kathaṃ grāhyaṃ pratīyate ||<220>

5,4.146

yathoṣṇe 'nuṣṇadhīr nāsti, jñāne 'py ajñānadhīs tathā |
tena na jñānamātratve syād apohyaṃ kathañ cana ||

5,4.147

grāhyagrāhakayoś cāto na jñānātmasamānatā |
tasmād anyataratredaṃ jñānatvaṃ sampratīyate ||

5,4.148

tatrāpy ubhayasiddhatvād grāhakasyeti gamyate |
vastubhede prasiddhe ca vyapadeśo yathāruci ||

5,4.149

jñānam astūbhayaṃ vārtho grāhako vārtha ucyatām |
buddhyor ayugapadbhāvān na dvayor mayamānatā ||

5,4.150

kṣaṇikā hītyanenoktam, <221>
artho hy ekaḥ prasajyate |
anyonyanirapekṣatvād yugapac cāpi janmani ||

5,4.151

mānameyatvāstitvam, kriyākārakavarjanāt |
arthavijñānayor atra yā mitiṃ prati saṅgatiḥ ||

5,4.152

kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'yam, nānyatraivaṃ ca dṛśyate |
niyamaś ca na labhyeta savyadakṣiṇaśṛṅgavat ||

5,4.153

idaṃ kāryam ayaṃ hetuḥ, dvayaṃ na, <222>
anyonyasaṃśrayāt |
tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ hetuḥ kair naiva varṇyate ||

5,4.154

paurvāparyavinirmuktaṃ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇam |
gavāśvasya yathā nāsti paurvāparye 'pi tat tathā ||

5,4.155

yugapajjāyamāne 'pi santatyantaraje kṣaṇe |
rūpādiṣu ghaṭe yadvat, tasmāt pūrvam avasthite ||

5,4.156

yo yasmāj jāyate paścāt sa tatkāryam itīṣyate |
hetuhetumatāṃ siddhaṃ yaugapadyanidarśanam ||

5,4.157

yat pradīpaprabhādyuktaṃ sūkṣamaḥ kālo 'sti tatra naḥ |
durlakṣas tu yathā vedhaḥ padmapattraśate tathā ||

5,4.158

bhāgayor yaugapadyena tathaiva syān nirākriyā |<223>
na ca śaktyarpaṇadvāraṃ krameṇālambanaṃ bhavet ||

5,4.159

grāhyaṃ tadā hy atītaṃ syāt, tadrūpyaṃ cāpramāṇakam |
atītvānuviddho hi smṛtyā grāhyo 'nubhūyate ||

5,4.160

tadvad eva bhaved atra, svapne na syāt, viparyayāt |
tatra hy avartamāno 'pi gṛhyate vartamānavat ||

5,4.161

bādhajñānād idaṃ bhrāntam, na tv atraivaṃ viparyayaḥ |
tasmāt pratyakṣabuddhīnāṃ nātito viṣayo bhavet ||

5,4.162

atītatvād yathaivāsāṃ vṛtto janmāntareṣu yaḥ |
tadrūpatvena vā jñānaṃ hetur bhāvivad ucyate ||<224>

5,4.163

atītatve 'pi nārtho 'yaṃ dhr eṣety atra kā pramā |
atītaṃ yac ca vijñānaṃ grāhyatvena prakalpitam ||

5,4.164

tasmād grāhakarūpaṃ vā grāhyaṃ vobhayathāpi vā |
grāhyākāratvamātre syād arthaḥ śabdāntareṇa te ||

5,4.165

svakāle cāpy asaṃvitter na syāc chaktyarpaṇaṃ tataḥ |
yathaivānāgatāj jñānāt santatyantarajād api ||

5,4.166

dṛḍhatvenāpy avijñātāt tathotpannād vinaśyataḥ |
kevalagrāhakatve tu viṣayatvaṃ na yujyate ||

5,4.167

kimapekṣya ca tasyedaṃ grāhakatvaṃ prakalpyate |
dvyākāratā nirastaiva, <225>
saṃvedyeta tadaiva ca ||

5,4.168

tataś cottaravijñānaṃ na pratīkṣeta bodhakam |
dvyākārakalpanāyāṃ ca parasyātmāṃśa eva te ||

5,4.169

pramāparyavasānena nātīto viṣayo bhavet |
pūrvagrāhyasarūpatve grāhakatvaṃ prahīyate ||

5,4.170

grāhakākāramātre syād viṣayo nāsarūpataḥ |
na ca śaktyarpaṇasyātra vyāpāra upalabhyate ||

5,4.171

śaktyarpaṇasya cābhāvo yuṣmatpakṣe prasādhitaḥ |
santānāntaravac caiṣāṃ niṣedhyā hetusādhyatā ||

5,4.172

vāsyavāsakabhāvaś ca jñānatvād ekasantatau |
tasmād yadbhāsakaṃ rūpaṃ tadgrāhyāt tasya bhinnatā ||

5,4.173

tatsaṃvittāv asaṃvitte rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |
grāhyaṃ tadgrāhakāc caiva tatparāmṛśatā yataḥ ||

5,4.174

na parāmṛśyate 'vaśyaṃ rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |<226>
dvayaṃ paraspareṇaivaṃ bhinnaṃ sādhyaṃ rasādivat ||

5,4.175

aikarūpyeṇa cājñānāt santānāntarabuddhivat |
jñānaṃ svāṃśaṃ na gṛhṇāti jñānotpatteḥ svaśaktivat ||

5,4.176

grāhyatvapratiṣedhaś ca dvayahīnā hi vāsate |
caitrajñānaṃ tadudbhūtajñānāṃśagrāhyabodhakam ||

5,4.177

jñānatvān na bhaved yadvat tasya dehāntarodbhavam |
etayaiva diśā vācyā śaktidvayanirākriyā ||

5,4.178

pramāṇāntarasiddhatvād anyatrānekaśaktitā |
na tv atra kāraṇaṃ tādṛk śaktibhedakṛdasti te ||<227>

5,4.179

tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāl lāghavād yaḥ parigrahaḥ |
upāyatvāc ca yat tasya pūrvagrahaṇakalpanam ||

5,4.180

cakṣuradīndriyair atra tadanaikāntikaṃ bhavet |
yad apy apratibaddhatvād utpattau gṛhyatām iti ||

5,4.181

tatrātmanā na śaktyaṃ tannānyotpattis tadasti vā |
tenaitat kāraṇābhāvāt tadānīṃ nānubhūyate ||

5,4.182

nānyathā hy arthasadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ sannupapadyate |
jñānaṃ cen netyataḥ paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate ||<228>

5,4.183

na cāpy apratibandhena kevalena graho bhavet |
viśiṣṭakāraṇābhāve 'py artho naivānubhūyate ||

5,4.184

vyāpṛtaṃ cārthasaṃvittau jñānaṃ nātmānamṛcchati |<229>
tena prakāśakatve 'pi bodhāyānyat pratīkṣyate ||

5,4.185

īdṛśaṃ vā prakāśatvaṃ tasyārthānubhavātmakam |
na cātmānubhavo 'sty asyetyātmano na prakāśakam ||

5,4.186

sati prakāśakatve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā |
rūpādau cakṣurādīnāṃ tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||

5,4.187

prakāśakatvaṃ bāhye 'rthe śaktyabhāvāt tu nātmani |
anyena vānubhāve 'sāv anavasthā prasajyate ||

5,4.188

tatra tatra smṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvānubhavakalpanā |
ekena tv anubhūtatve sarvaṃ tatraiva sambhavet ||

5,4.189

tatrāpi smṛtir ity etan na lokānumataṃ vacaḥ |
na hi vijñānasantānaṃ kaś cit smarati laukikaḥ ||<230>

5,4.190

ghaṭādāv agṛhīte 'rthe yadi tāvad anantaram |
arthāpattyāv abudhyante vijñānāni punaḥ punaḥ ||

5,4.191

yāvacchramaṃ tataḥ paścāt tāvatyeva smariṣyati |
tadā tv akalpite 'py evaṃ smṛtivarndhyāsutādivat ||

5,4.192

smṛtibhrāntaś ca yāpy atra paścāj jñāneṣu jāyate |
tadaivārthasmṛter eṣāṃ tajñānādipramāṇatā ||

5,4.193

yāvacchramaṃ ca tadbuddhis tatprabandhe mahaty api |
śramād rucyānyasamparkād vicchedo viṣayeṣv iva ||<231>

5,4.194

tatrāpi smṛtir ity eṣāṃ prathame pratyaye yadi |
tanmātragrahaṇād evaṃ nānavasthā prasajyate ||

5,4.195

smaraṇaṃ tv atha sarveṣu tatsiddhyai grahaṇaṃ tathā |
pramāṇavattvād āyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate ||

5,4.196

atha tānyādyavijñānaviṣayāṇīti kalpyate |
nottarottarabuddhīnāṃ viśeṣa upapadyate ||

5,4.197

vijñānaviṣayatvaṃ ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu |
ghaṭavijñāna tajñānaviśeṣas tena durlabhaḥ ||

5,4.198

smaran yathaiva vijñānaṃ nirākāraṃ smaratyayam |
tathā smaran gṛhītārthaṃ nirākāratayā smaret ||

5,4.199

jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvaṃ parāmarśo bhavaty asau |
tasyārtheṣv abhyupāyatvān na tu grāhyatvakāritaḥ ||<232>

5,4.200

pratyāsannatvasambandhau grāhyatvāsambhavāc cyutau |
viṣayatvena vāpy etau staḥ kiṃ deśāvibhāgataḥ ||

5,4.201

arthākārasya yo 'py ukto mithyājñāneṣv asambhavaḥ |
dośakālānyathāmātrasambhavaḥ keṣu cit kṛtaḥ ||

5,4.202

pratyakṣād anyavijñānam atītānāgatair api |
janyate 'rthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā ||

5,4.203

yaḥ punar nānubhūto 'rtho na vāpy anubhaviṣyate |
vāsanābhāvatas tatra tavāpy anubhavaḥ katham ||<233>

5,4.204

vināpi vāsanātaś ced buddhir utpadyate tataḥ |
vāsanāyā nimittatvam abhyupetaṃ virudhyate ||

5,4.205

vāsanā ced bhavet tatra sā ca saṃvittipūrvikā |
tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpy asau dhruvam ||

5,4.206

evaṃ ca naiva vaktavyam atyantābhavanaṃ kva cit |
anyathānupapatyā hi siddhā janmāntare 'stitā ||

5,4.207

duṣṭatvena ca vijñānam anyathāpi vyavasthitam |
pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhṇīyād ākāraṃ tannibandhanam ||

5,4.208

tānyapāsya tu naivārthe kva cid ākārakalpanā |
na jñānaṃ hy anavaṣṭambham ātmānaṃ labdhum arhati ||<234>

5,4.209

vijñānasyaiva vā kāryaṃ yady eṣo 'nye ca kalpitāḥ |
viśeṣaḥ ko 'tra yenāyam atyantāsannitīṣyate ||

5,4.210

tasmād bhrāntir api tv eṣāṃ kalpayantyartham eva naḥ |
kalpayatyanyathā santaṃ na tv ātmānaṃ vyavasyati ||

5,4.211

tataś ca bādhakajñānād vācoyuktir iyaṃ bhavet |
arthe 'nyathāpi saty eṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate ||

5,4.212

dvicandrādimatiṣv evam, tārakādimatau tathā |
strītvādyanyatra dṛṣṭaṃ syāt, kathañ cid veha sambhavet ||<235>

5,4.213

śabdamātrapratīyā vā, dṛṣṭair vā kaiś cid iṅganāt |
saṃstyānaprasavasthānair yathā pātañjale mate ||

5,4.214

tena liṅgatrayasyātra sadbhāvaḥ syāt pramāṇavān |
apekṣābhedataś cātra virodho 'pi na vidyate ||

5,4.215

kuṇapādimatau caivaṃ sārvarūpye vyavasthite |
vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||<236>

5,4.216

svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu |
nirdhāraṇe bhaved dhetur nāpūrvākārakalpane ||

5,4.217

tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā |
ākārabhedasampattir aviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||

5,4.218

nānekākārasaṃvitter nirākāratvakalpanā |
yuktā, pratītibhedāt tu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||

5,4.219

saṃvitteś ca viruddhānām ekasminn api sambhavaḥ |
ekākāraṃ bhaved ekam iti neśvarabhāṣitam ||

5,4.220

tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yad yathaivopalabhyate |
na cāpy aikāntikaṃ tasya syād ekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ ||<237>

5,4.221

tasmād deśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak |
vastvākārāḥ pratīyerann udbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||

5,4.222

yugapadgrāhāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam |
śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāv ākāraḥ sampratīyate ||

5,4.223

nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak |
cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||

5,4.224

evam eva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavaty api |
vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||

5,4.225

tasmād bahiḥ sthito 'py ātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ |
prāpya vāprāpya vā buddher viṣayatvena kalpyate ||

5,4.226

vadanti laukikā yac ca yādṛg jñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ |
te punar jñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||<238>

5,4.227

grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet |
tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||

5,4.228

laiṅgikāsattvam aprāptair etair bāhyārthavādibhiḥ |
jñānānubhavam utkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||

5,4.229

yathā loke ca tadbuddhir vācyam evaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |
na yādṛgantarākāras tādṛg bāhyo 'vakalpate ||

5,4.230

utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi |
pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||

5,4.231

bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivam icchati |
pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||<239>

5,4.232

uttaraṃ grahakābhāvāl liṅgābhāvāc ca nāsti naḥ |
tadā grahaṇam ity etat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||

5,4.233

teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam arthakāle 'vagamyate |
tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syād ity etadupadiśyate ||

5,4.234

nanv ity etadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt |<240>
paurvāpryavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||

5,4.235

kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syāj jñātatvam atha cet tadā |
bhūtakālāśrayād brūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||

5,4.236

atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājāt parasya tu |
bhrāntatvād anyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||

5,4.237

sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ |
prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitter yugapad veti cintyate ||

5,4.238

evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāj jñānāvabodhanam |
bravītu nūnam etasya paścād utpadyate 'pi tat ||

5,4.239

na caitac chaktyate tasmād utpatter apakarṣaṇam |
karomi tāvat tatkālā saṃvittir api setsyati ||<241>

5,4.240

prāk ca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayor dhruvam |
vivekādarśanam, tasmād idam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||

5,4.241

yugapad gṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate |
tasmād arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||

5,4.242

yas tv etasyottaro granthaḥ prāg evāsau nirūpitaḥ |
na tv etat sādhanaṃ sākṣāt pūrvaṃ buddher abodhane ||

5,4.243

na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'py ajñātavad yataḥ |
tasān na grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||<242>

5,4.244

ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ |
tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvād granthavarṇanā ||

5,4.245

kāmaṃ buddher iti tv etadarthādhīnatvam ucyate |
na cārtharūpād bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam ||

5,4.246

pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat |
asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||

5,4.247

svacchatvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām |
vāsanopaplavāt tena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||<243>

5,4.248

nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānam ubhayor api |
nijaśaktyanusāritvāj jñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||

5,4.249

tantvarthair api kasmād vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ |
nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tair mṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ ||

5,4.250

tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hy anuyojye mate yadi |
arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvad eva prasajyate ||

5,4.251

arthārambhavyavasthā cet sāmarthyaniyamāśrayā |
jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||

5,4.252

tasmād yatrobhayor doṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ |
naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyas tādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||

5,4.253

deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ |
śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||

5,4.254

śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattikalpitāḥ |
prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||

5,4.255

bhavatas tu na vijñānād bhinnābhinnā nirūpyate |
śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||<244>

5,4.256

vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate |
nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yad ucyate ||

5,4.257

tasyāś cāsambhavenaitad apārārthyāc ca durlabham |
deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||

5,4.258

matvaitad api cety āha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati |
tasmād aparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyas te yathā paṭaḥ ||

5,4.259

tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhir itīdṛśaḥ |
evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvad bāhyaśūnyatā ||

5,4.260

āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ, ato 'nyathāpi vā |<245>
nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattir viparyayāt ||

5,4.261

tasmād abhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ |
evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||

5,4.262

bāhyasyāṇusamūhāder grāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||

5,4.263

tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktād jñeyatvam anyasya balād upeyam |
grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||

5,4.264

iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ |
ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamam idaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

{5,5 anumānapariccheda AMP}

<246>

5,5.1

pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvād evaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat |
prasiddham anumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tad apy ataḥ ||

5,5.2

pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ, ekadeśyatha vocyate |
karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||

5,5.3

dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandham upalabdhaṃ parasparam |
tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau ||<247>
<248>

5,5.4

sambandho vyāptir iṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā |
vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyam iṣyate ||

5,5.5

yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet |
sa vyāpyo vyāpakas tasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||

5,5.6

tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakas tasya gṛhyate |
na hy anyathā bhavaty eṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||

5,5.7

vyāpakatvagṛhītas tu vyāpyo yady api vastutaḥ |
ādhikye 'py aviruddhatvād vyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||

5,5.8

vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭam etac ca goviṣāṇitvayor mitau |
vyāpyatvād gamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||

5,5.9

tena yatrāpy ubhau dhrmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau |
tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syād aṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||<249>

5,5.10

tena dharmyantareṣv eṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī |
deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||

5,5.11

tasya tāvati tādṛk sa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ |
vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādakaḥ ||

5,5.12

bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ |
jñāyate bhedahānena, kva cic cāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||

5,5.13

kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattikḷptivat |<250>
vyāpteś ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaś cid dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ ||

5,5.14

asmin saty amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate |
anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ ||

5,5.15

tair dṛṣṭair api naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā |
ye tu tān api visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||

5,5.16

sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣair bhrāmyanti te ciram |
teṣv āgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||

5,5.17

alaukikavivādāś ca varṇyas te haitukais tataḥ |
niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānām adharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||

5,5.18

tadabhāve na tatsiddhir hiṃsātvād aprayojakāt |
hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||<251>

5,5.19

jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ |
traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||

5,5.20

na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate |
kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca vināśitā ||

5,5.21

prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśair na prayujyate |
jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||

5,5.22

śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ |
tasmād ya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||

5,5.23

sa eva gamakas tasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ |
upāttaś caikadeśābhyāṃ dharmy apy atraikadeśatā ||

5,5.24

apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpair naikadeśatā |
sa eva cobhayātamāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||<252>

5,5.25

asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ |
ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktāṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||

5,5.26

anityaḥ kṛtako yasmād dhūmavān agnimān iti |
dharmyabhinnam upādānam, bhedo 'trāgnir itīdṛśe ||

5,5.27

ekadeśaviśiṣṭaś ca dharmyevātrānumīyate |
na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavaty anumeyatā ||

5,5.28

na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam |
vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||

5,5.29

ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca |
dvayaṃ ca na syād iṣṭaṃ sat pakṣeṣv eṣu yathākramam ||

5,5.30

anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi |
dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||<253>

5,5.31

sambandho 'py anupādānān nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau |
na cāpy anugamas tena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||

5,5.32

na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāg bhavet |
tasmad arthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||

5,5.33

na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ |
viśīṣṭārthapratītau syāt sambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||

5,5.34

viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam āpannau dvāv imāv ataḥ |
gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvas tu kaiś cid iṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||<254>

5,5.35

sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tv avagamyate |
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||

5,5.36

tatrotaraṃ vadanty anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam |
hetudharmeṇa samandhas tasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||

5,5.37

pradhānatvād dhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet |
tatrāsambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||

5,5.38

dhvaner ity atha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane |
bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||

5,5.39

agner deśaviśiṣṭatve na caitat pakṣalakṣaṇam |
viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhaved evamprakārikā ||

5,5.40

yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva cid deśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā |
agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||

5,5.41

yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā, yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā |
yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy ayam ||

5,5.42

etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yam agnir iti, <255>
iha tu |
pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syād viruddhatā ||

5,5.43

vyāptir etena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate |
nāpi pūrvasya, nāpy eṣa vahniḥ sarvair viśiṣyate ||

5,5.44

deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy asya na deśena viśeṣyatā |
etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yam ity etat kathyate katham ||

5,5.45

yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnir nāyam ity avadhāryate |
agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||

5,5.46

tajjñānakālabuddhaś ca na deśaḥ syād viśeṣaṇam |
deśasya parvatādes tu svarūpe pāvakād ṛte ||

5,5.47

gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati |<256>
tasmād dharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā ||

5,5.48

sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiś ca kalpitā |
nanu śabdavad eva syāl liṅgamyaṃ viśiṣaṇam ||

5,5.49

naivam, na hy atra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā |
na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaś cāvadhāritaḥ ||

5,5.50

viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāt tanmātrasyānumeyatā |
nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||

5,5.51

naitad asti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā |<257>
dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||

5,5.52

phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārāt puroditam |
prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakāras tu manyate ||

5,5.53

pratyakṣāniyamoktaś ca sarvatraivānuṣajyate |
anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||

5,5.54

parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ |<258>
tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||

5,5.55

niyamas tadvipakṣāc ca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ |
asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam ||

5,5.56

tādrūpyeṇa paricchittis tadviparyayato 'pi ca |
pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||

5,5.57

tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param |<259>
vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||

5,5.58

mūle tasya hy anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ |
pratyakṣādeś ca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||

5,5.59

tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāder asambhavāt |<260>
agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||

5,5.60

teṣām aśrāvaṇatvādi viruddham anumānataḥ |
na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||

5,5.61

sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu |
tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syāt pratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||<261>

5,5.62

pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ |
yāvajjīvam ahaṃ maunīty uktimātreṇa bādhyate ||

5,5.63

sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam |
dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||

5,5.64

bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate |
candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||

5,5.65

sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate |
jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayed idam ||

5,5.66

na gor gavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ |
gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃś caitro yadā bahiḥ ||

5,5.67

nāstīti sādhyate bādhas tatrārthāpattito bhavet |<262>
agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||

5,5.68

śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane |
śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||

5,5.69

divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam |
śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||

5,5.70

evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhas tāvad udāhṛtaḥ |
dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||

5,5.71

śrutyarthākṣiptayor vākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ |<263>
tṛṇādivikriyāhetor agnimaddhimasādhane ||

5,5.72

pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāt tadviśeṣotthabādhanam |
adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpam itīha tu ||

5,5.73

vihitatvād adharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam |
tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣas tasya bādhyate ||

5,5.74

ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ity ukte dvayabādhanam |
svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||

5,5.75

kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayor iha |<264>
darśanād ekadeśasyety anenaitad vyudasyate ||

5,5.76

yatraikasyobhayor vāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ |
śaityān na dāhako bahniś cākṣuṣatvād anityatā ||

5,5.77

śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ |
kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||

5,5.78

svokte caivamprakāre syād asiddho 'nyatarasya tu |
bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayor anyatarasya vā ||

5,5.79

dhūmas tridhāpy asiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvat svarūpataḥ |
eta eva prakārāḥ syur āśrayāsiddhikalpane ||<265>

5,5.80

jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā |
sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvād ātmā sarvagatas tv iti ||

5,5.81

bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādes tu saṃśayaḥ |
bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||

5,5.82

dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātas tadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam |
itarat sādhanaṃ tu syād vādinā yadi sādhyate ||

5,5.83

nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ |
sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||

5,5.84

jñātasambandhavacanāt, <266>
trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ |
san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||

5,5.85

dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāv ekatraikadeśini |
prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||

5,5.86

nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ |
nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syād asādhāraṇas tvayam ||

5,5.87

niścayaikāṅgavaikalyād eṣa saṃśayakāraṇam |<267>
sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||

5,5.88

viruddhaikānavāpteś ca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam |
atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||

5,5.89

dvayāsattvavirodhāc ca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam |
sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||

5,5.90

nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ |
vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāv amūrtivat ||

5,5.91

kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā |<268>
yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyor arūpatvena sādhyate ||

5,5.92

sparśāt pratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā |
ke cij jātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||

5,5.93

sādhāraṇatvam aṃśena samastaṃ vāpy ananvayam |
pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktair yasya sādhanaiḥ ||

5,5.94

tat parājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt |
kva cit saṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||

5,5.95

saṅghāte nirṇayas tābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat |
pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||

5,5.96

tasmād bhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau |
ṣoḍhā viruddhatām āhuś caturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||<269>

5,5.97

śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā |
nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhād viruddhatā ||

5,5.98

bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tv evaṃ prayujyate |
arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syāt prāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||

5,5.99

vibhaktimattvāt paścādvat svarūpeṇeti cāśrite |
asvarūpārthayogas tu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||

5,5.100

tena prāg api sambandhād asvarūpārthatā bhavet |
ihapratyayahetutvād dravyāder vyatiricyate ||

5,5.101

samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ |
atrāpy asamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||

5,5.102

tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyād viruddhatā |<270>
yac ca sattāvad ekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||

5,5.103

tatra saṃyogavadbhedāt syād viśeṣaviruddhatā |
nityam ātmāstitā kaiś cid yadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||

5,5.104

sādhyate 'vayavābhāvād vyomavad dvayabādhanam |
tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||

5,5.105

pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat |
śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||

5,5.106

ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam |
asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||

5,5.107

anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate |
gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptir gamyeti bhāṣitum ||

5,5.108

sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate |<271>
tatra hetvartham uddiśya sādhyopādānam iṣyate ||

5,5.109

uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaś cetaro mataḥ |
yadvṛttayoḥ prāthamyam ity ādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||

5,5.110

tadvṛttam eva kāraś ca syād upādeyalakṣaṇam |
vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||

5,5.111

sādhyahetutvam arthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ |
tatrājñānād yadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||

5,5.112

viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati |
vivakṣann api vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vaded yadi ||<272>

5,5.113

ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā |
na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syād aniṣṭasya caiva tat ||

5,5.114

tasmād vyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ |
yadā samyak prayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||

5,5.115

sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvāt paramārthataḥ |
nityo dhvaniramūrttatvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ||

5,5.116

ghaṭavad vyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati |
dharmyasiddhāv api hy evaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||

5,5.117

tat sadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite |
karmādyālocanād vyāptir hetor nāstīti varjanam ||

5,5.118

vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate |
sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||<273>

5,5.119

paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt tac ca nāpekṣate yadā |
vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vaded yadā ||

5,5.120

viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tat samādhitsayā tadā |
pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||

5,5.121

sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetos tatropayujyate |
vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayor yādṛg iṣyate ||

5,5.122

tayor abhāvayos tasmād viparītaḥ pratīyate |
dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnis tataś cyutaḥ ||

5,5.123

adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute |
tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmas tatacyutaḥ ||

5,5.124

anyatrānavakāśatvād vyāpyate dhruvam agninā |<274>
vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||

5,5.125

naiva vyāpyād vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet |
tasmād dhūmena sādhyatvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā ||

5,5.126

tadānagnir adhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ, na cānyathā |
anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāpter vāpi viparyaye ||

5,5.127

na prastutopakāraḥ syād anyad vāpi prasādhyate |
yatrāpy arthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet ||

5,5.128

yad anityaṃ tu tan mūrtam aṇuvad buddhivat khavat |<275>
sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||

5,5.129

yasyāyaṃ nāsty asau hetus tena sādhyena nāpyate |
tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate ||

5,5.130

sahadṛṣṭir na sambandho vyāptir naiva ca tāvatā |
mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmād aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||

5,5.131

karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvam iṣyate |
aśeṣāpekṣitatvāc ca saukaryāc cāpy adarśanāt ||

5,5.132

sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati |
tāvatā na hy anaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||<276>

5,5.133

bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpter bhaviṣyati |
astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||

5,5.134

ke cit sādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ |
vaidharmyoktim apīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||

5,5.135

hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt sādhyenaivāvadhārite |
vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||<277>

5,5.136

tat tu mandaphalaṃ yasmāt pakṣe 'py evaṃ nirūpitam |
vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyān nityaṃ nivartate ||

5,5.137

tasmād yathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām |
nivṛttir na tu dairdhyādes tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||

5,5.138

dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hy agnidhūmayoḥ |
pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyos tathaiva hi ||

5,5.139

āditye 'nupalabdhiś cen na deśe 'py adhunātane |
kva cit tatropalabdhiś ced devadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||<278>

5,5.140

yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā |
syād agnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmād evaṃ pracakṣate ||

5,5.141

pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayor eva viśeṣayoḥ |
gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||

5,5.142

taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam |
yadāgnir budhyate, <279>
tasya pūrvabodhāt punaḥ punaḥ ||

5,5.143

sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhāt pramāṇatā |
viśeṣadṛṣṭam etac ca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||

5,5.144

ākṛtyor eva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit |
hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||

5,5.145

agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau |
sāmānyadṛṣṭam ekāntād atretyāditya ucyate ||

5,5.146

pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam |
vastutvaṃ ca, atra hetur vā dvayasyāpy abhidhīyate ||

5,5.147

dhūmād agnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet |
abhāvānyapramāṇatvāt svārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||

5,5.148

sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca |
abhāvānyaprameyatvād asādhāraṇavastuvat ||<280>

5,5.149

sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate |
na ca liṅgavinirmuktam anumānaṃ pravartate ||

5,5.150

asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cid iṣyate |
na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñ cid asti prakāśakam ||

5,5.151

tasya vāpy anumānena syād anyena gatiḥ punaḥ |
tadutpattiś ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||

5,5.152

tasya cāpy anumānatvāt bhavel liṅgena codbhavaḥ |
anumānāntarād eva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||

5,5.153

liṅgaliṅgyanumānānām ānantyād ekaliṅgini |
gatir yugasahasreṣu bahuṣv api na vidyate ||

5,5.154

atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmād gatir bhavet |
pramāṇād apramāṇād vā, tathā liṅgigatir bhavet ||

5,5.155

evam apy anumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate |<281>
pramāṇāntaram eva syāt sāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||

5,5.156

apramāṇāvabuddhād vā liṅgāl liṅgini yā matiḥ |
sāpi mithyā bhaven nityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||

5,5.157

nanv apramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtir iṣyate |
yathā liṅgigatau hetus tathā liṅgagatir bhavet ||

5,5.158

tatra yat pūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate |
tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāc caritārthatā ||<282>

5,5.159

na tu liṅgagatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate |
tadabhāvāsmṛtiś cātra na kathañ cit pravartate ||

5,5.160

smārtam etadabhedena vijñānam iti yo vadet |
tasya vandhyāsute 'py asti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||

5,5.161

na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam |
yasmān nāsyāvinābhāvas tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañ cana ||

5,5.162

syād vā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat |
na hy asādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||

5,5.163

na cāpy avyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca |
vinā pūrvānusandhānāl liṅgatvam upapadyate ||<283>

5,5.164

kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'py aliṅgam ananvayāt |
etasmād eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasyāpy aliṅgatā ||

5,5.165

sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam |
kva cid vā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||

5,5.166

sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyam eṣitavyaś ca liṅganaḥ |
anumānapravṛttes tu prāg jñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||

5,5.167

na cāpi vāsanāmātrāl liṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ |
liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvat syāt trirūpāl liṅgato na tat ||<284>

5,5.168

tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāv ānumānikaḥ |
pramāṇāntaragamyatvāt tatra doṣo na jāyate ||

5,5.169

pratyakṣāvagatāl liṅgād yasya liṅgigatir bhavet |
tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñ cit prārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||

5,5.170

yatrāpy anumitāl liṅgāl liṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣād eva gamyate ||

5,5.171

liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā |
pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭam iti dūraṃ na gamyate ||

5,5.172

evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ |
taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||

5,5.173

tasmāt pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate |
pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatir bhavet ||

5,5.174

pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet |
yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||<285>

5,5.175

rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā |
svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||

5,5.176

te cāpi tāvat sāmānyaṃ yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ |
dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||

5,5.177

na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit |
na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||

5,5.178

bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet |
na ca bhinneṣv abhinnatvabuddher grāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||<286>

5,5.179

samudāyo na vāpy asti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā |
sarveṣām asatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||

5,5.180

na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā |
samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣām apagacchati ||

5,5.181

sāmānyam ity adṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ |
vyāsaṅginī bhavaty eṣā dhīrvināpy ekakalpanāt ||

5,5.182

vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ |
grahaṇaṃ tadvad eva syāt prativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||

5,5.183

mīmāṃsakaiś ca nāvaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ |
yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayed bhavān ||

5,5.184

samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ |
yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||

5,5.185

samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā |
yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||<287>

5,5.186

tasmād yad gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā |
tat tathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyam atha vetarat ||

5,5.187

sattādisāmānyam apekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatām upaiti |
tasmād asādhāraṇam akṣagamyaṃ vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta ||

5,5.188

sāmānyarupeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhir atra |
yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smin dvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

{5,6 śabdapariccheda SBP}

5,6.1

pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam |
adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrād abhidhīyate ||<288>

5,6.2

sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam |
na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ito 'py asya na vācyatā ||

5,6.3

yac coktaṃ śabdavijñānād arthe jñānam itīdṛśamū |
aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||

5,6.4

pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā |
puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstram abhidhīyate ||

5,6.5

svarūpakathanaṃ yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate |
tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvam avagamyate ||

5,6.6

bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyād evopajāyate |
pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tacchāstraṃ na padād yataḥ ||

5,6.7

aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam |
na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||

5,6.8

tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam |
vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||<289>

5,6.9

pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ |
śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||

5,6.10

yat tu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam |
tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||

5,6.11

veśeṣaś ca na sāmānyam antareṇāsti kaś cana |
tasmāt tam apy udāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayet sukham ||

5,6.12

sāmānyarūpam apy etadadhikārād viśiṣyate |<290>
codanā copadeśaś ca śāstram evety udāhṛtam ||

5,6.13

yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyām eva vartate |
śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||

5,6.14

pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam |
śāstrasyāpy aparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||

5,6.15

tatrānumānam evedaṃ bauddhair vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam |
bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhis tv iṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||

5,6.16

pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā |
vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstīty etena bhinnatā ||

5,6.17

yair uktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā |<291>
dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣān na hi bhinnatā ||

5,6.18

tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvan na pratipādyate |
tāvad viśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||

5,6.19

yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītir yāpi śabdataḥ |
na dhūmāder itīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||

5,6.20

hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane |
bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ ||<292>

5,6.21

puruṣākṣiptatayāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā |
padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||

5,6.22

sambandhātubhavaś cāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ |
etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||

5,6.23

kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ, uktā cānyair abhinnatā |
āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyād anumānataḥ ||

5,6.24

na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedāt sarvatra bhinnatā |
na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedas teṣāṃ pratīyate ||

5,6.25

na cāpy ajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñ cit prakāśakam |
sambandhān anubhūtyāto na syād ananumānatā ||<293>

5,6.26

tulyākāratayāpy atra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām |
agnidhūmeṣv adṛṣṭatvān na bhedas tannivāraṇāt ||

5,6.27

pratibimbeṣv anaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe |
tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||

5,6.28

pratyakṣatā tadāpy atra tadānyair vyabhicāritā |
yatra pādādi bambena gatānām anumīyate ||

5,6.29

ekavākyāt sakṛc coktān nāpy anekasya tatkṣaṇam |
syād viruddhāviruddhasya bodhād etasya bhinnātā ||

5,6.30

liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ |<294>
virodhān nānumānaṃ cet, syād anāgamatāpi te ||

5,6.31

yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syād anumānatā |
sakṛduccarite cāsmin vivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||

5,6.32

yas tv anirdhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |
sa liṅge 'py asphuṭe dṛṣṭas tasmān naitena bhidyate ||

5,6.33

dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |
prasiddhatvād dhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||

5,6.34

anabhyas te tv apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim |
atra pratyukta ity evaṃ budhyante hi cirāt kva cit ||

5,6.35

paroktā hetavaś cātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ |
śabdānumānayor aikyaṃ dhūmād agnyanumānavat ||

5,6.36

anvayavyatirekābhyām ekapratyakṣadarśanāt |
sambandhapūrvakatvāc ca pratipattir ito yataḥ ||

5,6.37

pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāt tadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt |
sāmānyaviṣayatvāc ca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||<295>

5,6.38

kaiś cin mīmāṃsakair ukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt |
pūrvābhyāṃ hy aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate ||

5,6.39

tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syāt puruṣokte, tathās tu cet |
pratyayaḥ kin nimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nv asau ||

5,6.40

na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañ cana |
viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||

5,6.41

tena vaktur abhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite |
puruṣoktir api śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||

5,6.42

na cāpy ananumeyatvam āgamārthasya śakyate |<296>
liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gner iva kalpyate ||

5,6.43

na cāpy ananumeyavāt pramāṇāntaragamyatā |
rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||

5,6.44

evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cin nātiprapañcinaḥ |
anumānaviśeṣo 'yam īdṛg dharmasya bodhakaḥ ||

5,6.45

bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam |
saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||

5,6.46

lakṣaṇena tv abhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ |
vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syād atallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||

5,6.47

āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyān nṛvacassu hi |
lakṣaṇenānumānatvāt prāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||

5,6.48

vede tv āptanarābhāvāt sambandhānubhavād ṛte |
lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyety aprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||<297>

5,6.49

nanv ekadeśasatyatve tasya syād anumānatā |
vedatvād agnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||

5,6.50

nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvad vā gauṇatā bhavet |
nātaḥ pratyanumānānām evaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||

5,6.51

tasmāl lakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā |
samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||

5,6.52

tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syād āgamalakṣaṇam |
nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmāt pramāṇatā ||

5,6.53

purastād varṇitaṃ hy etat, tsmāc chabdena yā matiḥ |<298>
tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cet syād doṣadarśanam ||

5,6.54

anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam |
pade tāvat kṛto yatnaḥ parair ity atra varṇyate ||

5,6.55

viṣayo 'nyādṛśas tāvad dṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ |
sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||

5,6.56

dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaś ca liṅgīty etac ca sādhitam |
na tāvad anumānaṃ hi yāvat tadviṣayaṃ na tat ||

5,6.57

sāmānyād atiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ |
sāmarthyād anumeyatvād aśrute 'pi padāntare ||

5,6.58

saṃkhyādimān padārthaś cet, na tāvat so 'vyayādiṣu |
yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakter viśeṣaṇam ||

5,6.59

padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyāc ca kriyātmanaḥ |<299>
vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||

5,6.60

saty apy atra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvān naiva pakṣatā |
tāvān eva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ ||

5,6.61

bhedabuddheś ca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ |
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||

5,6.62

viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiś cātra viparyayaḥ |
atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmān na kalpyate ||

5,6.63

pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetus tatra prasajyate |
pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ hetur iṣyate ||

5,6.64

śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate |<300>
vyaktir eva viśiṣyāto hetuś caikā prasajyate ||

5,6.65

bhaved vyañjakabhedāc cet, na tv evaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ |
kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvad deśakālataḥ ||

5,6.66

tatpratītiviśiṣṭaś cet, paraṃ kim anumīyate |
na pratyāyanaśaktiś ca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||

5,6.67

viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktir hi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat |
sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetus tad eva ca ||<301>

5,6.68

tasmād arthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā |
kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||

5,6.69

na kriyākartṛsambandhād ṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit |
rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||

5,6.70

vṛkṣas tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ |
deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||

5,6.71

kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate |
na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||

5,6.72

na cāsty asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā |
tasmān na pakṣadharmo 'yam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||

5,6.73

nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā |
vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||

5,6.74

tair apy etannirūpyaṃ tu śabdas tadviṣayaḥ katham |
na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||

5,6.75

tasmād utpādayaty eṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim |
tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||<302>

5,6.76

tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā |
na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchen na caivam anumānatā ||

5,6.77

gamakatāc ca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvād gamako yadi |
syād anyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmān naiṣāpi kalpanā ||

5,6.78

na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ |
śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatir bhavet ||

5,6.79

na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā |
na cāpi pūrvasambandham apekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||

5,6.80

dhūmavān ayam ity evam apūrvasyāpi jāyate |
pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||

5,6.81

na tv atra pūrvasambandhād adhikā pakṣadharmatā |<303>
na cārthapratyayāt pūrvam ity anaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||

5,6.82

na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet |
parvatādir yathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||

5,6.83

yaś cātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ |
na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃs taddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||

5,6.84

prāk sa cet pakṣadharmatvād gṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param |
paṣadharmādibhir jñātair yena syād anumānitā ||

5,6.85

anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate |
vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||

5,6.86

yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgner astitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
na tv evaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||

5,6.87

na tāvat tatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate |
bhaven nityavibhutvāc cet, sarvārtheṣu ca tat samam ||

5,6.88

tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvād vyatirekasya cāgateḥ |
sarvaśabdair aśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||<304>

5,6.89

athaivaṃ deśakālābhyām asatyatvaprakalpane |
vācakapratyayaṃ kaś cid brūyād arthadhiyānvitam ||

5,6.90

naivam apy asti dṛṣṭo hi vināpy arthadhiyā kva cit |
vācakapratyayo 'smābhir avyutpannanarān prati ||

5,6.91

dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhaved anvayakalpanā |
śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||

5,6.92

nanu ye jñātasambandhās teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
yady evam anvayāt pūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||

5,6.93

nāṅgam arthadhiyām eṣā bhaved anvayakalpanā |
anvayādhīnajanmatvam anumānasya ca sthitam ||

5,6.94

jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśād eva jāyate |
paścād anvaya ity eṣa kāraṇaṃ katham ucyate ||

5,6.95

tasmāt tannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate |<305>
na ca dhūmānvayāt pūrvaṃ śaktatvam avagamyate ||

5,6.96

vyatireko 'py avijñātād arthāc chabdadhiyau yadi |
so 'pi paścāt sthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||

5,6.97

sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam |
syād anvayo 'tirekaś ca na tv arthādhigamasya tau ||

5,6.98

tasmād ananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavad bhavet |
trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||

5,6.99

sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā |
yuktā na tu padajñānāt padārtho 'tra pramīyate ||<306>

5,6.100

padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate |
pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||

5,6.101

tatra yat pūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate |
pramite ca prayuktatvād anuvādo 'dhikād vinā ||

5,6.102

adṛṣṭapūrve tv ajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā |
sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tv anyagocaraḥ ||

5,6.103

parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matir bhavet |
parokṣaś cānubhūtaś ca yas tatra smṛtir iṣyate ||

5,6.104

pramite ca pravṛttatvāt smṛter nāsti pramāṇatā |
paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate ||

5,6.105

tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā |
pratyabhijñānavat kasmāt smṛter api na kalpyate ||

5,6.106

yāvān pūrvaparicchinnas tāvān evāvadhāryate |
smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||

5,6.107

padam abhyadhikābhāvāt smārakān na viśiṣyate |
padādhikyaṃ bhavet kiñ cit tatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||<307>

5,6.108

prāṇam anumānaṃ vā yady api syāt padānmitiḥ |
vākyārthasyāgamārthatvād doṣo nāgamavādinām ||

5,6.109

vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavād ṛte |
buddhir utpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||

5,6.110

vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati |
sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||

5,6.111

vākyeṣv adṛṣṭeṣv api sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim |
dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

{5,7 upamānapariccheda UMP}

5,7.1

kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikair yadi |
bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaur gavayas tathā ||<308>

5,7.2

etasminn upamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ |
tasyāgamābahirbhāvād anyathaivopavarṇitam ||

5,7.3

puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate |
tadīyavacanatvena tasmād āgama eva saḥ ||

5,7.4

sadṛśād upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare |
dhyānādismṛtitulyatvāt sā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||

5,7.5

deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate |
prameyaṃ naivam asty atra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||

5,7.6

śrutātideśavākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ |
yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñ cid gosādṛśyānurañjitā ||

5,7.7

pratyakṣo gavayas tāvat sādṛśyasmṛtir atra tu |
nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtir nendriyād gatiḥ ||<309>

5,7.8

pūrvavākyārthavijñānān nādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi |
smaraṇād aviśiṣṭatvāt saṅgater na pramāṇatā ||

5,7.9

atha tv adhikatā kā cit pratyakṣādivaśād bhavet |
yāvaddhīndriyasambandhas tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam ||

5,7.10

syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā |
śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||

5,7.11

ye 'pi hy aśrutatadvākyās teṣām api bhavaty ayam |
pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||

5,7.12

atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate |
na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||

5,7.13

na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate |<310>
sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyād avagato hy asau ||

5,7.14

na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane |
śaktyor atīndriyatvena smṛtir eva hi seṣyate ||

5,7.15

śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣam upapāditam |
tasmāt sādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||

5,7.16

vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate |
jātyādivat tadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||

5,7.17

pratyakṣābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpakavādinām |<311>
prameyavastvabhāvāc ca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||

5,7.18

sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyam apabādhitum |
bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||<312>

5,7.19

sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat |
tat svāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||

5,7.20

evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ |
ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedād etasya citratā ||

5,7.21

na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā |
bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||

5,7.22

yamayoḥ katham etac ced, dṛṣṭatvāt kim ihocyate |
kva cid dhi bhūyasām etat kva cid alpīyasām api ||

5,7.23

naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate |<313>
sāmānyāny api caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||

5,7.24

anantāśrayayogāc ca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate |
tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||

5,7.25

sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cid abhyupagamyate |
sarvasya hy āśrayaḥ kaś cid asti deśāntarādiṣu ||

5,7.26

teṣāṃ bhūyas tayā cedaṃ sādṛśyam atiricyate |
tāni vyastāni santy evaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva cit kva cit ||

5,7.27

sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate |
tad apy avayavānāṃ syāt samānavayavāntaraiḥ ||

5,7.28

evaṃ tāvad yato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā |
tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavet sādṛśyavarjitam ||

5,7.29

pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate |
sa eveti bhavet tatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||<314>

5,7.30

citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet |
tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā ||

5,7.31

rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cit tulyatā kva cit |
nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate ||

5,7.32

pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satām eva svabhāvataḥ |
pariṇāmādibhir vyaktir yathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||

5,7.33

na hi śaktyātmanā kiñ cid asajjama prapadyate |<315>
dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntararasthitiḥ ||

5,7.34

vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā |
dvayor ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||

5,7.35

sāmānyavac ca sādṛśyam ekaikatra samāpte |
pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāt tadupapadyate ||

5,7.36

tatra yady api gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānam upajāyate |
sannidhergavayasthatvād bhaved indriyagocaraḥ ||

5,7.37

tasmād yat smaryate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam |
prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||<316>
