5,7.38

pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ |
viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddher upamānanapramāṇatā ||

5,7.39

pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake |
viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||

5,7.40

yatra tv asadṛśād eva kalpayitvopajāyate |
sādṛśyapratyayas tatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||

5,7.41

bādhakapratyayāc caiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā |
yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||<317>

5,7.42

samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi |
na bādhyate samīpādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat ||

5,7.43

na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt |
prāk prameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||

5,7.44

gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavām anumāpakam |
pratijñārthaikadeśatvād gogatasya na liṅgatā ||

5,7.45

gavayaś cāpy asambandhān na gor liṅgatvamṛcchati |
sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||

5,7.46

ekasminn api dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane |
sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃs tadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||<318>

5,7.47

śṛṅgitvāder athocyeta sambandhāl liṅgatā gavi |
na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||

5,7.48

yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syān niḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet |
na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||

5,7.49

sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayāt param |
gavayapratyayād eva gojñānam upajāyate ||

5,7.50

sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣām evopamā bhavet |
na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gaur anumīyate ||

5,7.51

itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate |
nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇān nātivartate ||<319>

5,7.52

bhinnānumānād upameyam uktam, sauryādivākyair asahāyi dṛṣṭam |
sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayed ity upayujyate naḥ ||

5,7.53

pratinidhir api caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogād bhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau |
tad api phalam abhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtir api gauṇair bodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||

5,7.54

matir api ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminn |
itaraviṣayabodhe 'saty apītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

{5,8 arthāpattipariccheda AAP}

<320>

5,8.1

pramāṇaṣaṭkavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet |
adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayed anyaṃ sārthāpattir udāhṛtā ||

5,8.2

dṛṣṭaḥ pañcabhir apy asmād bhedenoktā śrutodbhavā |
pramāṇagrāhiṇītvena yasmāt pūrvavilakṣaṇā ||

5,8.3

tatra pratyakṣato jñānād dāhād dahanaśaktatā |
vahner anumitāt sūrye yānāt tacchaktiyogyatā ||

5,8.4

śrutārthāpattir atraiva parastād abhidhāsyate |
gavayopamitā yā gaus tajjñānagrāhyatā matā ||

5,8.5

abhidhānaprasiddhyartham arthāpattyāvabodhitāt |
śabde bodhakasāmarthyāt tannityatvaprakalpanam ||<321>

5,8.6

abhidhā nānyathā sidhyed iti vācakaśaktatām |
arthāpattyāvagamyaivaṃ tadananyagateḥ punaḥ ||

5,8.7

arthāpattyantareṇaiva śabdanityatvaniścayaḥ |
darśanasya parārthatvād ity asminn abhidhāsyate ||

5,8.8

pramāṇābhāvanirṇītacaitrābhāvaviśeṣitāt |
gehāc caitrabahirbhāvasiddhir yā tv iha darśitā ||

5,8.9

tām abhāvotthitām anyām arthāpattim udāharet |
pakṣadoṣeṣu cānyāsāmudāharaṇavistaraḥ ||

5,8.10

abhāvāvagatāc caitrād bahirbhāvasya sūcanam |
pakṣadharmādyanaṅgatvād bhinnaivāpy anumānataḥ ||

5,8.11

bahirdeśaviśiṣṭe 'rthe deśe vā tadviśeṣite |
prameye yo gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmas tv asau katham ||

5,8.12

tadabhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhaṃ dharmo na kasyacit |
gṛhābhāvaviśiṣṭas tu tadāsau na pratīyate ||

5,8.13

gamyate tu gṛhaṃ tatra na ca caitraḥ pratīyate |<322>
na cātrādarśanaṃ hetur yathābhāve 'bhidhāsyate ||

5,8.14

tena veśmanyadṛṣṭatvād iti hetur na kalpyate |
adarśanād abhāve ca prameyasyāvadhārite ||

5,8.15

bahirbhāvamatir nāsau tenādarśanahetukā |
caitrābhāvasya hetutvaṃ gehe 'bhāvaś ca saṃsthitaḥ ||

5,8.16

pūrvaṃ na cāgṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā |
na cātra bāhyadeśo vā caitro vā gṛhyate purā ||

5,8.17

nadīpūreṇa yā vṛṣṭir upariṣṭāt pratīyate |
deśe katham adṛṣṭe tu pakṣadharmatvasambhavaḥ ||

5,8.18

vṛṣṭimatparadeśatvaṃ nadīpuravato 'tra tu |
deśasya pratipadyante yadvārthāpattir eva sā ||<323>

5,8.19

jīvataś ca gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmo 'tra kalpyate |
tatsaṃvittir bahirbhāvaṃ na cābuddhvopajāyate ||

5,8.20

agnimattānapekṣā tu dhūmavattā pratīyate |
na tadgrahaṇavelāyām agnyadhīnaṃ hi kiñcana ||

5,8.21

gehābhāvas tu yaḥ śuddho vidyamānatvavarjitaḥ |
sa mṛteṣv api dṛṣṭatvād bahirvṛtter na sādhakaḥ ||

5,8.22

vidyamānatvasaṃsṛṣṭagṛhābhāvadhiyānayā |
gehād utkālitaś caitro vidyate bahir eva hi ||

5,8.23

gehābhāvatvamātraṃ tu yat svatantraṃ pratīyate |
na tāvatā bahirbhāvaś caitrasyaivāvadhāryate ||<324>

5,8.24

siddhe sadbhāvavijñāne gehābhāvadhiyātra tu |
gehād utkālitā sattā bahir evāvatiṣṭhate ||

5,8.25

tenāsya nirapekṣasya vyabhicāro mṛtādinā |
yasya tv avyabhicāritvaṃ na tato 'nyat pratīyate ||

5,8.26

tasmāt pratyakṣato gehe caitrābhāve hy abhāvataḥ |
jñāte yat sattvavijñānaṃ tad evedaṃ bahiḥ sthitam ||

5,8.27

pakṣadharmātmalābhāya bahirbhāvaḥ praveśitaḥ |
tadviśiṣṭo 'numeyaḥ syāt pakṣadharmānvayādibhiḥ ||

5,8.28

pakṣadharmādivijñānaṃ bahiḥ sambodhato yadi |
taiś ca tadbodhato 'vaśyam anyonyāśrayatā bhavet ||

5,8.29

anyathānupapattau tu prameyānupraveśitā |
tādrūpyeṇaiva vijñānān na doṣaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ||<325>

5,8.30

avinābhāvitā cātra tadaiva parikalpyate |
na prāg avadhṛtety evaṃ saty apy eṣā na kāraṇam ||

5,8.31

gṛhābhāvabahirbhāvau na ca dṛṣṭau niyogataḥ |
sāhitye 'pi pramāṇaṃ ca tayor anyan na vidyate ||

5,8.32

anyathānupapattyaiva hy ekenānyat pratīyate |
tathā na kalpyate tac cet sāhityaṃ na pratīyate ||

5,8.33

tena sambandhavelāyāṃ sambandhyanyataro dhruvam |
arthāpattyāvagantavyaḥ paścād asty anumānatā ||

5,8.34

gṛhadvāri sthito yas tu bahirbhāvaṃ prakalpayet |
yadaikasminn ayaṃ deśe na tadānyatra vidyate ||

5,8.35

tadāpy avidyamānatvaṃ na sarvatra pratīyate |
na caikadeśe nāstitvād vyāptir hetor bhaviṣyati ||<326>

5,8.36

nanv atrāvidyamānatvaṃ gamyate 'nupalabdhitaḥ |
sā cāprayatnasādhyatvād ekasthasyaiva sidhyati ||

5,8.37

naitayānupalabdhyātra vastvabhāvaḥ pratīyate |
taddeśāgamanāt sā hi dūrastheṣv asti satsv api ||

5,8.38

gatvā gatvā tu tān deśān yady artho nopalabhyate |
tato 'nyakāraṇābhāvād asann ity avagamyate ||

5,8.39

nanu cāgnyādyabhāve 'pi dhūmādivyatirekiṇām |
taddeśāgamanāt spaṣṭo vyatireko na sidhyati ||

5,8.40

yasya vastvantarābhāvaḥ prameyas tasya duṣyati |
mama tv adṛṣṭamātreṇa gamakaḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ||

5,8.41

nanv evam itaratrāpi sambandho 'nupalabdhitaḥ |
caitrābhāvasya bhāvena dṛṣṭatvād upapadyate ||<327>

5,8.42

sāhitye mitadeśatvāt prasiddhe cāgnidhūmayoḥ |
vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer gamakatvaṃ prakalpyate ||

5,8.43

iha sāhityam evedam ekasya sahabhāvinaḥ |
anantadeśavarttitvān na tāvad upapadyate ||

5,8.44

nanu deśāntaraṃ śūnyaṃ caitreṇaivaṃ pratīyate |
taddeśavyatiriktatvāt samīpasthitadeśavat ||

5,8.45

viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ tadvad eva hi gamyate |
samīpadeśabhinnatvāt caitrādhiṣṭhitadeśavat ||

5,8.46

puruṣasya tu kārtsnyena yad ekatropalambhanam |
tasyānyathā na siddhiḥ syād ity anyeṣv asya nāstitā ||<328>

5,8.47

tenārthāpattipūrvatvam atra yatra ca kāraṇe |
kāryādarśanataḥ śakter astitvaṃ sampratīyate ||

5,8.48

kāryasya nanu liṅgatvaṃ na sambandhānapekṣaṇāt |
dṛṣṭvā sambandhitāṃ caiṣā śaktir gamyeta nānyathā ||

5,8.49

taddarśane tadānīṃ ca pratyakṣāder asambhavāt |
arthāpatteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ trailakṣaṇyād vinā bhavet ||<329>

5,8.50

anumānād abhinnatvān noktau jayaparājayau |
vadhyaghātakabhāvena yau sarpanakulādiṣu ||

5,8.51

pīno divā na bhuṅkte cety evamādivacaḥ śrutau |
rātribhojanavijñānaṃ śrutārthāpattir ucyate ||

5,8.52

tām arthagocarāṃ kecid apare śabdagocarām |
kalpayanty āgamāc cainām abhinnāṃ pratijānate ||

5,8.53

prāyaśaś cānayā vede vyavahāro vyavasthitaḥ |
so 'vaidikaḥ prasajyeta yady eṣā bhidyate tataḥ ||

5,8.54

vacanasya śrutasyaiva so 'py arthaḥ kaiścid āśritaḥ |
tadarthopaplutasyānyair iṣṭo vākyāntarasya tu ||

5,8.55

na tāvac chrūyamāṇasya vacaso 'rtho 'yam iṣyate |
na hy anekārthatā yuktā vākye vācakatā tathā ||

5,8.56

padārthānvayarūpeṇa vākyārtho hi pratīyate |
na rātryādipadārthaś ca divāvākyena gamyate ||<330>

5,8.57

na divādipadārthānāṃ saṃsargo rātribhojanam |
na bhedo yena tadvākyaṃ tasya syāt pratipādakam ||

5,8.58

anyārthavyāpṛtatvāc ca na dvitīyārthakalpanā |
tasmād vākyāntareṇāyaṃ buddhisthena pratīyate ||

5,8.59

tasya cāgamikatve 'pi yat tad vākyaṃ pratīyate |
pramāṇaṃ tasya vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣādiṣu yad bhavet ||

5,8.60

na hy anuccārite vākye pratyakṣaṃ tāvad iṣyate |
nānumānaṃ na cedaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ tena saha kvacit ||

5,8.61

yadi tv anupalabdhe 'pi sambandhe liṅgateṣyate |
taduccāraṇamātreṇa sarvavākyamatir bhavet ||

5,8.62

na cārthāpattigamyāni sarvaiḥ sarvavacāṃsi hi |
sambaddhāny upalabdhāni yena teṣv anumā bhavet ||

5,8.63

na ca sattānumānena viśeṣo vānumīyate |<331>
iha vākyaviśeṣasya sattaiva tv avagamyate ||

5,8.64

pūrvasiddhaḥ svatantro 'rthaḥ svatantreṇa viśeṣitaḥ |
dharmādharmaviśiṣṭo 'tra nānumeyaḥ pratīyate ||

5,8.65

atha śrutasya vākyasya mīyate tadviśiṣṭatā |
tataḥ pakṣo 'bhyupetaḥ syād aprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||

5,8.66

kiñ ca liṅgāntarābhāvād etasya yadi liṅgatā |
pratijñārthaikadeśatvaṃ padavat te prasajyate ||

5,8.67

tadvad eva nirākāryā vacaso dharmadharmitā |
nāgṛhīte hi taddharmo gṛhīte nānumeyatā ||

5,8.68

kriyākārakasambandhād ṛte nāsti tu dharmatā |
avācakatayā caitan na dharmo viṣayātmanā ||

5,8.69

pratīter vācakatvaṃ cet prasaktānekaśaktitā |
anumāviṣayotthaṃ tu dharmatvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||

5,8.70

padārthair api tadvākyaṃ nāsambandhāt pratīyate |<332>
sāmānyānyanyathāsiddher viśeṣaṃ gamayanti hi ||

5,8.71

na tu vākyāntareṇaiṣāṃ vinā kiñcin na sidhyati |
na cāpy anyaḥ prakāro 'sti tena vākyena saṅgatau ||

5,8.72

athaitad vāci kalpyeta vākyam anyat tathaiva ca |
prasaṅgāt tatra dūre 'pi nāsambandhāt pramucyate ||

5,8.73

tataś ca prathamād eva varaṃ jñātum asaṅgatāt |
anvayavyatirekau ca pratiṣedhyau pade yathā ||

5,8.74

śrutavākyena sādṛśyaṃ nāśrutasyāsti kiñcana |
tasmād anupamānatvam arthasyāpy anayā diśā ||

5,8.75

upamānatvaliṅgatve vākyaṃ prati nivārite |
arthe 'pi caivam eva syāt, <333>
tasmāt pūrveṣv asambhavaḥ ||

5,8.76

ataḥ śrutasya vākyasya yad arthapratipādanam |
tadātmalābha eva syād vinā nety etad iṣyate ||

5,8.77

etadarthād vinā nāyam ity arthaḥ kiṃ na kalpyate |
vākyārthavac ca kiṃ nāyam āgamārthaḥ pratīyate ||

5,8.78

savikalpakavijñānaiḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate |
labdhaprayojane vākye paraṃ nāgamikaṃ ca naḥ ||<334>

5,8.79

nanu cāsati sambandhe sati vānavadhārite |
gamyajñānam idaṃ vākyaṃ prasajyetāpramāṇakam ||

5,8.80

sambandhasya pramāṇatvaṃ sthitaṃ kiñceśvarājñayā |
pratyakṣasya pramāṇatvaṃ kathaṃ vā saṅgater vinā ||

5,8.81

astīndriyārthasambandhas tatra cen nānapekṣaṇāt |
na hi pratyakṣavelāyāṃ sarveṇāsau nirūpyate ||

5,8.82

yenāpi tu nirūpyeta paścād anubhavād asau |
na syād eva pramāṇāṅgam asatā tulya eva saḥ ||

5,8.83

aprāpyakāriṇī yeṣāṃ cakṣuḥśrotre ca te yathā |
tajjñānasya pramāṇatvam icchanty evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||

5,8.84

tasmād asattve sattve vā sambandhasya yad eva naḥ |
jāyetābhaṅguraṃ jñānaṃ tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||<335>

5,8.85

na cāpy asyāḥ pramāṇatve kaścid vipratipadyate |
bhedābhede visaṃvādaḥ kṛtas tatra ca nirṇayaḥ ||

5,8.86

kṛte yatra ca sambandhād buddhir eva na jāyate |
tatra ki kriyatāṃ so 'pi prāmāṇye naiva kāraṇam ||

5,8.87

smṛtyā śrutir yā parikalpyate 'smin liṅgādibhir yā viniyojikā ca |
phalādibhir yat paripūraṇaṃ ca sambandhadṛk tatra na kācid asti ||

5,8.88

tat sarvam ityādy asamañjasaṃ syān na cediyaṃ syād anumānato 'nyā |
evaṃsvabhāvāpy anumānaśabdaṃ labheta ced asti yathepsitaṃ naḥ ||

{5,9 abhāvapariccheda ABH}

5,9.1

pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate |<336>
vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||

5,9.2

vastvasaṅkarasiddhiś ca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā |
kṣīre dadhyādi yan nāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate ||

5,9.3

nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate |
gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvas tu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||

5,9.4

śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ |
śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||

5,9.5

kṣīre dadhi bhaved evaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ |
śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtir ātmani ||

5,9.6

apsu gandho rasaś cāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha |
vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na ced asya pramāṇatā ||

5,9.7

na ca syād vyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ |
prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||

5,9.8

na cāvastuna ete syur bhedās tenāsya vastutā |<337>
kāryādīnām abhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||

5,9.9

yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatas tv ayam |
tasmād gavādivad vastu, prameyatvāc ca gamyate ||

5,9.10

na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntir vāpi yadṛcchayā |
bhavaty ato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||

5,9.11

pratyakṣāder anutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate |
sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||

5,9.12

svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake |
vastuni jñāyate kaiś cid rūpaṃ kiñ cit kadā cana ||<338>

5,9.13

yasya yatra yadodbhūtir jighṛkṣā vopajāyate |
cetyate 'nubhavas tasy tena ca vyapadiśyate ||

5,9.14

tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ |
ubhayor api saṃvittāv ubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||

5,9.15

ayam eveti yo hy eṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ |
naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamād ṛte ||<339>

5,9.16

nāstīty api ca saṃvittir na vastvanugamād ṛte |
jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñ cid upaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||

5,9.17

pratyakṣādyavatāras tu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā |
vyāpāras tadanutpatter abhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||

5,9.18

na tāvad indriyair eṣā nāstīty utpadyate matiḥ |<340>
bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||

5,9.19

nanu bhāvād abhinnatvāt samprayogo 'sti tena ca |
na hy atyantam abhedo 'sti rūpādivad ihāpi naḥ ||

5,9.20

dharmayor bheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite |
udbhavābhibhavātmatvād grahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||

5,9.21

idam eva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate |
bhāvābhāvadhiyor akṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||

5,9.22

rūpāder api bhedaṃ ca ke cid grāhakabhedataḥ |
varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||

5,9.23

buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityam eva hi |<341>
na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalanā ||

5,9.24

sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāder ekateṣyate |
svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||

5,9.25

yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syād bhedo 'tra naiva hi |
sadasadrūpatā buddher bhaved anyataratra naḥ ||

5,9.26

tatsambandhe sad ityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate |
nāsty atredam itīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||<342>

5,9.27

gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam |
mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||<343>

5,9.28

svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścāt kiñ cit smarann api |
tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭas tadaiva pratipadyate ||

5,9.29

na cāpy atrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvāt pratīyate |
bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||

5,9.30

abhāvāvagater janma bhāvāṃśe hy ajighṛkṣite |<344>
tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||

5,9.31

na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavat pratipadyate |
saha sarvair abhāvaiś ca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ ||

5,9.32

kva cid bhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana |
tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cid avagamyate ||

5,9.33

yatrāpy adṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca |
tadabhāvamatir dṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||

5,9.34

kasya cid yadi bhāvasya syād abhāvena kena cit |
sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||

5,9.35

gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ |
sarvatra matir ityevaṃ vyabhicārād aliṅgatā ||<345>

5,9.36

sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam |
tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇopajāyate ||

5,9.37

tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet |
tatrāvaśyam abhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||

5,9.38

pratyakṣāder anutpattir na tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati |
na viśeṣaṇasambandhas tasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||

5,9.39

na cāpy abhāvasāmānye pramāṇam upajāyate |
vyabhicārād viśeṣās tu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||<346>

5,9.40

na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate ced asāv api |
abhāvatvād abhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||

5,9.41

sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā |
tadgṛhītir hi liṅgena syād anyenety anantatā ||

5,9.42

liṅgābhāve tathaiva syād anavastheyam ity ataḥ |
kvāpy asya syāt pramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||

5,9.43

nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāder ajanmanaḥ |
tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvam ānantaryāt pratīyate ||

5,9.44

trilakṣaṇena yā buddhir janyate sānumeṣyate |
na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||

5,9.45

mānaṃ katham abhāvaś cet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam |
meyo yadvadabhavo hi mānam apy evam iṣyatām ||<347>

5,9.46

bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā |
tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||

5,9.47

bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam |
paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyaṃ syād dvayor api ||

5,9.48

yadi cāsya pramāṇatvam abhāvatvena neṣyate |
vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭam ity abhimānitā ||

5,9.49

na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvad eva hi |
tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||

5,9.50

pramāṇānām anutpatter nābhāvasyāpi dharmatā |
yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||

5,9.51

yo na sannihitas tatra tasya dharmo bhaved iyam |
na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||<348>

5,9.52

abhāvena tu sambandho bhavet tadviṣayatvataḥ |
tajjānād viṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||

5,9.53

saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate |
nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||

5,9.54

abhāvaśabdavācyatvāt pratyakṣādeś ca bhidyate |
pramāṇānām abhāvo hi prameyāṇām abhāvavat ||

5,9.55

abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate |
prameyatvād yathā bhāvas tasmād bhāvātmakāt pṛthak ||

5,9.56

karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvair yathāvac ca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ |
na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetat prabhavaṃ kratūnām ||

5,9.57

yuktyāgamābhyām iti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye |
tato 'dhikaṃ yad dvayam iṣṭam anyair bhedo na tasyety api siddham etat ||<349>

5,9.58

iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatir aviyutabhāvāt sānumānād abhinnā |
jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityam aitihyam uktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamād bhidyate tat ||

{5,10 citrākṣepavāda CAV}

5,10.1

paralokaphalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāś codanāḥ paraiḥ |
idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ, <350>
sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||

5,10.2

citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāś codaṇā mṛṣā |
pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tair arthāsaṅgatir yataḥ ||

5,10.3

yadīdṛk tanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsor yathā vacaḥ |
nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||

5,10.4

na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ |
snānabhujyādivat te 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||

5,10.5

tadutpattāvasadbhāvāt svarge tṛptisukhādivat |
vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukham ardane ||

5,10.6

ānantaryam ayuktaṃ cet, <351>
na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt |
śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tat pratipāditam ||

5,10.7

kālāntarānupādānāt karmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca |
codyamānasya citrāder ānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||

5,10.8

atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaś cottarasya tu |
svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||

5,10.9

yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ |
sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||

5,10.10

śarīrād yadi cānyaḥ syān nāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet |
na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||<352>

5,10.11

yadi syād vidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet |
viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syād idaṃ tataḥ ||

5,10.12

vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi |
virodhaparihāraḥ syād vartamāne 'pi nāsty asau ||

5,10.13

phalaṃ ca na bhaved evaṃ bhasmībhāvād vidhāv api |
tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||

5,10.14

prāyaś caivamprakāratvam arthavādeṣu dṛśyate |
mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnaḥ ||

5,10.15

evaṃ saty agnihotrādivākyeṣv api mṛṣārthatā |
vedavākyaikadeśatvāc citrādivacaneṣv api ||

{5,11 sambandhākṣepavāda SAV}

<353>

5,11.1

svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ |
svārthe vaktranapekṣatvāt padārthapadabuddhivat ||

5,11.2

tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ |
vākyabuddhivad eva atra pūrvoktāś cāpi hetavaḥ ||

5,11.3

nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā |
svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyartham aprāmāṇye nir kṛte ||

5,11.4

asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvam abravīt |
sambandho 'sti ca nityaś cety uktam autpattikādinā ||

5,11.5

mithyā tv asya nirāsārthaṃ tatparair neṣyate dvayam |
naiva cāsty atra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||<354>

5,11.6

asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate |
asminn eva ca sambandhe pratītir laukiko dhruvā ||

5,11.7

tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ |
taddeśānantarādṛṣṭer vindhyo himavatā yathā ||

5,11.8

evam artho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyam asaṅgatam |
kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetor uktam athāparaḥ ||

5,11.9

śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate |
sambandhasiddhasādhyatvam atha sambandhamātrakam ||

5,11.10

pitāputrādisambandhair anekāntaḥ prasajyate |
ekabhūmyādisambandhād dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||

5,11.11

vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam |
virodhaś ca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||

5,11.12

pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ |
abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||

5,11.13

śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam |<355>
pratipattāv upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite ||

5,11.14

niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ |
tatra yady apy asambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||

5,11.15

tathāpi yatkriyā tasyām upakāryopakāritā |
sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||<356>

5,11.16

na cātrāpy avinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam |
saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cen na tadaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||

5,11.17

gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ |
na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||

5,11.18

tasmād gamakatā paścād dhūmāder iva jāyate |
sānaṅgaṃ tadvad eva syād neyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||

5,11.19

nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hy asau |
gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||

5,11.20

iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ |
yad eva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||

5,11.21

tadaiva gamako 'syāyam iti nānyasvarūpataḥ |
kathayanti kva cit tāvad boddhavyo 'smād ayaṃ tv iti ||

5,11.22

kva cid vācaka ity evaṃ vācyo 'yam iti cocyate |
kva cid uccaritācchabdād dṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||<357>

5,11.23

keṣāñ cit tatra boddhṛtvam anumānāt pratīyate |
etenāsmād yataḥ śabdād artho 'yam avadhāritaḥ ||

5,11.24

tena nūnam imau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau |
itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||

5,11.25

anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate |
bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||

5,11.26

pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt |
na lokaḥ kāranābhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati ||

5,11.27

balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate |
kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||

5,11.28

sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābālāt |
tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||

5,11.29

kiyad vā nityasambandhād abhidheyena lakṣyate |<358>
tatra prayogabāhulyāt tadviśeṣeṣv asatsv api ||

5,11.30

prayogāt parasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ |
sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||

5,11.31

gośabda iti vijñānam anvayavyatirekajam |
tasmād gamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||

5,11.32

tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ |
sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||<359>

5,11.33

sambandhagrahaṇāt pūrva yasmān na gamayaty ataḥ |
gavāder nābhidhāśaktir devadattapade yathā ||

5,11.34

yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārāt pratīyate |
tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||

5,11.35

svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale |
tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktis tatkṛtā bhavet ||

5,11.36

yatsādhakatamatvena kasya cit kiñ cid ucyate |
tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||

5,11.37

na hi tat kāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñ cid īdṛśam |
itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||

5,11.38

pratyātmaniyatatvāc ca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet |
bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva cit syād vā vivakṣayā ||

5,11.39

udvigno hy andhakāreṇa kaś cid evaṃ bravīty api |
kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||<360>

5,11.40

nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭir dīpaśatair api |
rūpādidarśane yasmāt tasmāc cakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||

5,11.41

śarīrātmamanoyogād asādhāraṇātābalāt |
vijñānāsattibhāvāc ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate ||

5,11.42

tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānam aṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ |
gauravāt karaṇatvena mataṃ cet kena vāryate ||

5,11.43

yathā cakṣur itīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvam ucyate |
devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ ||

5,11.44

prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate |
phalānantaryataś cāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||

5,11.45

puruṣādhīnavijñānas tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ |
yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaś ced dhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||<361>

5,11.46

bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānād yathā rajjughaṭādiṣu |
samaṃ nāsty anayoḥ kiñ cit tenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

{5,12 sphoṭavāda SPH}

5,12.1

ādhārātmani viñāte sukham ādheyabodhanam |
tasyaiva tāvat prastāvād atha gaur ity ato 'bravīt ||

5,12.2

pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayam uttaram |
tebhyo dadyād iti jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matam abravīt ||<362>

5,12.3

tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam |
yair āsatāṃ tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||

5,12.4

pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite |
na hetur balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tataḥ ||

5,12.5

tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yady arthaṃ gamayen na vā |
sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||

5,12.6

yadi tv arthagatau śaktir na syād asya tataḥ punaḥ |
vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||

5,12.7

agnyādīn gamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi |
na vā 'pratyāyakatvāt syād ekavarṇeṣv aśabdatā ||

5,12.8

na ca prāgarthavijñānāś chotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ |
na cārthajñānataḥ paścād aśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||

5,12.9

parasparānapekṣāś ca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ |
varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||<363>

5,12.10

alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdam uccaritaṃ matiḥ |
yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||

5,12.11

pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit |
na ca varṇeṣv anusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvat paṭe ||

5,12.12

teṣām anupalabdheś ca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ |
nāgamas tatparaś cāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||

5,12.13

na cāpy anupapattiḥ syād varṇasyāvayavair vinā |
yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpy avayavāntaraiḥ ||

5,12.14

pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaś ca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ |
kiṃ na syād, vyomavac cātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||

5,12.15

tadvac cāsyaikabuddhitvād deśabhede 'py abhinnatā |
nanu bhedamatir na syāt, <364>
tavāpy ekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||

5,12.16

sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīs tadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ |
na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syād ekatvadhīr yataḥ ||

5,12.17

vyaktes tāvan na sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate |
varṇeṣv anyatra śabdatvān nānyac ced varṇa eva saḥ ||

5,12.18

sa eveti matir nāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tat kva cit |
vināvayavasāmānyād varṇeṣv avayavā na ca ||

5,12.19

pratyakṣaviṣayatvāc ca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate |
vācakaś cātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||

5,12.20

gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā |
gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitat kiṃ na kalpyate ||

5,12.21

śābaleyagakāradīn niṣpannān vyaktirūpataḥ |
sāmānyadhīr na gṛhṇātīty ato jātir apīṣyate ||

5,12.22

na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate |
gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktir aparā sphuṭā ||

5,12.23

tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhir ekopajāyate |<365>
viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhaved vyañjakabhedataḥ ||

5,12.24

yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ |
viśeṣair api nānekam evaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||

5,12.25

tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedād bhedo 'bhyupeyate |
mamāpi vyañjakair nādair bhedabuddhir bhaviṣyati ||

5,12.26

tena yat prārthyate jāte tad varṇād eva labhyate |
vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīr yathā ||

5,12.27

kalpayitvāpi tatpaścād vibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ |
pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyur mahataḥ śramāt ||

5,12.28

dvayasiddhas tu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca |
kalpitasyeṣyate tadvat siddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||<366>

5,12.29

pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati |
vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛk pratīyate ||

5,12.30

dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ |
vivedo 'sty eva na hy eṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||

5,12.31

akṣv apy evaṃ paropādhir drutādipratyayo yathā |
varṇā ''śritatvād varṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||

5,12.32

gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate |
gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvāt paraiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||

5,12.33

avastutvena sādhyatvān niṣedhād dhetusādhyayoḥ |
sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhir na doṣāyātra jāyate ||

5,12.34

varṇatvāc cāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivad eva ca |
vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer nātra dṛṣṭaṃ nirvartakam ||<367>

5,12.35

gotvādivāraṇe tv eva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet |
nānyathā hi matis tatra syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||

5,12.36

na cāpy atraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ |
na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvanir yathā ||

5,12.37

piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādir jātir nityaṃ pratīyate |
tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātir ekā pratīyate ||

5,12.38

nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet |
bhavato 'tīndriyatvāt tu kathaṃ nādair viśeṣadhīḥ ||

5,12.39

nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrād yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate |
tadupaśleṣas tat asya bodhaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||

5,12.40

naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhis tu tadvaśāt |<368>
saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||

5,12.41

madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā |
gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||

5,12.42

tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāś ca gacchataḥ |
parvatādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataś ca tān ||

5,12.43

maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ |
vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||

5,12.44

gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇād vinā |
vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntir bhaviṣyati ||

5,12.45

varṇāntaratvam evāhuḥ ke cid dīrghapluptādiṣu |
na hi drutādivat tatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||

5,12.46

tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate |
sāmānyakalpanā tv anyair na yuktety abhidhīyate ||<369>

5,12.47

atvam ity ucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayor bhavet |
ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayos traimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||

5,12.48

sarvasādhāraṇatvena tad vijñātuṃ na śakyate |
pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||

5,12.49

avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyād vanādivat |
samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||

5,12.50

svato hrasvādibhedas tu nityavāde virudhyate |
sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||

5,12.51

tasmād uccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate |
dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ ā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svayam ||

5,12.52

dīrghāder nanv anaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet |
itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||

5,12.53

yādṛśāt pūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāv artho gamyate tādṛśāt |
bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiś cet, <370>
nāsāv artham iti prati ||

5,12.54

yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet |
paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmās tathaiva naḥ ||

5,12.55

nanu dīrghādyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet |
ānupūrvīvad evāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||

5,12.56

tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ |
teṣāṃ dīrghādivad bhedo na kadā cit pratīyate ||

5,12.57

tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syād drutādivat |<371>
nātra varṇāntaravyaktir iva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||

5,12.58

ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ |
abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||

5,12.59

ke cit svarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cid bodhānuvartinaḥ |
yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||

5,12.60

tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā |
varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||

5,12.61

yugapatpracitais taiś ca syād udāttādikalpanā |
pracaye tv itareṣāṃ syād vatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||<372>

5,12.62

varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpām eva te matim |
śanair utpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||

5,12.63

vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yady apy ekāntato bhavet |
varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣas tathāpi na virudhyate ||

5,12.64

nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati |
gakārādivacaś caitat teṣv eva na virotsyate ||

5,12.65

vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiś ca nityaiḥ sarvagatair api |
vyatiriktapadārambho varṇair nātropapadyate ||

5,12.66

anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |
varṇasāmānyavac cāpi na tatkalpanam arhati ||<373>

5,12.67

varṇātmanām abhedāc ca siddhā sāmānyadhīr api |
samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||

5,12.68

abhedasamudāyas tu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati |
teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam arthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||

5,12.69

yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane |
varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathivāvabodhakāḥ ||

5,12.70

teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānām arthapratyāyanaṃ prati |
sāhityam ekakartrādikramaś cāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||

5,12.71

kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam |
prayuñjānasya yat pūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||<374>

5,12.72

yaugapadyaṃ tv aśakyatvān naiva teṣām ihāśritam |
kartṛbhedaś ca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||

5,12.73

yugapad dṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā |
bhāvās tathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||

5,12.74

dṛṣṭaś ca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ |
abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||

5,12.75

sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā |
sarvatrāstīti neha syād upālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||

5,12.76

niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi |
sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedās tu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||<375>

5,12.77

ekasādhanasāṃsthāś ca vyāpārāvayavā yadā |
svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā ||

5,12.78

kiṃ punar bahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ |
bhaveyur yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||

5,12.79

yadā tv ādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ |
kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||

5,12.80

tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt |
sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syād vyāpāre varttamānatā ||

5,12.81

pratyekaṃ ye punas tatra vyāpārās tannirūpaṇam |
phalāniṣpattito na syān nāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||

5,12.82

phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati |
kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||<376>

5,12.83

avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiś ca kasya cit |
na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣām anaṅgatā ||

5,12.84

dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayor dhruvam |
arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktis tatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||

5,12.85

yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā |
tathaivetarayoḥ śaktir ānantarye na vidyate ||

5,12.86

na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktis tatra sarveṣv aśaktatā |
tathā hy aṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||

5,12.87

śaktis tatrāsti kā cid dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate |
saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||

5,12.88

na hy arthāvayavaḥ kaś cit pratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate |
samastasyātha vā kaś cid bodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||

5,12.89

rathasyāpi tu yat kāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat |<377>
pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñ cin manāg api yathehitam ||

5,12.90

atha yatkiñcid ucyeta vahane tad ihāpi naḥ |
svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣv arthe 'pi vā kva cit ||

5,12.91

yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ |
so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||

5,12.92

tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate |
na cāvayavaśo vyaktis tadabhāvān na cātra śrīḥ ||

5,12.93

pratyekaṃ cāpy aśaktānāṃ samudāye 'py aśaktayā |
tatra yaḥ parihāras te sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||<378>

5,12.94

sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam |
tavādhikaṃ bhavet tasmād yatno 'sāv arthabuddhiṣu ||

5,12.95

nānyathānupapattiś ca bhaved arthamatiṃ prati |
tad evāsyā nimittaṃ syāj jāyate yadanantaram ||

5,12.96

sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā |
bhavatītīdṛg evāsyā nimittam avakalpate ||

5,12.97

vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ |
kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||

5,12.98

eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke cit pracakṣate |
adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvan mātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||

5,12.99

atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi |
dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||<379>

5,12.100

tasyārthabuddhihetutve visaṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye |
tadbhāvabhāvitāhetur anyatreva pratīyate ||

5,12.101

saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam |
niṣpramāṇakam eveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||

5,12.102

yady api smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam |
kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||

5,12.103

tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate |
tasyārthabuddhihetutvam adṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||

5,12.104

śabdapakṣe 'pi tac caitad adṛṣṭatvān na mucyate |
kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||

5,12.105

kṣīṇārthāpattir evaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet |
saṃskārakalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||

5,12.106

dhvanibhyo 'py aparas tāvan neṣyetārthamatiṃ prati |
te vā yady upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||<380>

5,12.107

varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyam arthitā |
nityatvāt sarvadā tat syān na tu kāraṇatā tathā ||

5,12.108

itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapad yātha vā parā |
sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syān nityam arthadhiyaṃ prati ||

5,12.109

yad vā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yat param |
samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||

5,12.110

tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate |
nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tad bhavet ||

5,12.111

citrarūpāṃ cā tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām |
ke cid āhur yathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||

5,12.112

antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam |
smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣv anye pracakṣate ||

5,12.113

sarveṣu caivam artheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām |
iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsv api ||<381>

5,12.114

na cet tadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi |
śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||

5,12.115

tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syāt kramād varṇeṣu yady api |
pūrvajñānaṃ parastāt tu yugapat smaraṇaṃ bhavet ||

5,12.116

tadārūḍhās tato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt |
śabdārthamatis tena laukikair abhidhīyate ||

5,12.117

citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |
paścād gaur iti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate ||

5,12.118

vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭam ekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam |
varṇarūpāvabodhāt tu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||

5,12.119

yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syād ekaikasmād trayasya tat |
varṇatrayaparityāge buddhir nānyatra jāyate ||

5,12.120

gaur ity ekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhir nivāryate |
tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syād ekatāmatiḥ ||<382>

5,12.121

śaidhyād alpāntaratvāc ca gośabde sābhaved api |
devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||

5,12.122

na gauṇaḥ śabda ity evaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet |
asy akṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||

5,12.123

śabdād iti ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate |
bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntāj jñānena vyavadhir bhavet ||

5,12.124

gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi |
na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya cit sampratīyate ||

5,12.125

svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminn eva kārake |
dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛk tu śabdasyety avyavetatā ||

5,12.126

gakārāder yadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate |
tadā tasmāt pratīte 'rthe śabdād iti kathaṃ bhavet ||<383>

5,12.127

śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā |
pratyaye śabdajanyatvam iti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||

5,12.128

saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam |
arthapratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||

5,12.129

tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate |
samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||

5,12.130

yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate |
varṇo 'ntyo gamakas tasya śabdatvān mudhyatā bhavet ||

5,12.131

varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ |
vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||

5,12.132

sattvād ghaṭādivac ceti sādhanāni yathāruci |
laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||

5,12.133

nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |
ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||<384>

5,12.134

pratiṣedhet tu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān |
dṛṣṭabādho bhavet tasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||

5,12.135

varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā |
yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāder iva bahnidhīḥ ||

5,12.136

dīpavad vā gakārādir gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ |
dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||

5,12.137

varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalam ādadhāti |
kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni katuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

{5,13 ākṛtivāda AKV}

<385>

5,13.1

ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca |
na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tad vācyatvam ihocyate ||

5,13.2

tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyartham atra tāvat prayatyate |
vācyatve vakṣyate yuktir vyaktyā saha balābale ||

5,13.3

jātim evākṛtiṃ prāhur vyaktir ākriyate yayā |
sāmānyaṃ tac ca piṇḍānām ekabuddhinibandhanam ||

5,13.4

tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcit sāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram |
sarva evecchatīty evam avirodho 'tra vādinām ||<386>

5,13.5

sarvavastuṣu buddhiś ca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā |
jāyate dvyātmatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||

5,13.6

viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatir bhavet |
sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||

5,13.7

na cāpy anyatarā bhrāntir upacāreṇa ceṣyate |
dṛḍhatvāt sarvadā buddher bhrāntis tadbhrāntivādinām ||

5,13.8

mukhyayoś cāpy adṛṣṭatvān nopacāreṇa kalpanā |
bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||

5,13.9

anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |
viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||<387>

5,13.10

nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat |
sāmānyarahitatvāc ca viśeṣās tadvad eva hi ||

5,13.11

tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ |
tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||

5,13.12

sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣv eva yo vadet |
vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktis tu kīdṛśī ||

5,13.13

grāhyā kiṃ vāpy asambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca |
gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātir evānyaśabdikā ||

5,13.14

bhaven nirviṣayā buddhir yadi śaktir na gṛhyate |
na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaś cid iṣyate ||<388>

5,13.15

parasparavibhinnatvād viśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ |
gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiś caiṣāṃ na vidyate ||

5,13.16

bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnām ekabuddhir na labhyate |
viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatir bhavet ||

5,13.17

bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca |
pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmāj jātir apīṣyatām ||

5,13.18

tenātmadharmo bhedānām ekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ |
sāmānyam ākṛtir jātiḥ śaktir vā so 'bhidhīyatām ||

5,13.19

nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyam iti jāyate |
buddhir vināpi sāmānyād anyasmāt sā kathaṃ bhavet ||

5,13.20

vanopanyāsatulyo 'yam upanyāsaḥ kṛtas tvayā |
bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntir gotvādidhīr api ||<389>

5,13.21

śabdāt pūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāv iva naikadhīḥ |
vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||

5,13.22

evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām anantatā |
punas tena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatir asti hi ||

5,13.23

viśeṣeṣv api vastutvāt sāmānyam iti dhīr bhavet |
sattādiṣv iva, ttenaitat sāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||

5,13.24

tasmād ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttis tannibandhanaḥ |
sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāv ekadhīkaraṇena vā ||

5,13.25

piṇḍeṣv eva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ |
na hy ākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñ cana ||

5,13.26

yad vā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ |<390>
śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||

5,13.27

tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tad eva tu |
tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣv etat pratīyate ||

5,13.28

bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñ cic chaktiḥ kāś cid aśaktikāḥ |
na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||

5,13.29

vahnir dahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām |
na cānyā mṛgyate yuktir yathā sandṛśyate tathā ||

5,13.30

na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstīty etaj jñānam anarthakam |
dharmaś cāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe ||

5,13.31

nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim |<391>
svābhāvikaś ca sambandho jātivyaktyor na hetumān ||

5,13.32

tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyat sāmānyam iṣyate |
śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||

5,13.33

yad vā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt |
viśeṣeṣv eva labdheṣu keṣu cin nānyavāñchanam ||

5,13.34

na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatas teṣu na dṛśyate |
tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||

5,13.35

sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet tasya vṛtter niyāmakam |
gotvenāpi vinā kasmād gobuddhir na niyamyate ||<392>

5,13.36

yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cid vṛttyapekṣitā |
gotvāder animitte 'pi tathā buddhir bhaviṣyati ||

5,13.37

viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattir iṣyate |
viśeṣād anyad icchanti sāmānyaṃ tena tad dhruvam ||

5,13.38

tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syur viṣayād ṛte |
na tv anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||

5,13.39

aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ |
naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedair ānantyato bhavet ||

5,13.40

anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate |
jātivyaktyos tu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||

5,13.41

siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāv indriyaiḥ punaḥ |
arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktir ekā niyāmikā ||

5,13.42

na cātmahetum evāsau siddhaṃ bādhitum arhati |<393>
śaktiś ca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||

5,13.43

sāmānyāntarayogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate |
tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||

5,13.44

sambandhas tasya hetur vā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam |
svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścād etad vikalpyate ||

5,13.45

sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvam ity upalakṣaṇam |
na ca svasamavāyy eva kevalaṃ cihnam iṣyate ||

5,13.46

sāsnādibhyas tu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā |
sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyas tadā syād etad uttaram ||<394>

5,13.47

kasmāt sāsnādimatsv eva gotvaṃ yasmāt tadātmakam |
tādātmyam asya kasmāc cet svabhāvād iti gamyatām ||

5,13.48

upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhir īdṛśī |
svato gotvādibhedas tu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||

5,13.49

sā bhūd drutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ |
bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataś cet, iha tatsamam ||<395>

5,13.50

vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
tasmāt svābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||

5,13.51

anekānanyavṛttittvān na sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |
ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||

5,13.52

bhinnebhyaś cāpy abhinnatvād bhedas tat svātmavad bhavet |
ekasmād vāpy abhinnatvād vyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||

5,13.53

ekānekatvam ekasya tathānyānanyatā katham |
tat sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś cety evamādi ca duṣkaram ||

5,13.54

virodhas tāvad ekāntād vaktum atra na yujyate |
sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||

5,13.55

sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ |<396>
evañ ca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||

5,13.56

kena cid dhy ātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit |
sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||

5,13.57

darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ |
yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||

5,13.58

citratvād vastuno 'py evaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam |
sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||

5,13.59

tasya hetor asiddhatvaṃ siddhaś cet siddhasādhanam |<397>
bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā ||

5,13.60

tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate |
tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||

5,13.61

sad apy agrāhyarūpatvād asadvat pratibhāti naḥ |
viśeṣān api sāmānyād yadā bhedena buddhyate ||

5,13.62

tadā sāmānyamātratvam evam eva pratīyate |
yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapat pratipadyate ||

5,13.63

tadānyān anyabhedādi sarvam eva pralīyate |
na ca tat tādṛśaṃ kaś cic chabdaḥ śaknoti bhāṣitum ||

5,13.64

sāmānyāṃśān apoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate |
samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ||

5,13.65

ke cid āhur asadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate |
sārūpyam eva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||

5,13.66

tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate |<398>
samānarūpabhāvaś cej jātiḥ sāsmābhir iṣyate ||

5,13.67

sādṛśyam atha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām |
na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||

5,13.68

viśeṣarūpataḥ, ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ |
śābaleya iveti syāt tatra buddhir na gaur iva ||

5,13.69

śābaleyo 'yam iti vā bhrāntyā gaur iti nāsti dhīḥ |
śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaur ity avatiṣṭhate ||

5,13.70

tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhir na syāt susadṛśeṣv api |
dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||

5,13.71

na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīr bhāvet |
na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣv asti sarvadā ||<399>

5,13.72

sarvapuṃsām ato bhrāntir naiṣā bādhakavarjanāt |
sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||

5,13.73

viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvād eva gauḥ kaś ca kathyatām |
babhūva yady asau pūrvam asmadādes tadagrahāt ||

5,13.74

sādṛśyāvadhṛtir nāstīty ato godhīr na labhyate |
na cāvayavasāmānyair vinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||

5,13.75

sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate |
vyaktitaś cātireko 'sya syān na veti vicārite ||

5,13.76

sāmānyam eva sādṛśyaṃ bhaved vā vyaktimātrakam |
tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam |
granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate ||

{5,14 apohavāda APV}

<400>

5,14.1

agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam |
gotvaṃ vastv eva tair uktam ago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||

5,14.2

bhāvāntaram abhāvo hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ |
tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||

5,14.3

neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇas tāvad viṣayo nirvikalpanāt |
tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||

5,14.4

śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam |
na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||<401>

5,14.5

na ca sākṣād viśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat |
na śābaleyavijñānam agovyāvṛttibandhanam ||

5,14.6

nivṛttyā bāhuleyādes tadvijñānaṃ pravartate |
kuryād agonivṛttiṃ cen nāpohetātmavad dhi tān ||

5,14.7

tenāṃśenānapohaś ca svarūpeṇāpy apohanam |
kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samamākṣepavāraṇe ||

5,14.8

tasmāt prātyātmikai rūpair ago 'poho na yujyate |
samudāye 'pi naiteṣām agovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||

5,14.9

sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhir vyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate |
na pratyekaṃ bhaved eṣā, na samasteṣv aśaktitaḥ ||<402>

5,14.10

tasmāt sarveṣu yad rūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam |
gobuddhis tannimittā syād gotvād anyac ca nāsti tat ||

5,14.11

nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate |
sattaiva hy atra sāmānyam anutpattyādirūṣitā ||

5,14.12

tām utpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate |
anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||

5,14.13

anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyam ucyate |
abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syād bhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||

5,14.14

puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, <403>
viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ |
sāmānyapratyayaś caiṣu pratyekam upajāyate ||

5,14.15

tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syād avastu tat |
gotvādāv api tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||

5,14.16

kaiś cit tv atraikaśabdatvam akṣādāv iva kalpitam |
jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||

5,14.17

nātra hy anantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate |
tasmāt kriyāguṇāḥ ke cid dhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||

5,14.18

puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitad brāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam |
cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sad gamyate 'rthādibhir yathā ||

5,14.19

yady apy avāntarā nāsti triṣu jātir vyavasthitā |
nañsāmārthyān naratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||<404>

5,14.20

śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā |
puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||

5,14.21

dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktir gṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ |
yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve pumabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ ||

5,14.22

brāhmaṇavyatiriktārthavṛtti puṃstvam itīdṛśam |
vākyaṃ yatra pravarteta tatrābrāhmaṇadhīpade ||

5,14.23

pārthivatvādisāmānyam evam evāghaṭādiṣu |
ghaṭatvādivinirmuktaṃ viṣayaḥ sampratīyate ||

5,14.24

asādhāraṇabhāvāc ca nañā śabdo viśeṣitaḥ |
tāvanmātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate ||<405>

5,14.25

viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyaṃ yadanantaram |
sāmānyākāṅkṣiṇaṃ śabdaṃ niruṇad dhi tadātmani ||

5,14.26

prathamātikrame tasya kāraṇaṃ naiva vidyate |
brāhmaṇatvād ato 'petaṃ naratvam avaśiṣyate ||

5,14.27

vyudasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe |
naratvodasanaṃ yat tu kalpetāśrutam eva tat ||

5,14.28

tasmād yasyaiva te bhedā niṣiddhyeraṃs tadarthataḥ |
bhedāntarasthaṃ sāmānyam, loke 'py evaṃ pratīyate ||

5,14.29

prasaṅginyāṃ ca tadbuddhau niṣedho 'rthād apīṣyate |
tanmātrarahite cārthe sādṛśyāt tanmatir bhavet ||<406>

5,14.30

sādṛśyam eva vā vācyam iṣṭam abrāhmaṇādiṣu |
tac cāvayavasāmānyād, vināpy etena lakṣyate ||

5,14.31

kva cid vināpi sādṛśyāt sāhacaryādihetukā |
nañyuktaśabdavṛttiḥ syād yathā vakṣyaty anīkṣaṇe ||

5,14.32

īkṣaṇavyatiriktā hi kriyā tatrāpy apekṣitā |
pratyāsatter na saṅkalpam atikramya pratīyate ||

5,14.33

nāmadhātvarthayogī ca naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ |
vadato 'brāhmaṇādharmāv anyamātravirodhinau ||<407>

5,14.34

yatrāpy ākhyātasambandhāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate |
tatraudāsīnyavastv eva pratipattā 'valambate ||

5,14.35

tasmād vastuny apohāḥ syuḥ, api cāvastukalpane |
prāgntyebhyo viśeṣebhyo na kiñ cid vastu labhyate ||

5,14.36

na cāntyair vyavahāro 'sti, śakyaṃ naiṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |
apohaśabdavācyātha śūnyatānyaprakārikā ||

5,14.37

tasyāṃ cāśvādibuddhīnātmāṃśagrahaṇaṃ bhavet |
tatrānyāpohavācyatvaṃ mudhaivābhyupagamyate ||

5,14.38

sāmānyaṃ vasturūpaṃ hi buddhyākāro bhaviṣyati |
śabdārtho 'rthānapekṣo hi vṛthāpohaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||

5,14.39

vasturūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabdārtheṣūpajāyate |
tena vastv eva kalpeta vācyaṃ buddhyanapohakam ||<408>

5,14.40

asaty api ca bāhye 'rthe vākyārthapratibhā tathā |
padārthe 'pi tathaiva syāt kim apohaḥ prakalpyate ||

5,14.41

buddhyantarād vyavacchedo na ca buddheḥ pratīyate |
svarūpotpādamātrāc ca nānyam aṃśaṃ bibharti sā ||

5,14.42

bhinnasāmānyavacanā viśeṣavacanāś ca ye |
sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyā yady apohasya vācyatā ||

5,14.43

nanu bhedād apohānāṃ prasaṅgo 'yaṃ na yujyate |
sāmānyāpohakḷptyā ced vastumātre samaṃ tava ||

5,14.44

bhidyante mama vastutvāt sāmānyāni parasparam |
asaṅkīrṇasvabhāvāni na caikatvaṃ vitanvate ||

5,14.45

saṃsṛṣṭaikatvanānātvavikalparahitātmanām |
avastutvād apohānāṃ tva syād bhinnatā katham ||

5,14.46

yadi vā bhidyamānatvād vastvasādhāraṇāṃśavat |<409>
avastutve tv anānātvāt paryāyatvān na mucyate ||

5,14.47

nanu cāpohyabhedena bhedo 'pohasya setsyati |
na viśeṣaḥ svatas tasya parataś caupacārikaḥ ||

5,14.48

tenaivādhārabhedenāpy asya bhedo na yujyate |
na hi sambandhibhedena bhedo vastuny apīṣyate ||

5,14.49

kim utāvastvasaṃsṛṣṭam anyataś cānivartitam |
anavāptaviśeṣāṃśaṃ yat kim apy anirūpitam ||

5,14.50

tasmād yathaiva bhede 'pi piṇḍānāṃ naiva bhidyate |
tathaivāpohyabhede 'pi nāneko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ||

5,14.51

bhede vā pratipiṇḍaṃ syād ago 'pohaḥ, tathā sati |
sāmānyaṃ śābaleyāder iti neṣṭaṃ prasidhyati ||

5,14.52

saṃsargiṇo 'pi cādhārā yaṃ na bhindanti rūpataḥ |
apohyaiḥ sa bahirbhūtair bhidyetety atikalpanā ||

5,14.53

agavyaśvātirekaḥ syād anaśvaś ca gavādhikaḥ |
śeṣaṃ hastyādyapohyaṃ tu dvayor api na bhidyate ||

5,14.54

tatraikabhedād bhedo 'stu bahvabhedād abhinnatā |
bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam ity abhedaḥ prasajyate ||<410>

5,14.55

gauś ca hastyādyapohena nāśvarūpād viśeṣyate |
karoti tadapohaṃ ced aikarūpyaṃ virudhyate ||

5,14.56

sarvaśabdeṣu caikaikam apohyamatiricyate |
tatrāsādhāraṇatvena tanmātrāpohyatā bhavet ||

5,14.57

tato 'śvāpoharūpatvāt siṃhādiḥ sarva eva te |
tannimittam ago 'pohaṃ bibhrad ucyeta gaur iti ||

5,14.58

sarvāpoho yadīṣyeta, <411>
sa vaktavyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ |
yadi pratyekarūpeṇa nāpohyānantatā bhavet ||

5,14.59

bhinnatvāc cāpy apohyānāṃ bhinno 'pohaḥ prasajyate |
tatraikasmin bhavet piṇḍe 'nantajātisamanvayaḥ ||

5,14.60

tato gaur iti sāmānyaṃ vācyam ekaṃ na sidhyati |
jātyantaramatiś caiṣu bhavej jātyantareṣv iva ||

5,14.61

samudāyātmanā nāpi bhaved eṣām apohyatā |
samudāyo hi naikena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate ||

5,14.62

nāpy ekadeśatā teṣām asti nāpy ekakālatā |
vyatiriktaś ca saṅghātas teṣāṃ kaś cin na vidyate ||

5,14.63

yadi tv avyatiriktaḥ syād ānanyaṃ tadavasthitam |
yadi sāmānyarūpeṇa te 'pohyante, na vastutā ||

5,14.64

kathaṃ vā vastv apohyeta, <412>
nābhāvo bhāvamṛcchati |
apohyamāne cābhāve bhāva evāvaśiṣyate ||

5,14.65

apohyabhedakḷptiś ca nābhāvābhedato bhavet |
tadbhedo 'pohabhedāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||

5,14.66

gosāmānyasya bhinnatvād agaur ity eṣa bhidyate |
agaur ity asya bhedena gosāmānyaṃ ca bhidyate ||

5,14.67

agāvo 'śvādayaś ca syus te 'py abhāvātmakāḥ punaḥ |
karkādyapekṣayā te 'pi tathety evaṃ na gamyate ||

5,14.68

kim apohyam, kva cāpohaḥ, gopiṇḍeṣv evam eva ca |<413>
tatra syād dvayam apy etadantyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||

5,14.69

na cāntyeṣu dvayor asti vyavahāro bhidāṃ prati |
gavāśvaparamāṇūnāṃ viśeṣaś ca na vidyate ||

5,14.70

svarūpajātisaṃsthānaparimāṇādilakṣaṇaḥ |
kim apohyaṃ kva cāpohas tatrāpi na viśiṣyate ||

5,14.71

na cāprasiddhasārūpyānapohaviṣayātmanā |
śaktaḥ kaś cid api jñātuṃ gavādīnaviśeṣataḥ ||

5,14.72

apohyān api cāśvādīnekadharmānvayād ṛte |
na nirūpayituṃ śaktis tatrāpoho na siddhyati ||

5,14.73

na cānvayavinirmukte pravṛttir liṅgaśabdayoḥ |
tābhyāṃ ca na vināpoho na cāsādhāraṇe 'nvayaḥ ||

5,14.74

apohaś cāpy aniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryaṃ kva dṛśyatām |
tasminn adṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syāt pramāṇatā ||<414>

5,14.75

na cādarśanamātreṇa tābhyāṃ pratyāyanaṃ bhavet |
sarvatraiva hy adṛṣṭatvāt pratyāyyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||

5,14.76

athāsaty api sārūpye syād apohasya kalpanā |
gavāśvayor ayaṃ kasmād ago 'poho na kalpyate ||

5,14.77

śābaleyāc ca bhinnatvaṃ bāhuleyāśvayoḥ samam |
sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet kvāgo 'pohaḥ pravartatām ||<415>

5,14.78

indriyair nāpy ago 'pohaḥ prathamaṃ vyavasīyate |
nānyatra śabdavṛttiś ca kiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām ||

5,14.79

pūrvoktena prabandhena nānumāpy atra vidyate |
sambandhānubhāvo 'py asya tena naivopapadyate ||

5,14.80

nivṛttivācinaḥ śabdā na prasiddhāś ca yān prati |
teṣām agor asiddhatvān na sāmānyanirākriyā ||

5,14.81

agośabdābhidheyatvaṃ gamyatāṃ ca kathaṃ punaḥ |
na dṛṣṭo yatra gośabdaḥ sambandhānubhavakṣaṇe ||

5,14.82

ekasmāt tarhi gopiṇḍād yadanyat sarvam eva tat |
bhaved apohyam ity evaṃ na sāmānyasya vācyatā ||

5,14.83

siddhaś cāgaur apohyeta goniṣedhātmakaś ca saḥ |
tatra gaur eva vaktavyo nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate ||

5,14.84

sa ced agonivṛttyātmā bhaved anyonyasaṃśrayaḥ |<416>
siddhaś ced gaur apohyārthaṃ vṛthāpohaprakalpanā ||

5,14.85

gavyasiddhe tv agaur nāsti tadabhāve ca gauḥ kutaḥ |
nādhārādheyavṛttyādisambandhaś cāpy abhāvayoḥ ||

5,14.86

na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'pohavat tayā |
kathaṃ vā parikalpyeta sambandho vastvavastunoḥ ||

5,14.87

svarūpasattvamātreṇa na ca kiñ cid viśeṣaṇam |
svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tad viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.88

na cāpy aśvādiśabdebho jāyate 'pohabodhanam |
viśiṣṭabuddhir iṣṭeha na cājñātaviśeṣaṇā ||<417>

5,14.89

na cānyarūpam anyādṛk kuryāj jñānaṃ viśeṣaṇam |
kathaṃ cānyādṛśe jñāte tad ucyeta viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.90

athānyathā viśeṣye 'pi syād viśeṣaṇakalpanā |
tathā sati hi yatkiñcit prasajyeta viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.91

abhāvarūpagamye ca na viśeṣye 'sti vastutā |
viśeṣitam apohena vastu vācyaṃ na te 'sty ataḥ ||

5,14.92

yady apy apohanirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabdaliṅgayoḥ |
yuktā tathāpi buddhis tu jñātur vastvavalambate ||

5,14.93

na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu buddhau viparivarttate |
na cāpi nirvikalpatvāt tasya yuktā viśeṣyatā ||<418>

5,14.94

śabdenāgamyamānaṃ ca viśeṣyam iti sāhasam |
tena sāmānyam eṣṭavyaṃ viṣayo buddhiśabdayoḥ ||

5,14.95

yadā cāśabdavācyatvān na vyaktīnām apohyatā |
tadāpohyeta sāmānyaṃ tasyāpohāc ca vastutā ||

5,14.96

nāpohyatvam abhāvānām abhāvābhāvavarjanāt |
vyakto 'pohāntare 'pohas tasmāt sāmānyavastunaḥ ||

5,14.97

abhāvasya ca yo 'bhāvaḥ sa cet tasmād vilakṣaṇaḥ |
bhāva eva bhaven no ced gaur agaus te prasajyate ||

5,14.98

yady apy aneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syād apohyatā |
sacchabdasya tv abhāvākhyān nāpohyaṃ bhinnam iṣyate ||

5,14.99

tatrāsato 'pi bhāvatvam itikleśo mahān bhavet |<419>
tadasiddhau na sattāsti na cāsattā prasidhyati ||

5,14.100

na cāpi vāsanābhedād bhedaḥ sadrūpatāpi vā |
apohānāṃ prakalpyeta, na hy avastuni vāsanā ||

5,14.101

smṛtiṃ muktvā na cāsty asyāḥ śaktiyogaḥ kriyāntare |
tasmān nānyādṛśe sārthe karoty anyādṛśīṃ matim ||

5,14.102

bhavadbhiḥ śabdabhedo 'pi tannimitto na labhyate |
na hy asādhāraṇaḥ śabdo vācakaḥ prāgadṛṣṭitaḥ ||

5,14.103

bhinnatvāc cāpi naivaikā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate |
na cāsti śabdavastv ekaṃ vāsanāṃ yat kariṣyati ||<420>

5,14.104

tatra śabdāntarāpohe sāmānye parikalpite |
tathaivāvasturūpatvāc chabdabhedo na kalpyate ||

5,14.105

vācakānāṃ yathā caivaṃ vācyavācakayor mithaḥ |
na cāpy apohyabhedena bhedo 'stīty upapāditam ||

5,14.106

nāgṛhītaś ca gamakaḥ śabdāpohaḥ kathañ cana |
pratyakṣaṃ na ca tacchaktaṃ na ca sto liṅgavācakau ||

5,14.107

yataḥ syād grahaṇaṃ tasya, liṅgādīnāṃ ca kalpane |
na vyavastheti vācyaivaṃ vinā pratyakṣamūlataḥ ||

5,14.108

na gamyagamakatvaṃ syād avastutvād apohayoḥ |
bhavatpakṣe, yathā loke khapuṣpaśaśaśṛṅgayoḥ ||

5,14.109

vṛṣṭimeghāsator dṛṣṭvā yady anaikāntikaḥ vadet |
vastv evātrāpi matpakṣe bhavatpakṣe 'py adaḥ kutaḥ ||

5,14.110

vidhirūpaś ca śabdārtho yena nābhyupagamyate |
na bhaved vyatireko 'pi tasya tatpūrvako hy asau ||<421>

5,14.111

niṣedhadvayayogitvād asato yāpy abhāvatā |
savastuke bhavet sāpi na tucche buddhyasambhavāt ||

5,14.112

nanu yuktyānayaivāyaṃ vastunāpi na bhidyate |
apohas tena doṣo 'tra pūrvokto na bhaviṣyati ||

5,14.113

siddham evaṃ madiṣṭaṃ syāt, naivānyā gatir asti hi |
abhāve vastubuddhir vā yad vā vastunyabhāvadhīḥ ||

5,14.114

tatrābhāvātmakatve syān nirnimittaiva vastudhīḥ |
vastuny abhāvabodhas tu sidhyaty anyam apekṣya tu ||<422>

5,14.115

apohamātravācyatvaṃ yadi cābhyupagamyate |
nīlotpalādiśabdeṣu śabalārthābhidhāyiṣu ||

5,14.116

viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyayoḥ |
na siddhiḥ, na hy anīlatvavyudāse 'nutpalacyutiḥ ||

5,14.117

nāpi tatretaras tasmān na viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe |
śabdayor nāpi te syātām abhidheyānapekṣayoḥ ||

5,14.118

sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na bhinnatvād apohayoḥ |
arthataś caitad iṣyeta kīdṛśyādheyatā tayoḥ ||

5,14.119

na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'nyac ca nāsti te |<423>
agamyamānam aikārthyaṃ śabdayoḥ kvopayujyate ||

5,14.120

athānyāpohavad vastu vācyam ity abhidhīyate |
tatrāpi paratantratvād vyāptiḥ śabdena durbalā ||

5,14.121

khaṇḍe bhinnavyapohyatvād yathaiva madhurādibhiḥ |
śuklādivyāptyabhāvena nākṣepo na viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.122

tathaivāsadvyudāsāṃśāvacchinnārthāvadhāraṇe |
nāghaṭādinivṛttyaṃśavyāptiḥ śabdāt pratīyate ||<424>

5,14.123

vyāptiś ced artharūpeṇa sattayaivaṃ hi sā bhavet |
na ghaṭatvādimān arthaḥ kaś cin na vyāpyate tayā ||

5,14.124

na ca vastutayā vyāptis tayā śabdasya vāryate |
pratītiṃ prati tulyas tu vyāpāro vastvavastunoḥ ||

5,14.125

nirbhāgo 'pi hi vastvātmā śabdair bhāgena gamyate |
na hi sacchabdavijñānād ghaṭādyarthaḥ pratīyate ||

5,14.126

tenānākṣepadoṣo 'sti, bhāktadoṣaś ca vidyate |
viśeṣaṇatvān mukhyatvam apohasya hi jātivat ||<425>

5,14.127

tasmāt tadvati gauṇatvān nābhidheyatvasambhavaḥ |
avastutvān na mukhyaś cet, na syād evaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.128

bhedāś cāpohavantaḥ syus teṣāṃ cāvācyatoditā |
ānantyavyabhicārābhyām, anyo nāsti tv apohavān ||

5,14.129

nāpohavattvam anyad dhi bhedāpohāntare 'sti te |
tac cāpi kalpyamānaṃ syād abhāvo bhāva eva vā ||

5,14.130

vastu cej jātir eva syād avastutve 'pi pūrvavat |
sambandho vaiṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācyatā ||<426>

5,14.131

na caiko 'pohavān artho vartate 'rthāntare kva cit |
tasmād api na sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ na ca viśeṣaṇam ||

5,14.132

nātmanyavidyamānatvād viśeṣo 'pohasūcakaḥ |
tasmān na tair viśeṣyatvaṃ prakṛṣṭatvena nīlavat ||

5,14.133

arthākṣepo 'pi nāsty eva sandehāl liṅgaliṅgivat |
na sāmānyātmanāpohas tair vinā na ca siddhyati ||<427>

5,14.134

evam eva tv anākṣepaḥ syād apohena vastunaḥ |
yataḥ śaśaviṣāṇe 'pi tadapohasya sambhavaḥ ||

5,14.135

liṅgasaṃkhyādisambandho na vāpohasya vidyate |
vyakter avyapadeśyatvāt taddvāreṇāpi nāsty asau ||

5,14.136

na hy asādhāraṇatvena sāpohenāpi gamyate |
na cāpy agamyamānasya vastunaḥ syād viśeṣyatā ||

5,14.137

liṅgasaṃkhyādyapohānāṃ nopakāraḥ svarūpataḥ |
vastunaś copakāryatvaṃ kathaṃ śabdaiḥ pratīyate ||<428>

5,14.138

na vinānupalabdhyā ca syād abhāvamatiḥ kva cit |
na cābhāvaprameyatvaṃ gotvāder iha gamyate ||

5,14.139

ākhyāteṣu ca nānyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate |
na paryudāsarūpaṃ hi niṣedhyaṃ tatra vidyate ||

5,14.140

na neti hy ucyamāne 'pi niṣedhasya niṣedhanam |
pacatīty aniṣiddhaṃ tu svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate ||

5,14.141

sādhyatvapratyayaś cātra tathābhūtādirūpaṇam |
niṣpannatvād apohasya nirnimittaṃ prasajyate ||

5,14.142

vidhyādāv artharāśau ca nānyāpohanidarśanam |
nañaś cāpi nañā yuktād apohaḥ kīdṛśo bhavet ||

5,14.143

cādīnām api nañyogo naivāstīty anapohanam |
vākyārtho 'nyanivṛttiś ca vyapadeṣṭuṃ na śakyate ||

5,14.144

ananyāpohaśabdādau vācyaṃ na ca nirūpyate |
prameyajñeyaśabdāder apohyaṃ kuta eva tu ||

5,14.145

apohyakalpanāyāṃ tu varaṃ vastv eva kalpitam |<429>
jñānākāraniṣedhāc ca nāntarārthābhidheyatā ||

5,14.146

na cāpy apohyatā, tasmān nāpohas teṣu sidhyati |
evam ityādiśabdānāṃ na vāpohyaṃ nirūpyate ||

5,14.147

virodhitvena bhedānām apoho yadi kalpyate |
virodho 'pohatas tatra virodhāc cāpy apohanam ||

5,14.148

na sāmānyāpahāritvaṃ vidhirūpeṇa tatra te |
palaśādīn apohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||<430>

5,14.149

sāmānyādyanapohaś ca nāvirodhena kalpyate |
na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syād viruddhāviruddhatā ||

5,14.150

na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdair asaṅgateḥ |
prāk śabdavyāpṛter nāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||

5,14.151

anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate |
sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||

5,14.152

śabdānurūpataś cet syād anyāpohanirūpaṇam |
bhinnatvād vṛkṣatarvāder apohaḥ kena vāryate ||

5,14.153

śabdaspṛṣṭer vināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate |
na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgāc ca sidhyati ||<431>

5,14.154

adṛṣṭatvād vyudāsas tu purastād eva vāritaḥ |
sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||

5,14.155

vyudāsas tatra durvāraḥ, kathañ cid dṛṣṭatā punaḥ |
brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ||

5,14.156

ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgas tulyo dravyakriyādiṣu |
vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhatyāder asaṃśayam ||

5,14.157

puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā |
avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syān nīlotpalatulyatā ||<432>

5,14.158

vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate |
prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||

5,14.159

tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate |
deśāvibhāgato vṛttir netrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||

5,14.160

grāhakatvena vṛttis tu pratijāti vyavasthitā |
cakṣurādivad evātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||

5,14.161

nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ |
sattvāder bodhakatvaṃ syād ekanyūnātirekataḥ ||

5,14.162

tavaiva doṣaḥ syād eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate |
sāmānyaśabdaḥ, <433>
vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpy asti vastutaḥ ||

5,14.163

api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ |
nirupākhyeṣv apoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||

5,14.164

tasmād yeṣv eva śabdeṣu nañyogas teṣu kevalam |
bhaved anyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||

5,14.165

jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāt tvagādivat |
yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syād vyabhicāritā ||

5,14.166

pakṣīkuryād yadā sarvāṃs tadāthāvītahetubhiḥ |
anaikānto virodhaś ca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||

5,14.167

nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena ced bhavet |
kevalāpohabuddher vā tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatā ||

5,14.168

athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttir nāstīti sādhyate |
tataḥ prāk pakṣabādhaḥ syād gotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||<434>

5,14.169

sādhyahīnaś ca dṛṣṭāntaś cakṣurādy api tasya hi |
varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yady api na budhyate ||

5,14.170

athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam |
apoharūpam apy etad vastv ity eva hi gamyate ||

5,14.171

athāpohanimittāsya vṛttir arthe niṣidhyate |
vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvāt punaḥ prāk pakṣabādhanam ||

5,14.172

anumāne tathā caitad ity anaikāntiko bhavet |
sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||

5,14.173

viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivad yataḥ |
ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||

5,14.174

vidhirūpapravṛttir vā śabdo 'pohena varttate |
anumānāṅgabhūtatvād yathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||<435>

5,14.175

jātiṃ vā na bravīty eṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām |
pramāyām aṅgabhūtatvāt tvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||

5,14.176

evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā |
nāvātiṣṭhata ity atra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

{5,15 vanavāda VAV}

5,15.1

sāsnādibhir viśiṣṭatvam ākṛter ucyate katham |
yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||

5,15.2

ekāvayavisambandhas teṣāṃ gotvena vidyate |
tenāsādhāraṇatvāt te syur gotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||

5,15.3

piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā |
tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhir asaṃśayam ||

5,15.4

na caite vyañjakās tasya guṇavad vā viśeṣaṇam |<436>
tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syād gotvabodhanam ||

5,15.5

teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punargrahaṇakalpanā |
tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syād gotvāvadhāraṇam ||

5,15.6

sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ |
gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhisambhavaḥ ||

5,15.7

tasmāt sadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ |
kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||

5,15.8

yady evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate |
taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||

5,15.9

gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ |
sāsnādeḥ kasya cid bodhas taddeśatvena jāyate ||

5,15.10

tadanatyantabhedād vā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate |<437>
bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||

5,15.11

pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hy atra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak |
taddhīhānāv avijñānāt paṅktiyūthavanādivat ||

5,15.12

sarvatra lokasiddhatvān na vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam |
niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||

5,15.13

visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ |
pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kuto nv iyam ||

5,15.14

rūpādāv api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate |
vivādaḥ, naiva lokas tu jātau vipratipadyate ||

5,15.15

vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ |
dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||<438>

5,15.16

ākṛtir jātir evātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate |
na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate ||

5,15.17

anyadanyac ca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate |
saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||

5,15.18

atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāv api tatsamam |
na gotvena vinā hy etad vyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||

5,15.19

sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne saty apīdṛśe |
na gotvādimatir dṛṣṭā, tasmāj jātiḥ pṛthak tataḥ ||

5,15.20

rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvād yudāhṛtam |
bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||<439>

5,15.21

vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā |
tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiś cāpy uttarārthinaḥ ||

5,15.22

hemārthinas tu mādhyasthaṃ tasmād vastu trayātmakam |
notpādasthitibhaṅgānām abhāve syān matitrayam ||

5,15.23

na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham |
sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||

5,15.24

mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate |
tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātir indriyagocaraḥ ||

5,15.25

ārād dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu |
na syād yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā ||

5,15.26

tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva cit kena cid iṣyate |
rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādy apekṣayā ||<440>

5,15.27

suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāt tāmratvāder asaṃśayam |
tailād ghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||

5,15.28

bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate |
aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||

5,15.29

saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ |
kva cid ācārataś cāpi samyag rājānupālitāt ||

5,15.30

pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate |
tathā saty api nānātvaṃ naikabuddher bhaviṣyati ||

5,15.31

na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam |
vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||

5,15.32

yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ |
kālabhede 'py abhinnaiva jātir bhinnāśrayā satī ||

5,15.33

kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate |<441>
na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||

5,15.34

tasmād vyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttir astīti gamyate |
viśeṣāvasarābhāvāt tanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||

5,15.35

yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate |
bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeś ca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||

5,15.36

tatrāvayavayogitvam avibhutvaṃca kāraṇam |
ākṛtes tadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||

5,15.37

na ca dvaividhyam eveti vṛtter asti niyāmakam |
trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvāt sambhaved dvividhā yathā ||

5,15.38

itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cet sragādiṣv api tatsamam |
naiva hy anyonyatulyatvaṃ tayor nāpy anayā saha ||

5,15.39

na hy anyasminn adṛṣṭatvād vahner auṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati |<442>
na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñched yena nidarśanam ||

5,15.40

svarūpataś ca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtter na pararūpataḥ |
nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣam apaśyatām ||

5,15.41

aṅgāṅgāsambhavāc cāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā |
sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||

5,15.42

tasmād asambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam |
yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavan bādham arhati ||

5,15.43

tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī |
vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavat tatra gṛhyate ||

5,15.44

tasmāt piṇḍeṣu gobuddhir ekagotvanibandhanā |
gavābhāsaikarūpyābhām ekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||<443>

5,15.45

na śābaleyād gobuddhis tato 'nyālambanāpi vā |
tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvād ghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||

5,15.46

pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ |
pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvāt pratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||

5,15.47

pratyekasamavetāpi jātir ekaikabuddhitaḥ |
nañyukteṣv api vākyeṣu brahmaṇādinivartanam ||

5,15.48

na ca sādṛśyaviṣayā godhīs tādrūpyajanmataḥ |
prāmāṇye sati yadvad dhi pratyabhijñaikavastuni ||

5,15.49

naikarūpamatir gotve mithyā vaktuṃ ca śakyate |
nātra kāraṇadoṣo 'sti bādhakapratyayo 'pi vā ||

5,15.50

yadā vyaktyatirekeṇa grāhyatvād anyatākṛteḥ |
vanavannāsty anaikāntāt tatrāsambaddhatā katham ||

5,15.51

sādhanaṃ cen mayocyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā |
dūṣaṇatvadhiyā tv etad asambaddhatvam ucyate ||<444>

5,15.52

nāstitvahetor uktaiṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā |
parasya sādhanaṃ hy atra yat tat pūrvam udāhṛtam ||

5,15.53

pratyakṣābhāsatā cātra naivāsti vanabuddhivat |
kasya cin na hi mithyātvāt sarvaṃ mithyety asaṅgatiḥ ||

5,15.54

yathā vanādibuddhīnāṃ mithyātvān na rasādidhīḥ |
mithyaivaṃ jātibuddhiḥ syād viśeṣo vābhidhīyatām ||

5,15.55

vṛkṣebhyo vyatirekeṇa vane yaikamatir bhavet |
dūratvadoṣāt tatra syād ākṛtau tu na vidyate ||

5,15.56

sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhyekatvaṃ nivartate |
kena cit tu prakāreṇa jātibuddhir na naśyati ||

5,15.57

yaikatvadhīr vinā śabdāt saivaṃ tāvan nirākṛtā |
vanaśabdānuraktā tu madhyasthasyāpi jāyate ||

5,15.58

mithyātvakalpanā tv asyāḥ pratyakṣāder asambhavāt |
jātiḥ sarvapramāṇais tu tadrūpaivāvagamyate ||<445>

5,15.59

pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭe ca padam arthe prayujyate |
tasmād dṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvaṃ syād vanādiṣu ||

5,15.60

ke cin nityaṃ vanaikatvaṃ śabdagamyaṃ samāśritāḥ |
anyaiḥ saṅgatyabhāve 'pi satyaṃ tat syād rasādivat ||

5,15.61

mithyātvaṃ yadasaṅgatyā tadajñāne prasajyate |
jñāyamānasya doṣas tu na tu kaś cid asaṅgateḥ ||

5,15.62

pramāṇāntaragamye 'rthe padaṃ nityaṃ prayujyate |
dharmo 'yaṃ na ca sarveṣāṃ padānām abhyupeyate ||

5,15.63

asty eva saṅgatiś cātra vṛkṣā hi bahavo vanam |
te pramāṇāntarāj jñātāḥ, saṃkhyā caiṣānyavastuni ||<446>

5,15.64

nānekasyaikaśabdyaṃ ced, ekaśeṣavad iṣyatām |
tatra saṃkhyāvivṛddhiś ced, astu tanmātravarjanam ||

5,15.65

tasmāt sāmānyadṛṣṭena siddhaikatvasya saṅgatiḥ |
tenānyānavagamyāpi saṃkhyā syāt sūryayānavat ||

5,15.66

ke cid bahutvasāmānyam āhur vṛkṣasthitaṃ vanam |
tatra caikatvam asty eva, vanatvaṃ vāpi vidyate ||<447>

5,15.67

vināpy ekāśrayatvena yathaivāvayavo tathā |
asaṃyuktair abhivyaktir dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate ||

5,15.68

anyatrāpi ca tadbuddheḥ sāmānyaṃ tad abhaviṣyati |
yathā ca bhramaṇatvādibhaṅgiṣv avayaveṣv api ||

5,15.69

vyaktaṃ nānāśrayatve 'pi gṛhyate vanatā tathā |
yadvaikakāryahetutvād ekagośabdavad vanam ||

5,15.70

nityaṃ ye vyastavijñātā vṛkṣā neṣṭā hi te vanam |
yad vā lakṣaṇayaikatvaṃ deśakālakriyādibhiḥ ||

5,15.71

dravyaikatvād vināpīṣṭaṃ paṅktiyūthavanādiṣu |<448>
vṛkṣāṇāṃ samudāye ca vanadhīr jāyate yathā ||

5,15.72

naivaṃ gosamudāye 'pi gotvadhīr upajāyate |
yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīs tatra gotvadhīr api tādṛśī ||

5,15.73

vanavan nāpṛthaksiddheḥ samudāyatvakalpanā |
na ca sāsnādisaṅghātas tadbuddhyālambanaṃ bhavet ||

5,15.74

kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍabuddhyaiṣu tatsāmānye hi gotvadhīḥ |
tenāvayavyabhāve 'pi sāmānyaṃ vyatiricyate ||

5,15.75

pūrvoktād eva tu nyāyāt sidhyed atrāvayavy api |
tasyāpy atyantabhinnatvaṃ na syād avayavaiḥ saha ||

5,15.76

vyaktibhyo jātivac caiṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate |<449>
kaiś cid avyatiriktatvaṃ kaiś cic ca vyatiriktatā ||

5,15.77

dūṣitā sādhitā vāpi na ca tatra balābalam |
kadā cin niścitaṃ kaiś cit tasmān madhyasthatā varam ||

5,15.78

tato 'nyānanyate nasya sto na staś ceti kīrttyate |
tasmāc citravadevāsya mṛṣā syād ekarūpatā ||

5,15.79

vastvanekatvavādāc ca na sandindhāpramāṇatā |
jñānaṃ sandihyate yatra tatra na syāt pramāṇatā ||

5,15.80

ihānaikāntikaṃ vastv ityevaṃ jñānaṃ suniścitam |
niṣkṛṣyāvayavān buddhyā yāvayavyapratītatā ||

5,15.81

buddhisthatvād vināśasya saulūkyasyāpi yujyate |<450>
vṛttiś cāvayaveṣv asya vyāsajyaiva pratīyate ||

5,15.82

tataḥ kārtsnyādisampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyo 'tra jātivat |
sāsnādiguṇahetuś cen nānyasmin gotvadhīr bhavet ||

5,15.83

bhinna eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍāt piṇḍāntareyataḥ |
na cāvayavasāmānyaṃ pareṣām upapadyate ||

5,15.84

tasmāt sāsnādito 'nyena gotvadhīr upajanyate |
vanāntareṣa yā buddhir vanam ity upajāyate ||

5,15.85

tasyās tad eva vṛkṣatvaṃ grāhyaṃ bahvāśrayaṃ viduḥ |
ekatve 'py ākṛter yadvad bahutvaṃ vyaktyapekṣayā ||

5,15.86

bahutve hi tathā vyakter ekatvaṃ jātyapekṣayā |<451>
ekānekābhidhāne ca śabdā niyataśaktayaḥ ||

5,15.87

ke cid vyaktiṃ tv asaṃkhyākāṃ gamayanty ambarādiṣu |
eko vrīhiḥ suniṣpannaḥ iti jātiṃ svasaṃkhyayā ||

5,15.88

patnīsannahanādau tu vyaktim ākṛtisaṃkhyayā |
kapiñjalādijātes tu pratītir vyaktisaṃkhyayā ||

5,15.89

vyaktijātī vadanty anye dravyāvayavasaṃkhyayā |
asmān iti yathaikasmin pāśānaditir ity api ||

5,15.90

tatra vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ saṃkhyāyogo yathāruci |
vanadārādiśabdās tu pravartante vyavasthayā ||

5,15.91

jaṅgame sthāvare cārthe yathā yūthavanādayaḥ |
tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dārādiś cet prayujyate ||

5,15.92

vyakter avayavānāṃ ca saṃkhyām ādāya vartate |<452>
vanaśabdaḥ punarvyaktīr jātisaṃkhyāviśeṣitāḥ ||

5,15.93

bahvīrāhātha vā jātiṃ bahuvyaktisamāśrayām |
evaṃ paṅktyādiśabdānāṃ saṃyogādi viśeṣaṇam ||

5,15.94

sarveṣāṃ kiñ cid astīti na nirālambanaikadhīḥ |
tulyaṃ pratyakṣayā ''kṛtyā vane yat tadasad yadi ||

5,15.95

vṛkṣās tatra tayā tulyā iti śūnyatvavāditā |
pratyakṣābhāsagamyatvād vṛkṣebhyo 'nyat tu tadvanam ||

5,15.96

nā''kṛtyā saha tasyāsti sparddhā pratyakṣagamyayā |
athā''kṛtyā vanaṃ tulyaṃ sadbhāvena prasajyate |
jātipakṣavimokena vanasiddhāntadūṣaṇam ||

5,15.97

iti nigaditam etallokasiddhaiḥ padārthair vyavahṛtir iha śāstre na svatantrābhyupetaiḥ |
bhavati ca janadṛṣṭyā jātipaṅktyādibhedo yadi tu na ghaṭate 'sau naiva bādho 'sti kaś cit ||

{5,16 sambandhākṣepaparihāra SAP}

<453>

5,16.1

bhavetāṃ nāma śabdārthau yāvetāvuditau tvayā |
yadarthas tu prayāso 'yaṃ sa sambandho nirūpyatām ||

5,16.2

pūrvam evopadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate |
svarūpākathanāc caitad uttaraṃ nopapadyate ||

5,16.3

kim auṣadhaṃ jvarasyeti pṛṣṭo yadi vaded idam |
yenāsau naśyatīty evaṃ kiṃ tena kathitaṃ bhavet ||

5,16.4

tatra ke cid vanty eva pūrvatrāparitoṣataḥ |
praśnaḥ punarupakrāntaḥ sambandhāntaram icchatā ||

5,16.5

yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ pratītyuttaro yataḥ |
sā cānyapūrvikā tasmān nāsya pratyāyanāṅgatā ||<454>

5,16.6

ajānāno 'pi saṃjñātvaṃ sambandhāntaradarśanāt |
buddhyate 'rthaṃ tataḥ paścāt kaś cit saṃjñeti manyate ||

5,16.7

tam evānyo 'vinābhāvam atra sambandham icchati |
na hi tasmād vinā śabde jñāte syād arthabodhanam ||

5,16.8

tattvayuktam, na bhāṣye 'sti tādṛksambandhakīrtanam |
yadi hy etāvatocyeta kiṃ nānuktaḥ pratīyate ||

5,16.9

prayuktaś cāvinābhāvasaṃjñā lokāt tu gamyate |
saṃjñetyagamyamāne 'pi gamakatvaṃ pratīyate ||<455>

5,16.10

tasmāt sa eva śabdārthacintāvyavahito 'dhunā |
nityānityavicārārthaṃ sambandhaḥ smāryate punaḥ ||

5,16.11

yacchabde jñāta ity evaṃ śaktir evātra kīrtyate |
kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā yat tasyārthābhidhāṃ prati ||

5,16.12

svato naivāsti śaktatvaṃ vācyāvācakayor mithaḥ |
pratītiḥ samayāt puṃsāṃ bhaved akṣinikocavat ||

5,16.13

samayaḥ pratimartyaṃ yā pratyuccāraṇam eva vā |
kriyate jagadādau vā sakṛdekena kena cit ||

5,16.14

pratyekaṃ vāpi sambandho bhidyetaiko 'tha vā bhavet |
ekatve kṛtako na syād, bhinnaś ced bhedadhīr bhavet ||

5,16.15

bhinnatve pratisambandhaṃ śaktiḥ kalpyābhidhā prati |
ekasmin jñātaśaktau vā nānyenārthamatir bhavet ||<456>

5,16.16

atha yo yasya puṃsaḥ syāt sa tena pratipadyate |
yasyānekena sambandhaḥ kṛtas tasya kathaṃ bhavet ||

5,16.17

ekārthānāṃ vikalpaś cet, netarātyantabādhanāt |
samuccayo 'pi naiteṣāṃ vyavahāre 'vagamyate ||

5,16.18

kiñ cid evaikamādāya vyavahāro hi dṛśyate |
bahubhiḥ kṛtasambandhe na caiko gamako bhavet ||

5,16.19

śabdārthayor abhede 'pi pumbahutve 'pi kartari |
nāyaṃ veti matir dṛṣṭā vikalpo 'to na yujyate ||

5,16.20

gośabde sakṛdukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu |
vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaś cid budhyeta netare ||<457>

5,16.21

samuccayo nṛbhedāc cet, na, vaktraikyād asambhavāt |
vaktṛśrotṛdhiyor bhedād vyavahāraś ca duṣyati ||

5,16.22

vaktur anyo hi sambandho buddhau śrotus tathāparaḥ |
śrotuḥ kartuṃ ca sambandhaṃ vaktā kaṃ pratipadyatām ||

5,16.23

pūrvadṛṣṭo hi yas tena śrotur naiva karoti tam |
yaṃ karoti navaṃ so 'pi na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||

5,16.24

sarvathā śrotṛsiddhiś ced, asiddhaṃ netaro vadet |
ghaṭādāv api tulyaṃ cet, na, sāmānyaprasiddhitaḥ ||<458>

5,16.25

yady api jñātasāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate |
kriyate yā na tasyāś ca śaktiḥ kārye 'vadhāritā ||

5,16.26

tathāpy ākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktir utpādanādiṣu |
tasyā na cādimattāsti, sambandhas tvādimāṃs tava ||

5,16.27

yadi tatrāpi sāmānyaṃ nityam abhyupagamyate |
tathāpy asmanmataṃ siddham, na tu dvyākārasambhavaḥ ||

5,16.28

śaktir eva hi sambandho bhedaś cāsyā na vidyate |
sā hi kāryānumeyatvāt tadbhedam anuvartate ||
